# TaskFlow — Azure Boards work items (export)

> **How to run.** Target: org https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi, project taskflow, process **Agile**, types **Epic** / **User Story**. Run every Epic create command **first**; Claude desktop (or a human) must capture each created Epic's returned id and substitute it for the <EPIC-n-id> placeholder in that Epic's child-story relation add commands. Then run each Story's create, capture its own returned id, and run its relation add to link it to its Epic. All Epics are listed before any User Story so every parent id exists before its children are linked. The Area Path and Iteration named taskflow must already exist in the project. Commands are single-line and shell-agnostic; HTML field values keep the Given/When/Then text verbatim.

## Epics
### Epic — EPIC-0: Walking Skeleton — register → board → card → persist
- **Type:** Epic · **Parent:** —
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-0; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Goal:</b> A new user can register, log in, create a single board, add one card to it, and find that card still there after reloading or signing back in — proving the whole stack (Vue SPA → REST API → EF Core → SQL Server, under Clean Architecture with JWT auth) end-to-end through the thinnest possible vertical slice.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Authentication &amp; accounts (§1.3, §1.4 self-as-Owner only); Boards — minimal create + read; Cards — minimal create + read. No lists UI, labels, comments, real-time, activity, search, drag-and-drop, or member management.</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.2, §1.3, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "Epic" --title "EPIC-0: Walking Skeleton — register → board → card → persist" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-0; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p><b>Goal:</b> A new user can register, log in, create a single board, add one card to it, and find that card still there after reloading or signing back in — proving the whole stack (Vue SPA → REST API → EF Core → SQL Server, under Clean Architecture with JWT auth) end-to-end through the thinnest possible vertical slice.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Authentication &amp; accounts (§1.3, §1.4 self-as-Owner only); Boards — minimal create + read; Cards — minimal create + read. No lists UI, labels, comments, real-time, activity, search, drag-and-drop, or member management.</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.2, §1.3, §1.6, §2.2</p>"
```

### Epic — EPIC-1: Board Membership & Per-Board Roles
- **Type:** Epic · **Parent:** —
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-1; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Goal:</b> An Owner can build a team on a board and precisely control what each member can do; per-board roles (Owner / Editor / Viewer) are enforced server-side on every mutation, turning EPIC-0's single-Owner board into a fully collaborative workspace.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Per-board roles &amp; membership management (§1.4); Authentication — current-user &amp; sign-out (§1.3); Server-enforced authorization across all mutations (§1.4, §1.6).</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "Epic" --title "EPIC-1: Board Membership & Per-Board Roles" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-1; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p><b>Goal:</b> An Owner can build a team on a board and precisely control what each member can do; per-board roles (Owner / Editor / Viewer) are enforced server-side on every mutation, turning EPIC-0's single-Owner board into a fully collaborative workspace.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Per-board roles &amp; membership management (§1.4); Authentication — current-user &amp; sign-out (§1.3); Server-enforced authorization across all mutations (§1.4, §1.6).</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>"
```
### Epic — EPIC-2: Lists CRUD &amp; Reorder
- **Type:** Epic · **Parent:** —
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-2; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Goal:</b> Editors and Owners can structure a board into multiple ordered lists (columns) — creating, renaming, deleting, and reordering them — making lists first-class managed entities beyond the single seeded default list from EPIC-0.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Lists (§1.5); Boards → Lists → Cards hierarchy (§1.1); Server-enforced per-board roles — Owner/Editor mutate, Viewer read-only (§1.4, §1.6).</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "Epic" --title "EPIC-2: Lists CRUD & Reorder" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-2; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p><b>Goal:</b> Editors and Owners can structure a board into multiple ordered lists (columns) — creating, renaming, deleting, and reordering them — making lists first-class managed entities beyond the single seeded default list from EPIC-0.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Lists (§1.5); Boards → Lists → Cards hierarchy (§1.1); Server-enforced per-board roles — Owner/Editor mutate, Viewer read-only (§1.4, §1.6).</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>"
```

### Epic — EPIC-3: Cards — Full Lifecycle, Move &amp; Reorder (Drag-and-Drop)
- **Type:** Epic · **Parent:** —
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-3; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Goal:</b> Editors and Owners can open, edit, move, reorder, and delete cards — including drag-and-drop reordering within a list and moving cards across lists on the same board — with a stable, concurrency-safe ordering model. Card metadata (labels, assignees, due dates, priorities) is EPIC-4; comments are EPIC-5; real-time broadcast of these mutations is EPIC-6.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Cards CRUD with ordering; drag-and-drop positioning (§1.3, §1.5); per-board role enforcement — Editor+ mutates, Viewer read-only (§1.4); performance NFR board ≤1.5s with ~200 cards (§1.6).</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.3, §1.4, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "Epic" --title "EPIC-3: Cards — Full Lifecycle, Move & Reorder (Drag-and-Drop)" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-3; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p><b>Goal:</b> Editors and Owners can open, edit, move, reorder, and delete cards — including drag-and-drop reordering within a list and moving cards across lists on the same board — with a stable, concurrency-safe ordering model. Card metadata (labels, assignees, due dates, priorities) is EPIC-4; comments are EPIC-5; real-time broadcast of these mutations is EPIC-6.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Cards CRUD with ordering; drag-and-drop positioning (§1.3, §1.5); per-board role enforcement — Editor+ mutates, Viewer read-only (§1.4); performance NFR board ≤1.5s with ~200 cards (§1.6).</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.3, §1.4, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>"
```
### Epic — EPIC-4: Card metadata — labels, assignees, due dates, priorities
- **Type:** Epic · **Parent:** —
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-4; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Goal:</b> Editors and Owners can enrich cards with board-scoped labels, member assignees, due dates, and priorities, so that work can be categorised, owned, and tracked across a board.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Labels &amp; filtering (§1.3, §1.5); assignees (§1.3, §1.4); due dates and priorities (§1.3). Assignee pool is the board's member list (§1.4). Card entity established by EPIC-3; member roster established by EPIC-1.</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Create**

```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "Epic" --title "EPIC-4: Card metadata — labels, assignees, due dates, priorities" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-4; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p><b>Goal:</b> Editors and Owners can enrich cards with board-scoped labels, member assignees, due dates, and priorities, so that work can be categorised, owned, and tracked across a board.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Labels &amp; filtering (§1.3, §1.5); assignees (§1.3, §1.4); due dates and priorities (§1.3). Assignee pool is the board's member list (§1.4). Card entity established by EPIC-3; member roster established by EPIC-1.</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>"
```

### Epic — EPIC-5: Comments on cards
- **Type:** Epic · **Parent:** —
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-5; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Goal:</b> Editors and Owners can discuss a card via threaded comments; Viewers can read them. Comments are paginated, editable by their author (showing an edited indicator), and deletable by their author or by the board Owner. All mutations are enforced server-side with the standard role and status-code conventions.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Comments (§1.3, §1.5); Per-board roles — Viewer read-only, Editor+ write (§1.4); Pagination (§1.6); RFC 7807, WCAG 2.2 AA, real-time propagation (§1.6, §2.2).</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.5, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "Epic" --title "EPIC-5: Comments on cards" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-5; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p><b>Goal:</b> Editors and Owners can discuss a card via threaded comments; Viewers can read them. Comments are paginated, editable by their author (showing an edited indicator), and deletable by their author or by the board Owner. All mutations are enforced server-side with the standard role and status-code conventions.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Comments (§1.3, §1.5); Per-board roles — Viewer read-only, Editor+ write (§1.4); Pagination (§1.6); RFC 7807, WCAG 2.2 AA, real-time propagation (§1.6, §2.2).</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.5, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>"
```

### Epic — EPIC-6: Real-time Collaboration (Azure SignalR)
- **Type:** Epic · **Parent:** —
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-6; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Goal:</b> When any member mutates a board (creates/edits/moves/deletes a list, card, metadata field, or comment; renames the board; changes membership), every other member currently viewing that board sees the change within ~1 s — delivered over Azure SignalR Service (Default mode) in a way that keeps the API stateless and horizontally scalable.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Real-time collaboration (§1.2, §1.5); Azure SignalR Default-mode architecture (§2.4, §2.9); Stateless API scale-out (§2.1, §2.3 D5); &lt; ~1 s propagation NFR (§1.6); WCAG 2.2 AA (§1.6).</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.2, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2, §2.4, §2.9</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "Epic" --title "EPIC-6: Real-time Collaboration (Azure SignalR)" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-6; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p><b>Goal:</b> When any member mutates a board (creates/edits/moves/deletes a list, card, metadata field, or comment; renames the board; changes membership), every other member currently viewing that board sees the change within ~1 s — delivered over Azure SignalR Service (Default mode) in a way that keeps the API stateless and horizontally scalable.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Real-time collaboration (§1.2, §1.5); Azure SignalR Default-mode architecture (§2.4, §2.9); Stateless API scale-out (§2.1, §2.3 D5); &lt; ~1 s propagation NFR (§1.6); WCAG 2.2 AA (§1.6).</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.2, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2, §2.4, §2.9</p>"
```

### Epic — EPIC-7: Per-board activity feed
- **Type:** Epic · **Parent:** —
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-7; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Goal:</b> Any board member (Owner, Editor, or Viewer) can see a chronological history of what changed on the board — who did it, what they did, and when — giving teams full visibility into board activity. Non-members cannot read the feed (existence not disclosed). The log is append-only and immutable: entries are written by the system as a side effect of other mutations; users cannot create, edit, or delete them.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Activity feed (§1.3, §1.5); per-board roles enforced server-side (§1.4); pagination and authorization NFRs (§1.6).</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "Epic" --title "EPIC-7: Per-board activity feed" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-7; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p><b>Goal:</b> Any board member (Owner, Editor, or Viewer) can see a chronological history of what changed on the board — who did it, what they did, and when — giving teams full visibility into board activity. Non-members cannot read the feed (existence not disclosed). The log is append-only and immutable: entries are written by the system as a side effect of other mutations; users cannot create, edit, or delete them.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Activity feed (§1.3, §1.5); per-board roles enforced server-side (§1.4); pagination and authorization NFRs (§1.6).</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>"
```
### Epic — EPIC-8: Search & Filtering Within a Board
- **Type:** Epic · **Parent:** —
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-8; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Goal:</b> A board member can quickly narrow a board&apos;s cards by metadata attributes or freetext to find the work that matters, entirely within a single board, with server-enforced membership scoping, sub-1.5s performance on a ~200-card board, and a clear UX for active filters and empty results.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Search/filter (&sect;1.3); Performance &mdash; board ~200 cards &lt; ~1.5s, all list endpoints paginated (&sect;1.6); Roles/membership enforced server-side (&sect;1.4).</p><p><b>Traces:</b> &sect;1.3, &sect;1.4, &sect;1.6, &sect;2.2</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "Epic" --title "EPIC-8: Search & Filtering Within a Board" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-8; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p><b>Goal:</b> A board member can quickly narrow a board&apos;s cards by metadata attributes or freetext to find the work that matters, entirely within a single board, with server-enforced membership scoping, sub-1.5s performance on a ~200-card board, and a clear UX for active filters and empty results.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> Search/filter (&sect;1.3); Performance &mdash; board ~200 cards &lt; ~1.5s, all list endpoints paginated (&sect;1.6); Roles/membership enforced server-side (&sect;1.4).</p><p><b>Traces:</b> &sect;1.3, &sect;1.4, &sect;1.6, &sect;2.2</p>"
```

### Epic — EPIC-9: My Tasks — cross-board assigned card aggregation
- **Type:** Epic · **Parent:** —
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-9; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Goal:</b> A user sees, in one place, every card assigned to them across all boards they are a member of, can triage those cards by sorting and filtering, and can navigate directly to any card in its board &mdash; without ever surfacing a card from a board they cannot access.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> &apos;My Tasks&apos; cross-board view (&sect;1.3, &sect;1.5); per-board roles and membership boundary (&sect;1.4); assignees established by EPIC-4; board membership established by EPIC-1. Aggregation must respect the membership boundary at query time.</p><p><b>Traces:</b> &sect;1.4, &sect;1.5, &sect;1.6, &sect;2.2</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "Epic" --title "EPIC-9: My Tasks — cross-board assigned card aggregation" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-9; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p><b>Goal:</b> A user sees, in one place, every card assigned to them across all boards they are a member of, can triage those cards by sorting and filtering, and can navigate directly to any card in its board &mdash; without ever surfacing a card from a board they cannot access.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> &apos;My Tasks&apos; cross-board view (&sect;1.3, &sect;1.5); per-board roles and membership boundary (&sect;1.4); assignees established by EPIC-4; board membership established by EPIC-1. Aggregation must respect the membership boundary at query time.</p><p><b>Traces:</b> &sect;1.4, &sect;1.5, &sect;1.6, &sect;2.2</p>"
```
### Epic — EPIC-10: Observability, Health & Resilience
- **Type:** Epic · **Parent:** —
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-10; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Goal:</b> The running system is observable, fails safe, and is probe-ready for load balancers and orchestrators. Unhandled errors are captured centrally in Sentry and surface to callers as consistent RFC 7807 problem responses. Engineers and on-call responders can correlate every request, confirm process health, and trust that no secrets or PII are ever leaked through logs or error responses.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> §1.6 (reliability, structured logging, global error handling); §2.9 (health probes /health liveness + /health/ready readiness); §2.10 (secrets handling — Sentry DSN via app setting/Key Vault for the backend, public ingestion-scoped DSN in runtime config.json for the SPA); ADR-000 R3 (Sentry replaces App Insights; CI uploads release + source maps; Sentry alert wires incident.opened).</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.6, §2.9, §2.10, ADR-000 R3</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "Epic" --title "EPIC-10: Observability, Health & Resilience" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-10; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p><b>Goal:</b> The running system is observable, fails safe, and is probe-ready for load balancers and orchestrators. Unhandled errors are captured centrally in Sentry and surface to callers as consistent RFC 7807 problem responses. Engineers and on-call responders can correlate every request, confirm process health, and trust that no secrets or PII are ever leaked through logs or error responses.</p><p><b>FRs covered:</b> §1.6 (reliability, structured logging, global error handling); §2.9 (health probes /health liveness + /health/ready readiness); §2.10 (secrets handling — Sentry DSN via app setting/Key Vault for the backend, public ingestion-scoped DSN in runtime config.json for the SPA); ADR-000 R3 (Sentry replaces App Insights; CI uploads release + source maps; Sentry alert wires incident.opened).</p><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.6, §2.9, §2.10, ADR-000 R3</p>"
```

## User Stories
### User Story — STORY-0.1: Register an account
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-0 → <EPIC-0-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-0; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a new visitor, I want to register with an email and password, so that I have an account that owns my boards and cards.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security:</b> password stored as a salted hash (ASP.NET Core Identity / PBKDF2-class); input validated server-side; <b>DTOs only at the API boundary</b> (no entity leakage); <b>RFC 7807</b> for every error path; secrets (JWT signing key) sourced from Key Vault, not config (§2.10) — relevant once login is added in STORY-0.2.</li><li><b>Password policy (the 'policy' the ACs refer to):</b> minimum <b>8</b> characters, maximum <b>128</b>; <b>no</b> mandatory character-class complexity (per NIST SP 800-63B); enforced via ASP.NET Core Identity PasswordOptions and surfaced as the RFC 7807 400 when violated.</li><li><b>Clean Architecture (§2.2):</b> User entity in Domain; register use-case in Application; EF Core persistence + password hasher in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api. Dependencies point inward only.</li><li><b>Reliability:</b> EF Core migration creates the Users table with a <b>unique index on Email</b> (concurrency-safe duplicate rejection); structured logging on the register path (no PII/secrets in logs); global error handler emits the 7807 envelope.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA on the registration form (labels, error association, focus order, contrast).</li><li>This story has <b>no server-side authorization</b> AC — registration is the pre-authentication boundary itself.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Login / JWT issuance (STORY-0.2), email verification, password reset, social/OAuth login, account lockout, rate-limiting, and CAPTCHA.</li><li>Board/card creation (later stories in this epic).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.6, §2.2, §2.10</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am an unregistered visitor on the registration page <b>When</b> I submit a well-formed, unused email and a password that meets the policy <b>Then</b> my account is created and persisted in SQL, the password is stored only as a salted hash, and I receive a 201 Created with a DTO containing my id and email (never the password/hash).</p><p><b>Given</b> an email that is already registered <b>When</b> I submit registration with that email <b>Then</b> I receive an RFC 7807 problem response with status 409 Conflict, and no second account is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> two registration requests for the same new email arrive concurrently <b>When</b> both are processed <b>Then</b> exactly one account is created and the other returns the same 409 Conflict RFC 7807 response — enforced by a <b>unique index on Users.Email</b>, not by an application-layer check alone.</p><p><b>Given</b> invalid input (malformed email, or a password failing the policy) <b>When</b> I submit registration <b>Then</b> I receive an RFC 7807 400 validation problem that names the offending field(s), and no account is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> the registration form <b>When</b> it is loading, submitting, or showing a server error <b>Then</b> distinct loading and error states are shown, the form is fully keyboard-operable with programmatic labels and focus management, and it meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p><p><b>Given</b> a successfully created account <b>When</b> I inspect the stored row <b>Then</b> the password column holds a salted one-way hash only — plaintext never appears in the database or in logs.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-0.1: Register an account" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-0; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As a new visitor, I want to register with an email and password, so that I have an account that owns my boards and cards.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security:</b> password stored as a salted hash (ASP.NET Core Identity / PBKDF2-class); input validated server-side; <b>DTOs only at the API boundary</b> (no entity leakage); <b>RFC 7807</b> for every error path; secrets (JWT signing key) sourced from Key Vault, not config (§2.10) — relevant once login is added in STORY-0.2.</li><li><b>Password policy (the 'policy' the ACs refer to):</b> minimum <b>8</b> characters, maximum <b>128</b>; <b>no</b> mandatory character-class complexity (per NIST SP 800-63B); enforced via ASP.NET Core Identity PasswordOptions and surfaced as the RFC 7807 400 when violated.</li><li><b>Clean Architecture (§2.2):</b> User entity in Domain; register use-case in Application; EF Core persistence + password hasher in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api. Dependencies point inward only.</li><li><b>Reliability:</b> EF Core migration creates the Users table with a <b>unique index on Email</b> (concurrency-safe duplicate rejection); structured logging on the register path (no PII/secrets in logs); global error handler emits the 7807 envelope.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA on the registration form (labels, error association, focus order, contrast).</li><li>This story has <b>no server-side authorization</b> AC — registration is the pre-authentication boundary itself.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Login / JWT issuance (STORY-0.2), email verification, password reset, social/OAuth login, account lockout, rate-limiting, and CAPTCHA.</li><li>Board/card creation (later stories in this epic).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.6, §2.2, §2.10</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am an unregistered visitor on the registration page <b>When</b> I submit a well-formed, unused email and a password that meets the policy <b>Then</b> my account is created and persisted in SQL, the password is stored only as a salted hash, and I receive a 201 Created with a DTO containing my id and email (never the password/hash).</p><p><b>Given</b> an email that is already registered <b>When</b> I submit registration with that email <b>Then</b> I receive an RFC 7807 problem response with status 409 Conflict, and no second account is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> two registration requests for the same new email arrive concurrently <b>When</b> both are processed <b>Then</b> exactly one account is created and the other returns the same 409 Conflict RFC 7807 response — enforced by a <b>unique index on Users.Email</b>, not by an application-layer check alone.</p><p><b>Given</b> invalid input (malformed email, or a password failing the policy) <b>When</b> I submit registration <b>Then</b> I receive an RFC 7807 400 validation problem that names the offending field(s), and no account is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> the registration form <b>When</b> it is loading, submitting, or showing a server error <b>Then</b> distinct loading and error states are shown, the form is fully keyboard-operable with programmatic labels and focus management, and it meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p><p><b>Given</b> a successfully created account <b>When</b> I inspect the stored row <b>Then</b> the password column holds a salted one-way hash only — plaintext never appears in the database or in logs.</p>"
```

**Link to parent**
```
az boards work-item relation add --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --id <this-story-id> --relation-type parent --target-id <EPIC-0-id>
```

### User Story — STORY-0.2: Log in and receive a session
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-0 → <EPIC-0-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-0; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a registered user, I want to log in with my email and password and receive a session token, so that I can make authenticated requests for the rest of my session.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security:</b> JWT signing key sourced from <b>Key Vault via managed identity</b> (§2.10), never in config, with <b>fail-fast startup</b> if the key is unavailable (no silent dev-key fallback); token transmitted over HTTPS; <b>no user enumeration</b> on failed login; credentials never written to logs; <b>RFC 7807</b> on every error path; <b>DTOs only</b> at the API boundary.</li><li><b>Token handling (client):</b> the SPA stores the JWT in sessionStorage (cleared on tab close) and attaches it as Authorization: Bearer &lt;token&gt; on every subsequent API request — not an HttpOnly cookie (this is the agreed skeleton convention; the auth middleware and Vue HTTP client are built to match).</li><li><b>Clean Architecture (§2.2):</b> authenticate use-case in Application; token service + password verification in Infrastructure; thin controller + auth middleware in Api; User entity in Domain.</li><li><b>Reliability:</b> structured logging on the auth path (outcome only, no secrets); global error handler emits the 7807 envelope.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA on the login form.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Refresh tokens, 'remember me', server-side logout/token revocation, MFA, password reset, social/OAuth login, and lockout/rate-limiting (all deferred).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.6, §2.2, §2.10</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> a registered user submitting correct credentials <b>When</b> I log in <b>Then</b> I receive 200 OK with a signed JWT and a user DTO (id, email); the token is signed with the Key Vault–sourced key and carries my user id and an expiry.</p><p><b>Given</b> an unknown email or a wrong password <b>When</b> I log in <b>Then</b> I receive an RFC 7807 401 with a <b>generic</b> message that does not reveal which field was wrong (no user enumeration), and no token is issued.</p><p><b>Given</b> missing or malformed fields <b>When</b> I log in <b>Then</b> I receive an RFC 7807 400 validation problem naming the offending field(s), and no token is issued.</p><p><b>Given</b> a request to a protected endpoint <b>When</b> I present a valid unexpired JWT <b>Then</b> it is accepted; <b>When</b> the token is expired or tampered <b>Then</b> I receive 401 and the request is rejected.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am on the SPA with an active session <b>When</b> any authenticated request returns 401 (e.g. the token expired while I was idle) <b>Then</b> the stored token is cleared and I am redirected to the login page — no silent failure or infinite retry.</p><p><b>Given</b> the API is starting up <b>When</b> the Key Vault–held signing key cannot be loaded (managed identity not provisioned or misconfigured) <b>Then</b> the application <b>fails to start</b> with a structured error log entry — it never falls back silently to a dev/in-config key.</p><p><b>Given</b> the login form <b>When</b> it is loading, submitting, or showing an auth error <b>Then</b> distinct loading and error states are shown, and the form meets WCAG 2.2 AA (labels, error association, keyboard operability, focus).</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-0.2: Log in and receive a session" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-0; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As a registered user, I want to log in with my email and password and receive a session token, so that I can make authenticated requests for the rest of my session.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security:</b> JWT signing key sourced from <b>Key Vault via managed identity</b> (§2.10), never in config, with <b>fail-fast startup</b> if the key is unavailable (no silent dev-key fallback); token transmitted over HTTPS; <b>no user enumeration</b> on failed login; credentials never written to logs; <b>RFC 7807</b> on every error path; <b>DTOs only</b> at the API boundary.</li><li><b>Token handling (client):</b> the SPA stores the JWT in sessionStorage (cleared on tab close) and attaches it as Authorization: Bearer &lt;token&gt; on every subsequent API request — not an HttpOnly cookie (this is the agreed skeleton convention; the auth middleware and Vue HTTP client are built to match).</li><li><b>Clean Architecture (§2.2):</b> authenticate use-case in Application; token service + password verification in Infrastructure; thin controller + auth middleware in Api; User entity in Domain.</li><li><b>Reliability:</b> structured logging on the auth path (outcome only, no secrets); global error handler emits the 7807 envelope.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA on the login form.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Refresh tokens, 'remember me', server-side logout/token revocation, MFA, password reset, social/OAuth login, and lockout/rate-limiting (all deferred).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.6, §2.2, §2.10</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> a registered user submitting correct credentials <b>When</b> I log in <b>Then</b> I receive 200 OK with a signed JWT and a user DTO (id, email); the token is signed with the Key Vault–sourced key and carries my user id and an expiry.</p><p><b>Given</b> an unknown email or a wrong password <b>When</b> I log in <b>Then</b> I receive an RFC 7807 401 with a <b>generic</b> message that does not reveal which field was wrong (no user enumeration), and no token is issued.</p><p><b>Given</b> missing or malformed fields <b>When</b> I log in <b>Then</b> I receive an RFC 7807 400 validation problem naming the offending field(s), and no token is issued.</p><p><b>Given</b> a request to a protected endpoint <b>When</b> I present a valid unexpired JWT <b>Then</b> it is accepted; <b>When</b> the token is expired or tampered <b>Then</b> I receive 401 and the request is rejected.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am on the SPA with an active session <b>When</b> any authenticated request returns 401 (e.g. the token expired while I was idle) <b>Then</b> the stored token is cleared and I am redirected to the login page — no silent failure or infinite retry.</p><p><b>Given</b> the API is starting up <b>When</b> the Key Vault–held signing key cannot be loaded (managed identity not provisioned or misconfigured) <b>Then</b> the application <b>fails to start</b> with a structured error log entry — it never falls back silently to a dev/in-config key.</p><p><b>Given</b> the login form <b>When</b> it is loading, submitting, or showing an auth error <b>Then</b> distinct loading and error states are shown, and the form meets WCAG 2.2 AA (labels, error association, keyboard operability, focus).</p>"
```

### User Story — STORY-0.3: Create a board
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-0 → <EPIC-0-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-0; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As an authenticated user, I want to create a board with a name, so that I have a place to organize my cards and can return to it later.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security / authorization:</b> every board mutation and read is <b>authenticated and authorized server-side</b> — the creator becomes Owner; non-members cannot read or mutate the board. <b>Status-code convention (shared across this epic):</b> 401 unauthenticated; 404 for an authenticated <b>non-member</b> (the resource's existence is not disclosed — prevents enumeration); 403 is reserved for a <i>member</i> whose role forbids the action (not reachable in EPIC-0, where the only role is Owner); 400 for validation.</li><li><b>Performance / pagination contract:</b> GET /boards is <b>paginated</b> (§1.6 — all list endpoints paginated), even though EPIC-0 expects ~1 board. Contract (shared by every list endpoint in this epic): <b>offset-based</b>, query params page (1-indexed, default 1) and pageSize (default 20, max 100); response envelope { items: [...], page, pageSize, total }.</li><li><b>API:</b> <b>DTOs only</b> at the boundary; input validated; <b>RFC 7807</b> on every error path.</li><li><b>Data:</b> board name is <b>1–100 characters</b> (enforced in the Domain entity, the EF column, and client validation consistently); board creation + default-list seeding commit in <b>one transaction</b>.</li><li><b>Clean Architecture (§2.2):</b> Board, List, BoardMember entities in Domain; create-board use-case in Application; EF Core persistence in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li><b>Reliability:</b> EF Core migration creates Boards, Lists, BoardMembers; structured logging; global 7807 error handling.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA on the create-board form and the boards view.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Renaming/deleting boards, inviting/managing members, assigning roles beyond creator-as-Owner, multiple lists or any list UI/management, real-time propagation of board creation to other users.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.3, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I POST a board with a valid name (<b>1–100 characters</b>) <b>Then</b> the board is created and persisted with me recorded as its <b>Owner</b>, a single default list is seeded inside it, and I receive 201 Created with a board DTO (id, name, my role = Owner).</p><p><b>Given</b> board creation is in progress <b>When</b> seeding the default list fails <b>Then</b> the whole operation is rolled back in a <b>single transaction</b> — no orphaned board exists without its default list.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I submit a blank name or one longer than <b>100 characters</b> <b>Then</b> I receive an RFC 7807 400 validation problem and no board is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I present no token or an invalid JWT <b>When</b> I POST a board <b>Then</b> I receive 401 and no board is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> a board I own <b>When</b> I GET /boards/{id} (e.g. after a page reload) <b>Then</b> I retrieve the board; <b>Given</b> a board I am not a member of <b>When</b> I GET it <b>Then</b> I receive 404 — its existence is not disclosed to non-members (server-side authorization on read).</p><p><b>Given</b> I have signed back in <b>When</b> I GET /boards <b>Then</b> I receive my boards as a <b>paginated</b> response (page metadata present even for a single board), so the SPA can land me back on my board.</p><p><b>Given</b> the create-board UI <b>When</b> there are no boards yet, while loading, or on error <b>Then</b> empty, loading, and error states are shown, and the form/dialog meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-0.3: Create a board" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-0; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As an authenticated user, I want to create a board with a name, so that I have a place to organize my cards and can return to it later.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security / authorization:</b> every board mutation and read is <b>authenticated and authorized server-side</b> — the creator becomes Owner; non-members cannot read or mutate the board. <b>Status-code convention (shared across this epic):</b> 401 unauthenticated; 404 for an authenticated <b>non-member</b> (the resource's existence is not disclosed — prevents enumeration); 403 is reserved for a <i>member</i> whose role forbids the action (not reachable in EPIC-0, where the only role is Owner); 400 for validation.</li><li><b>Performance / pagination contract:</b> GET /boards is <b>paginated</b> (§1.6 — all list endpoints paginated), even though EPIC-0 expects ~1 board. Contract (shared by every list endpoint in this epic): <b>offset-based</b>, query params page (1-indexed, default 1) and pageSize (default 20, max 100); response envelope { items: [...], page, pageSize, total }.</li><li><b>API:</b> <b>DTOs only</b> at the boundary; input validated; <b>RFC 7807</b> on every error path.</li><li><b>Data:</b> board name is <b>1–100 characters</b> (enforced in the Domain entity, the EF column, and client validation consistently); board creation + default-list seeding commit in <b>one transaction</b>.</li><li><b>Clean Architecture (§2.2):</b> Board, List, BoardMember entities in Domain; create-board use-case in Application; EF Core persistence in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li><b>Reliability:</b> EF Core migration creates Boards, Lists, BoardMembers; structured logging; global 7807 error handling.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA on the create-board form and the boards view.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Renaming/deleting boards, inviting/managing members, assigning roles beyond creator-as-Owner, multiple lists or any list UI/management, real-time propagation of board creation to other users.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.3, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I POST a board with a valid name (<b>1–100 characters</b>) <b>Then</b> the board is created and persisted with me recorded as its <b>Owner</b>, a single default list is seeded inside it, and I receive 201 Created with a board DTO (id, name, my role = Owner).</p><p><b>Given</b> board creation is in progress <b>When</b> seeding the default list fails <b>Then</b> the whole operation is rolled back in a <b>single transaction</b> — no orphaned board exists without its default list.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I submit a blank name or one longer than <b>100 characters</b> <b>Then</b> I receive an RFC 7807 400 validation problem and no board is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I present no token or an invalid JWT <b>When</b> I POST a board <b>Then</b> I receive 401 and no board is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> a board I own <b>When</b> I GET /boards/{id} (e.g. after a page reload) <b>Then</b> I retrieve the board; <b>Given</b> a board I am not a member of <b>When</b> I GET it <b>Then</b> I receive 404 — its existence is not disclosed to non-members (server-side authorization on read).</p><p><b>Given</b> I have signed back in <b>When</b> I GET /boards <b>Then</b> I receive my boards as a <b>paginated</b> response (page metadata present even for a single board), so the SPA can land me back on my board.</p><p><b>Given</b> the create-board UI <b>When</b> there are no boards yet, while loading, or on error <b>Then</b> empty, loading, and error states are shown, and the form/dialog meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>"
```

### User Story — STORY-0.4: Add a card to a board (persists)
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-0 → <EPIC-0-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-0; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As an authenticated board Owner, I want to add a card with a title to my board, so that I can capture a task and trust it is still there when I come back.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security / authorization:</b> card creation and the card-read are <b>authenticated and authorized server-side</b> against board membership. In EPIC-0 the <b>only role is Owner</b> (the board's creator) — Owner may add; non-member cannot. The <b>Editor</b> role (and any other non-Owner authorization) is deferred to the later epic that introduces membership management, and is intentionally not wired here (no dead role-check code). <b>Status codes</b> follow the shared convention defined in STORY-0.3: 401 unauthenticated, 404 non-member (existence not disclosed), 400 validation; 403 is not reachable in EPIC-0. The target <b>listId is verified to belong to the caller's board</b> before the card is created (prevents cross-board insertion / IDOR).</li><li><b>Data:</b> card title is <b>1–255 characters</b> (enforced consistently in the Domain entity, EF column, and client validation).</li><li><b>Performance / pagination contract:</b> the board's card list is <b>paginated</b> (§1.6 — board target ~200 cards loads in &lt;1.5s), using the <b>same envelope as STORY-0.3</b>: offset-based, page (1-indexed, default 1) + pageSize (default 20, max 100); response { items: [...], page, pageSize, total }.</li><li><b>API:</b> <b>DTOs only</b> at the boundary; input validated; <b>RFC 7807</b> on every error path.</li><li><b>Clean Architecture (§2.2):</b> Card entity in Domain; add-card use-case in Application; EF Core persistence in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li><b>Reliability:</b> EF Core migration creates Cards; structured logging; global 7807 error handling.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA on the add-card form and board view.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Editing, moving, or deleting cards; drag-and-drop ordering / card positions; labels, assignees, due dates, priorities, comments; <b>real-time propagation to other users</b> (no SignalR in EPIC-0); the activity feed.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.3, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am the Owner of a board (with its seeded default list) <b>When</b> I POST a card with a valid title (<b>1–255 characters</b>) <b>Then</b> the card is created in that list, persisted, and I receive 201 Created with a card DTO (id, title, listId).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I POST a card whose listId does not belong to a board I am a member of (or does not exist) <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (the list's existence is not disclosed to non-members) and no card is created — list ownership is validated server-side, not assumed from board membership alone.</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a blank title or one longer than <b>255 characters</b> <b>When</b> I add a card <b>Then</b> I receive an RFC 7807 400 validation problem and no card is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board, or present no/invalid token <b>When</b> I POST a card <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member — existence not disclosed) or 401 (unauthenticated) and no card is created (server-side authorization — <b>Owner only</b> in EPIC-0).</p><p><b>Given</b> I created a card <b>When</b> I reload the board — or sign out and back in and re-open it — <b>Then</b> GET of the board's cards returns the card exactly as created (the epic's headline persistence proof), as a <b>paginated</b> response.</p><p><b>Given</b> the board view <b>When</b> it has no cards yet, is loading, or errors <b>Then</b> empty, loading, and error states are shown, and the add-card form meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-0.4: Add a card to a board (persists)" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-0; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As an authenticated board Owner, I want to add a card with a title to my board, so that I can capture a task and trust it is still there when I come back.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security / authorization:</b> card creation and the card-read are <b>authenticated and authorized server-side</b> against board membership. In EPIC-0 the <b>only role is Owner</b> (the board's creator) — Owner may add; non-member cannot. The <b>Editor</b> role (and any other non-Owner authorization) is deferred to the later epic that introduces membership management, and is intentionally not wired here (no dead role-check code). <b>Status codes</b> follow the shared convention defined in STORY-0.3: 401 unauthenticated, 404 non-member (existence not disclosed), 400 validation; 403 is not reachable in EPIC-0. The target <b>listId is verified to belong to the caller's board</b> before the card is created (prevents cross-board insertion / IDOR).</li><li><b>Data:</b> card title is <b>1–255 characters</b> (enforced consistently in the Domain entity, EF column, and client validation).</li><li><b>Performance / pagination contract:</b> the board's card list is <b>paginated</b> (§1.6 — board target ~200 cards loads in &lt;1.5s), using the <b>same envelope as STORY-0.3</b>: offset-based, page (1-indexed, default 1) + pageSize (default 20, max 100); response { items: [...], page, pageSize, total }.</li><li><b>API:</b> <b>DTOs only</b> at the boundary; input validated; <b>RFC 7807</b> on every error path.</li><li><b>Clean Architecture (§2.2):</b> Card entity in Domain; add-card use-case in Application; EF Core persistence in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li><b>Reliability:</b> EF Core migration creates Cards; structured logging; global 7807 error handling.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA on the add-card form and board view.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Editing, moving, or deleting cards; drag-and-drop ordering / card positions; labels, assignees, due dates, priorities, comments; <b>real-time propagation to other users</b> (no SignalR in EPIC-0); the activity feed.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.3, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am the Owner of a board (with its seeded default list) <b>When</b> I POST a card with a valid title (<b>1–255 characters</b>) <b>Then</b> the card is created in that list, persisted, and I receive 201 Created with a card DTO (id, title, listId).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I POST a card whose listId does not belong to a board I am a member of (or does not exist) <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (the list's existence is not disclosed to non-members) and no card is created — list ownership is validated server-side, not assumed from board membership alone.</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a blank title or one longer than <b>255 characters</b> <b>When</b> I add a card <b>Then</b> I receive an RFC 7807 400 validation problem and no card is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board, or present no/invalid token <b>When</b> I POST a card <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member — existence not disclosed) or 401 (unauthenticated) and no card is created (server-side authorization — <b>Owner only</b> in EPIC-0).</p><p><b>Given</b> I created a card <b>When</b> I reload the board — or sign out and back in and re-open it — <b>Then</b> GET of the board's cards returns the card exactly as created (the epic's headline persistence proof), as a <b>paginated</b> response.</p><p><b>Given</b> the board view <b>When</b> it has no cards yet, is loading, or errors <b>Then</b> empty, loading, and error states are shown, and the add-card form meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>"
```

### User Story — STORY-1.1: View a board's members and their roles
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-1 → <EPIC-1-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-1; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a board member (any role), I want to see the full list of members on a board and their roles, so that I understand who has access and what they can do.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security / authorization:</b> read is permitted for all three roles; 404 (not 403) for non-members (HTTP status convention from STORY-0.3/EPIC-0: 401 unauthenticated, 404 non-member, 403 wrong-role-for-action).</li><li><b>Performance / pagination:</b> offset-based pagination envelope (page, pageSize default 20 max 100) consistent with the shared envelope in EPIC-0.</li><li><b>API:</b> DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li><b>Clean Architecture:</b> query handler in Application; EF Core projection in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api. No EF / Microsoft.* types in Domain.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA; role badges must not rely solely on colour.</li><li><b>Real-time:</b> membership changes made by another Owner propagate &lt;1s (via EPIC-6) — this story does not author SignalR code.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Adding, removing, or changing roles (STORY-1.2, 1.3, 1.4).</li><li>Pagination UI controls (infinite scroll or page buttons) — the API contract is defined here; UI pagination controls may be deferred.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am an authenticated member of a board (Owner, Editor, or Viewer) <b>When</b> I request GET /boards/{boardId}/members (with optional page / pageSize) <b>Then</b> I receive 200 OK with a paginated envelope { items, page, pageSize, total } where each item contains the member's user id, display name, email, role, and the date they were added.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated but not a member of the board <b>When</b> I request GET /boards/{boardId}/members <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (board existence not disclosed to non-members).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am unauthenticated <b>When</b> I request GET /boards/{boardId}/members <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> the board has more than pageSize members <b>When</b> I request page 2 <b>Then</b> I receive the correct slice, with total accurately reflecting the full member count.</p><p><b>Given</b> the members panel is loading <b>When</b> data is in flight <b>Then</b> a visible loading indicator is shown and the list area is not blank.</p><p><b>Given</b> the board has at least one member <b>When</b> the data loads <b>Then</b> each member row shows display name, email, and role badge; the list is accessible and meets WCAG 2.2 AA (role badge has sufficient contrast, row is keyboard-navigable, name is not conveyed by colour alone).</p><p><b>Given</b> the fetch fails (network or 5xx) <b>When</b> the panel is open <b>Then</b> an error state with a retry action is displayed and a role='alert' message is announced to screen-reader users.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-1.1: View a board's members and their roles" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-1; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As a board member (any role), I want to see the full list of members on a board and their roles, so that I understand who has access and what they can do.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security / authorization:</b> read is permitted for all three roles; 404 (not 403) for non-members (HTTP status convention from STORY-0.3/EPIC-0: 401 unauthenticated, 404 non-member, 403 wrong-role-for-action).</li><li><b>Performance / pagination:</b> offset-based pagination envelope (page, pageSize default 20 max 100) consistent with the shared envelope in EPIC-0.</li><li><b>API:</b> DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li><b>Clean Architecture:</b> query handler in Application; EF Core projection in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api. No EF / Microsoft.* types in Domain.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA; role badges must not rely solely on colour.</li><li><b>Real-time:</b> membership changes made by another Owner propagate &lt;1s (via EPIC-6) — this story does not author SignalR code.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Adding, removing, or changing roles (STORY-1.2, 1.3, 1.4).</li><li>Pagination UI controls (infinite scroll or page buttons) — the API contract is defined here; the list is accessible and meets WCAG 2.2 AA (role badge has sufficient contrast, row is keyboard-navigable, name is not conveyed by colour alone).</p><p><b>Given</b> the fetch fails (network or 5xx) <b>When</b> the panel is open <b>Then</b> an error state with a retry action is displayed and a role='alert' message is announced to screen-reader users.</p>"
```

### User Story — STORY-1.2: Add a member to a board by email (Owner only)
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-1 → <EPIC-1-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-1; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a board Owner, I want to add a registered user to my board by their email address and assign them an initial role, so that they can immediately collaborate within the permissions I choose.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security / authorization:</b> Owner-only mutation; 403 for Editor/Viewer; 404 for non-members; 401 for unauthenticated callers. The email lookup MUST NOT disclose whether an email is registered when the caller is not an Owner (guard is: request rejected before lookup for non-Owners).</li><li><b>API:</b> DTOs only; RFC 7807 on every error path; 422 for unregistered email; 409 for duplicate.</li><li><b>Data:</b> role is validated against the BoardRole enumeration in the Domain; no free-text roles accepted.</li><li><b>Clean Architecture:</b> AddBoardMemberCommand in Application; user lookup + membership persistence in Infrastructure; no EF/Microsoft.* types in Domain.</li><li><b>Real-time:</b> the new member's appearance in other Owners' members panels propagates &lt;1s (via EPIC-6) — this story does not author SignalR code.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA on the add-member form; confirm or success feedback via role='status'.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Email invitation with a pending-accept flow — this story requires the invitee to already be a registered user.</li><li>Bulk add / CSV import.</li><li>Notification email to the new member (future).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I POST { email, role } to /boards/{boardId}/members where email matches a registered user and role is one of Owner, Editor, or Viewer <b>Then</b> the user is added as a member with that role, I receive 201 Created with the new membership DTO (userId, displayName, email, role, addedAt), and the board's member list reflects the addition.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I POST an email that is not registered in the system <b>Then</b> I receive 422 Unprocessable Entity RFC 7807 with a human-readable detail ('No account found for that email address') and no membership is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I POST an email for a user who is already a member of the board <b>Then</b> I receive 409 Conflict RFC 7807 ('User is already a member of this board') and no duplicate membership is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I POST an invalid role value or omit email <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 validation problem and no membership is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Viewer <b>When</b> I POST to /boards/{boardId}/members <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 (Owner-only action).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am unauthenticated <b>When</b> I POST to /boards/{boardId}/members <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated but not a member of the board <b>When</b> I POST to /boards/{boardId}/members <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (existence not disclosed).</p><p><b>Given</b> a user is successfully added <b>When</b> the form is submitted <b>Then</b> the member immediately appears in the members list, a success confirmation is displayed, and the add-member form resets.</p><p><b>Given</b> the add-member form is visible <b>When</b> it is in idle, submitting, or error states <b>Then</b> all states are visually distinct, the submit button is disabled while submitting, error messages are associated with their fields via aria-describedby, and the form meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>
```

**Create**
```

The email lookup MUST NOT disclose whether an email is registered when the caller is not an Owner (guard is: request rejected before lookup for non-Owners).</li><li><b>API:</b> DTOs only; RFC 7807 on every error path; 422 for unregistered email; 409 for duplicate.</li><li><b>Data:</b> role is validated against the BoardRole enumeration in the Domain; no free-text roles accepted.</li><li><b>Clean Architecture:</b> AddBoardMemberCommand in Application; user lookup + membership persistence in Infrastructure; no EF/Microsoft.* types in Domain.</li><li><b>Real-time:</b> the new member's appearance in other Owners' members panels propagates &lt;1s (via EPIC-6) — this story does not author SignalR code.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA on the add-member form; confirm or success feedback via role='status'.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Email invitation with a pending-accept flow — this story requires the invitee to already be a registered user.</li><li>Bulk add / CSV an email that is not registered in the system <b>Then</b> I receive 422 Unprocessable Entity RFC 7807 with a human-readable detail ('No account found for that email address') and no membership is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I POST an email for a user who is already a member of the board <b>Then</b> I receive 409 Conflict RFC 7807 ('User is already a member of this board') and no duplicate membership is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I POST an invalid role value or omit email <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 validation problem and no membership is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Viewer <b>When</b> I POST to /boards/{boardId}/members <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 (Owner-only action).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am unauthenticated <b>When</b> I POST to /boards/{boardId}/members <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated but not a member of the board <b>When</b> I POST to /boards/{boardId}/members <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (existence not disclosed).</p><p><b>Given</b> a user is successfully added <b>When</b> the form is submitted <b>Then</b> the member immediately appears in the members list, a success confirmation is displayed, and the add-member form resets.</p><p><b>Given</b> the add-member form is visible <b>When</b> it is in idle, submitting, or error states <b>Then</b> all states are visually distinct, the submit button is disabled while submitting, error messages are associated with their fields via aria-describedby, and the form meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>"
```

### User Story — STORY-1.3: Change a member's role (Owner only)
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-1 → <EPIC-1-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-1; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a board Owner, I want to change any member's role between Owner, Editor, and Viewer, so that I can adjust team permissions as the project evolves — without accidentally leaving a board with no Owner.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security / authorization:</b> Owner-only mutation; 403 for Editor/Viewer; 404 for non-members of the calling user; 401 unauthenticated. The last-Owner guard is enforced in the <b>Domain layer</b> (invariant on Board aggregate) so it cannot be bypassed at any call site.</li><li><b>Last-Owner protection:</b> the check counts active Owner memberships <b>before</b> applying the change; the domain raises a domain exception that the Application layer maps to 409.</li><li><b>API:</b> DTOs only; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li><b>Clean Architecture:</b> ChangeMemberRoleCommand in Application; persistence in Infrastructure; invariant in Domain.</li><li><b>Real-time:</b> the role change is visible to other members &lt;1s (via EPIC-6) — this story does not author SignalR code.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA on role selectors; change confirmation via role='status'.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Bulk role changes.</li><li>A dedicated 'transfer ownership' flow — an Owner can promote another user to Owner, then demote themselves (two sequential PATCH calls).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner and the target member exists on this board <b>When</b> I PATCH /boards/{boardId}/members/{userId} with { role: 'Editor' } (or any valid role) <b>Then</b> the member's role is updated, I receive 200 OK with the updated membership DTO (userId, displayName, email, role, addedAt), and subsequent reads reflect the new role.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I attempt to demote the last remaining Owner on the board (including demoting myself) <b>Then</b> I receive 409 Conflict RFC 7807 ('Cannot remove the last Owner from a board') and the role is not changed.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I PATCH with an invalid role value or an empty body <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 validation problem and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I PATCH the role of a userId who is not a member of this board <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (member not found on this board) and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Viewer <b>When</b> I PATCH any member's role <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 (Owner-only action).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am unauthenticated <b>When</b> I PATCH a member's role <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated but not a member of the board <b>When</b> I PATCH a member's role <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (existence not disclosed).</p><p><b>Given</b> a role change is submitted via the UI <b>When</b> it is in idle, submitting, or error states <b>Then</b> the role selector is disabled while submitting, a success confirmation is displayed on completion, and the last-Owner conflict is surfaced as a user-readable error (not a generic 5xx).</p><p><b>Given</b> the role selector is rendered <b>When</b> used by keyboard or assistive technology <b>Then</b> it meets WCAG 2.2 AA (labelled, focus-visible, role change announced via role='status').</p>
```

**Create**
```

The last-Owner guard is enforced in the <b>Domain layer</b> (invariant on Board aggregate) so it cannot be bypassed at any call site.</li><li><b>Last-Owner protection:</b> the check counts active Owner memberships <b>before</b> applying the change; the domain raises a domain exception that the Application layer maps to 409.</li><li><b>API:</b> DTOs only; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li><b>Clean Architecture:</b> ChangeMemberRoleCommand in Application; persistence in Infrastructure; invariant in Domain.</li><li><b>Real-time:</b> the role change is visible to other members &lt;1s (via EPIC-6) — this story does not author SignalR code.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA on role selectors; change confirmation via role='status'.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Bulk role changes.</li><li>A dedicated 'transfer ownership' flow — an Owner can promote another user to Owner, then demote themselves (two sequential PATCH calls).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner and the target member exists on this board <b>When</b> I PATCH /boards/{boardId}/members/{userId} with { role: 'Editor' } (or any valid role) <b>Then</b> the member's role is updated, I receive 200 OK with the updated membership DTO (userId, displayName, email, role, addedAt), and subsequent reads reflect the new role.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I attempt to demote the last remaining Owner on the board (including demoting myself) <b>Then</b> I receive 409 Conflict RFC 7807 ('Cannot remove the last Owner from a board') and the role is not changed.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I PATCH with an invalid role value or an empty body <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 validation problem and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I PATCH the role of a userId who is not a member of this board <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (member not found on this board) and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Viewer <b>When</b> I PATCH any member's role <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 (Owner-only action).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am unauthenticated <b>When</b> I PATCH a member's role <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated but not a member of the board <b>When</b> I PATCH a member's role <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (existence not disclosed).</p><p><b>Given</b> a role change is submitted via the UI <b>When</b> it is in idle, submitting, or error states <b>Then</b> the role selector is disabled while submitting, a success confirmation is displayed on completion, and the last-Owner conflict is surfaced as a user-readable error (not a generic 5xx).</p><p><b>Given</b> the role selector is rendered <b>When</b> used by keyboard or assistive technology <b>Then</b> it meets WCAG 2.2 AA (labelled, focus-visible, role change announced via role='status').</p>"
```
