### User Story — STORY-1.4: Remove a member from a board (Owner only)
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-1 → <EPIC-1-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-1; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a board Owner, I want to remove a member from a board after confirming the action, so that I can revoke access when someone leaves the project — without risking accidental removal of the last Owner.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security / authorization:</b> Owner-only mutation; 403 for Editor/Viewer; 404 for non-members (calling user); 401 unauthenticated. Last-Owner guard enforced in the Domain layer (same invariant as STORY-1.3).</li><li><b>Destructive action:</b> a confirm step is mandatory before the DELETE request is sent (per §1.6 usability requirement); no undo.</li><li><b>Self-removal:</b> an Owner removing themselves is permitted if at least one other Owner exists. The Domain invariant is the sole guard — no special client-side logic for self vs. other.</li><li><b>API:</b> DTOs only; RFC 7807 on every error path; 204 on success (no body).</li><li><b>Clean Architecture:</b> RemoveBoardMemberCommand in Application; persistence in Infrastructure; invariant in Domain.</li><li><b>Real-time:</b> the removal is reflected for other members &lt;1s (via EPIC-6) — this story does not author SignalR code.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA; confirm dialog focus trap; destructive button styled distinctively (but not by colour alone).</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Revoking access tokens in-flight (stateless JWT — the removed member's existing tokens are valid until expiry; token revocation is a future concern).</li><li>Notifying the removed member (future).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner and the target member is not the last Owner <b>When</b> I confirm removal and DELETE /boards/{boardId}/members/{userId} <b>Then</b> the membership is deleted, I receive 204 No Content, and the member no longer appears in GET /boards/{boardId}/members.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I attempt to remove the last remaining Owner on the board (including removing myself when I am the only Owner) <b>Then</b> I receive 409 Conflict RFC 7807 ('Cannot remove the last Owner from a board') and the membership is not deleted.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I DELETE a userId who is not a member of this board <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (member not found on this board) and nothing changes.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Viewer <b>When</b> I DELETE any member <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 (Owner-only action).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am unauthenticated <b>When</b> I DELETE a member <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated but not a member of the board <b>When</b> I DELETE a member <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (existence not disclosed).</p><p><b>Given</b> I initiate removal via the UI <b>When</b> I click the remove control <b>Then</b> a confirmation dialog appears naming the member ('Remove Jane Doe from this board?') with a destructive-confirm button and a cancel button before any request is sent.</p><p><b>Given</b> I confirm removal <b>When</b> the request is in flight <b>Then</b> the confirm button is disabled/replaced with a spinner, preventing double-submission.</p><p><b>Given</b> removal succeeds <b>When</b> the response is 204 <b>Then</b> the member row is removed from the list without a full page reload, and a role='status' announcement confirms the action.</p><p><b>Given</b> removal fails (409 last-Owner, or any 5xx) <b>When</b> the dialog is still open <b>Then</b> an error message is displayed within the dialog (role='alert'), the dialog remains open, and the member is not removed from the visible list.</p><p><b>Given</b> the confirm dialog and remove controls are rendered <b>When</b> used by keyboard or assistive technology <b>Then</b> focus is trapped within the dialog when open, focus returns to the triggering element on close, and the dialog meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-1.4: Remove a member from a board (Owner only)" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-1; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As a board Owner, I want to remove a member from a board after confirming the action, so that I can revoke access when someone leaves the project — without risking accidental removal of the last Owner.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security / authorization:</b> Owner-only mutation; 403 for Editor/Viewer; 404 for non-members (calling user); 401 unauthenticated. Last-Owner guard enforced in the Domain layer (same invariant as STORY-1.3).</li><li><b>Destructive action:</b> a confirm step is mandatory before the DELETE request is sent (per §1.6 usability requirement); no undo.</li><li><b>Self-removal:</b> an Owner removing themselves is permitted if at least one other Owner exists. The Domain invariant is the sole guard — no special client-side logic for self vs. other.</li><li><b>API:</b> DTOs only; RFC 7807 on every error path; 204 on success (no body).</li><li><b>Clean Architecture:</b> RemoveBoardMemberCommand in Application; persistence in Infrastructure; invariant in Domain.</li><li><b>Real-time:</b> the removal is reflected for other members &lt;1s (via EPIC-6) — this story does not author SignalR code.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA; confirm dialog focus trap; destructive button styled distinctively (but not by colour alone).</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Revoking access tokens in-flight (stateless JWT — the removed member's existing tokens are valid until expiry; token revocation is a future concern).</li><li>Notifying the removed member (future).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner and the target member is not the last Owner <b>When</b> I confirm removal and DELETE /boards/{boardId}/members/{userId} <b>Then</b> the membership is deleted, I receive 204 No Content, and the member no longer appears in GET /boards/{boardId}/members.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I attempt to remove the last remaining Owner on the board (including removing myself when I am the only Owner) <b>Then</b> I receive 409 Conflict RFC 7807 ('Cannot remove the last Owner from a board') and the membership is not deleted.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I DELETE a userId who is not a member of this board <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (member not found on this board) and nothing changes.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Viewer <b>When</b> I DELETE any member <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 (Owner-only action).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am unauthenticated <b>When</b> I DELETE a member <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated but not a member of the board <b>When</b> I DELETE a member <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (existence not disclosed).</p><p><b>Given</b> I initiate removal via the UI <b>When</b> I click the remove control <b>Then</b> a confirmation dialog appears naming the member ('Remove Jane Doe from this board?') with a destructive-confirm button and a cancel button before any request is sent.</p><p><b>Given</b> I confirm removal <b>When</b> the request is in flight <b>Then</b> the confirm button is disabled/replaced with a spinner, preventing double-submission.</p><p><b>Given</b> removal succeeds <b>When</b> the response is 204 <b>Then</b> the member row is removed from the list without a full page reload, and a role='status' announcement confirms the action.</p><p><b>Given</b> removal fails (409 last-Owner, or any 5xx) <b>When</b> the dialog is still open <b>Then</b> an error message is displayed within the dialog (role='alert'), the dialog remains open, and the member is not removed from the visible list.</p><p><b>Given</b> the confirm dialog and remove controls are rendered <b>When</b> used by keyboard or assistive technology <b>Then</b> focus is trapped within the dialog when open, focus returns to the triggering element on close, and the dialog meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>"
```

**Link to parent**
```
az boards work-item relation add --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --id <this-story-id> --relation-type parent --target-id <EPIC-1-id>
```

---

### User Story — STORY-1.5: Enforce the per-board role matrix server-side
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-1 → <EPIC-1-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-1; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a product stakeholder, I want every board mutation to be gated by the caller's per-board role, so that Editors can collaborate freely while Viewers remain read-only and only Owners can manage membership and delete the board — with no way to bypass these rules from the client.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security / authorization (the spine):</b> This story defines the canonical authorization model. All epics EPIC-2 through EPIC-9 that introduce mutations MUST cite this convention and invoke the shared authorization service — they do not re-define it. The 403 / 404 / 401 status code meanings are frozen here and must not be varied in later epics.</li><li><b>Implementation:</b> Authorization logic lives in the <b>Application layer</b> as IBoardAuthorizationService (interface in Application; implementation in Infrastructure). The Domain layer has no dependency on it. The Api layer applies it via a policy/filter or at the top of each command handler.</li><li><b>No role caching:</b> the caller's BoardMembership row is read from the database on each authorized request. No in-process role cache (avoids stale-role window after STORY-1.3/1.4).</li><li><b>Clean Architecture:</b> no EF / Microsoft.* types in Domain; the authorization service is resolved via DI, not instantiated inline.</li><li><b>RFC 7807:</b> every 401, 403, and 404 path returns a structured problem-detail response (type, title, status, detail).</li><li><b>Testability:</b> the authorization service MUST be unit-testable in isolation (injectable, mockable) so that handler tests can assert role enforcement without a database.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Row-level security at the database layer (SQL Server RLS) — server-side application-layer enforcement is sufficient for v1.</li><li>Fine-grained permissions within a role (e.g. an Editor who can comment but not delete cards) — three-tier role matrix only.</li><li>Caching of membership for performance — deferred behind ICacheService seam (§2.11) if needed.</li><li>The SignalR hub authorization (EPIC-6 will call the same IBoardAuthorizationService when clients subscribe to board groups).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.4, §1.6, §2.2; EPIC-4 (card metadata row); EPIC-5 (comment authority rows)</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> a Viewer calls any mutating endpoint (list/card/comment/label create, edit, move, or delete) <b>When</b> the request reaches the server <b>Then</b> the server returns 403 RFC 7807 before any data is written, regardless of the request body.</p><p><b>Given</b> an Editor calls an Owner-only endpoint (add/change/remove member, delete board) <b>When</b> the request reaches the server <b>Then</b> the server returns 403 RFC 7807 before any data is written.</p><p><b>Given</b> an authenticated non-member calls any board endpoint <b>When</b> the request reaches the server <b>Then</b> the server returns 404 RFC 7807 (existence not disclosed to non-members) before any data is read or written.</p><p><b>Given</b> an unauthenticated caller reaches any board endpoint <b>When</b> the request reaches the server <b>Then</b> the server returns 401 RFC 7807 before any board-specific logic runs.</p><p><b>Given</b> a user's role is changed from Editor to Viewer (STORY-1.3) <b>When</b> they subsequently call a mutating endpoint <b>Then</b> the server immediately enforces their new Viewer restriction (role is re-read from the database per request — no in-memory caching of role).</p><p><b>Given</b> a user is removed from a board (STORY-1.4) <b>When</b> they subsequently call any endpoint for that board <b>Then</b> the server returns 404 (non-member) for all subsequent requests.</p><p><b>Given</b> an authorization check determines the caller's role <b>When</b> the board id in the route does not match any board the caller is a member of <b>Then</b> the check returns 404 (not 403), preventing membership enumeration.</p><p><b>Given</b> the role×action matrix is implemented <b>When</b> a new mutation endpoint is added in any future epic <b>Then</b> it MUST invoke the same IBoardAuthorizationService (or equivalent policy) — not implement its own ad-hoc role check. The service interface and its contract are defined in this story.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-1.5: Enforce the per-board role matrix server-side" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-1; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As a product stakeholder, I want every board mutation to be gated by the caller's per-board role, so that Editors can collaborate freely while Viewers remain read-only and only Owners can manage membership and delete the board — with no way to bypass these rules from the client.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security / authorization (the spine):</b> This story defines the canonical authorization model. All epics EPIC-2 through EPIC-9 that introduce mutations MUST cite this convention and invoke the shared authorization service — they do not re-define it. The 403 / 404 / 401 status code meanings are frozen here and must not be varied in later epics.</li><li><b>Implementation:</b> Authorization logic lives in the <b>Application layer</b> as IBoardAuthorizationService (interface in Application; implementation in Infrastructure). The Domain layer has no dependency on it. The Api layer applies it via a policy/filter or at the top of each command handler.</li><li><b>No role caching:</b> the caller's BoardMembership row is read from the database on each authorized request. No in-process role cache (avoids stale-role window after STORY-1.3/1.4).</li><li><b>Clean Architecture:</b> no EF / Microsoft.* types in Domain; the authorization service is resolved via DI, not instantiated inline.</li><li><b>RFC 7807:</b> every 401, 403, and 404 path returns a structured problem-detail response (type, title, status, detail).</li><li><b>Testability:</b> the authorization service MUST be unit-testable in isolation (injectable, mockable) so that handler tests can assert role enforcement without a database.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Row-level security at the database layer (SQL Server RLS) — server-side application-layer enforcement is sufficient for v1.</li><li>Fine-grained permissions within a role (e.g. an Editor who can comment but not delete cards) — three-tier role matrix only.</li><li>Caching of membership for performance — deferred behind ICacheService seam (§2.11) if needed.</li><li>The SignalR hub authorization (EPIC-6 will call the same IBoardAuthorizationService when clients subscribe to board groups).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.4, §1.6, §2.2; The service interface and its contract are defined in this story.</p>"

### User Story — STORY-1.6: Delete a board (Owner only)
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-1 → <EPIC-1-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-1; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a board Owner, I want to permanently delete a board after confirming the action, so that I can remove projects that are no longer needed and clean up all associated data.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security / authorization:</b> Owner-only; 403 for Editor/Viewer; 404 for non-members; 401 unauthenticated (per STORY-1.5 role matrix).</li><li><b>Cascade:</b> deletion must cascade in the <b>database</b> (EF DeleteBehavior.Cascade or SQL ON DELETE CASCADE) so that no orphaned rows remain. The cascade order: members → comments → card labels → card assignees → cards → lists → labels → board. A single transaction must cover the whole cascade.</li><li><b>Destructive action:</b> confirmation dialog mandatory before the DELETE request is sent; no undo.</li><li><b>API:</b> RFC 7807 on every error path; 204 No Content on success (no body).</li><li><b>Clean Architecture:</b> DeleteBoardCommand in Application; cascade persistence in Infrastructure; no EF/Microsoft.* types in Domain.</li><li><b>Real-time:</b> board deletion is propagated to all connected members &lt;1s (via EPIC-6), redirecting them to the boards list — this story does not author SignalR code.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA; confirm dialog focus trap; destructive button styled distinctively; board name shown in dialog to prevent misidentification.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Soft-delete / archive / restore (permanent deletion only in v1).</li><li>Notifying other members that the board was deleted (future notification system).</li><li>Exporting board data before deletion (future).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I confirm deletion and DELETE /boards/{boardId} <b>Then</b> the board, all its lists, all cards on those lists, all memberships, all labels, and all comments are deleted (cascade), I receive 204 No Content, and subsequent GET /boards/{boardId} returns 404 for all users.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board Owner <b>When</b> I DELETE the board and the cascade completes <b>Then</b> the board no longer appears in any member's board list (GET /boards), including for users who were previously Editors or Viewers.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Viewer <b>When</b> I DELETE /boards/{boardId} <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 (Owner-only action) and the board is not deleted.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am unauthenticated <b>When</b> I DELETE /boards/{boardId} <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated but not a member of the board <b>When</b> I DELETE /boards/{boardId} <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (existence not disclosed).</p><p><b>Given</b> I initiate board deletion via the UI <b>When</b> I click the 'Delete board' action <b>Then</b> a confirmation dialog appears with the board name ('Delete board 'My Project'? This will permanently delete all lists, cards, and members. This action cannot be undone.') with a destructive-confirm button and a cancel button before any request is sent.</p><p><b>Given</b> I confirm deletion <b>When</b> the request is in flight <b>Then</b> the confirm button is disabled/spinner shown, preventing double-submission.</p><p><b>Given</b> deletion succeeds <b>When</b> the response is 204 <b>Then</b> I am navigated away from the (now-deleted) board to the boards list, a role='status' announcement confirms deletion, and the board does not appear in the list.</p><p><b>Given</b> deletion fails (5xx) <b>When</b> the dialog is still open <b>Then</b> an error message is shown within the dialog (role='alert'), the dialog remains open, and the board is not removed from the UI.</p><p><b>Given</b> the confirm dialog and delete action are rendered <b>When</b> used by keyboard or assistive technology <b>Then</b> focus is trapped within the dialog when open, focus returns to a sensible element (boards list heading or first board) on close, and the dialog meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>
```

**Create**
```

The cascade order: members → comments → card labels → card assignees → cards → lists → labels → board. A single transaction must cover the whole cascade.</li><li><b>Destructive action:</b> confirmation dialog mandatory before the DELETE request is sent; no undo.</li><li><b>API:</b> RFC 7807 on every error path; 204 No Content on success (no body).</li><li><b>Clean Architecture:</b> DeleteBoardCommand in Application; cascade persistence in Infrastructure; no EF/Microsoft.* types in Domain.</li><li><b>Real-time:</b> board deletion is propagated to all connected members &lt;1s (via EPIC-6), redirecting them to the boards list — this story does not author SignalR code.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA; ### User Story — STORY-1.7: Current-user endpoint and sign-out
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-1 → <EPIC-1-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-1; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As an authenticated user, I want to retrieve my own profile from the server and sign out of the application, so that the UI can display my identity accurately and I can end my session cleanly on any device.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security / authorization:</b> GET /me is read-only and serves only the authenticated caller's own data (derived from JWT sub / email / name claims — no DB write). 401 for any unauthenticated call.</li><li><b>Stateless JWT:</b> sign-out is <b>client-side only</b> — no token blacklist, no server-side session invalidation. The JWT remains cryptographically valid until its exp claim; this is an accepted trade-off for stateless auth (documented in Out of scope). The client MUST clear the token from all storage locations and clear auth state from Pinia.</li><li><b>No database write on GET /me:</b> the endpoint reads claims from the validated JWT; it does not update LastLoginAt or any other field (that is a future concern).</li><li><b>API:</b> RFC 7807 on every error path; DTO only at the boundary.</li><li><b>Clean Architecture:</b> GetCurrentUserQuery in Application (reads claims from ICurrentUserService); thin endpoint in Api; no EF query needed.</li><li><b>Client route guard:</b> all board/list/card routes are protected; unauthenticated navigation redirects to /login with the original path preserved as a redirect query param.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA on sign-out control and user identity display in header.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Server-side token revocation / blacklist (stateless JWT trade-off — acceptable for v1, noted as future concern).</li><li>'Sign out all devices' / session list (future).</li><li>Profile editing (display name, email, password change) — future.</li><li>Social/OAuth login — deferred (EPIC-0 notes).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I call GET /me <b>Then</b> I receive 200 OK with a user DTO containing my id, display name, and email — derived from the JWT claims without a database write.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am unauthenticated (missing, expired, or invalid token) <b>When</b> I call GET /me <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated and the app header is rendered <b>When</b> the page loads <b>Then</b> my display name (and/or avatar initials) is shown in the header, populated from the GET /me response, before any board-level data loads.</p><p><b>Given</b> I click 'Sign out' in the app <b>When</b> I confirm (or the action has no confirm prompt — sign-out is not destructive) <b>Then</b> my JWT is removed from client storage (localStorage / sessionStorage / cookie), the Pinia auth store is cleared, I am navigated to the login page, and no subsequent API request carries the old token.</p><p><b>Given</b> I sign out <b>When</b> I press the browser back button <b>Then</b> protected routes redirect me to the login page (client-side route guard) and no board data is displayed.</p><p><b>Given</b> the sign-out control is rendered <b>When</b> used by keyboard or assistive technology <b>Then</b> it is reachable by Tab, activatable by Enter/Space, and the resulting navigation to the login page is announced appropriately. WCAG 2.2 AA.</p><p><b>Given</b> GET /me fails (network error or 5xx) <b>When</b> the app header renders <b>Then</b> an error state is shown (e.g. 'Could not load user') and sign-out is still accessible (does not depend on a successful /me response).</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-1.7: Current-user endpoint and sign-out" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-1; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As an authenticated user, I want to retrieve my own profile from the server and sign out of the application, so that the UI can display my identity accurately and I can end my session cleanly on any device.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li><b>Security / authorization:</b> GET /me is read-only and serves only the authenticated caller's own data (derived from JWT sub / email / name claims — no DB write). 401 for any unauthenticated call.</li><li><b>Stateless JWT:</b> sign-out is <b>client-side only</b> — no token blacklist, no server-side session invalidation. The JWT remains cryptographically valid until its exp claim; this is an accepted trade-off for stateless auth (documented in Out of scope). The client MUST clear the token from all storage locations and clear auth state from Pinia.</li><li><b>No database write on GET /me:</b> the endpoint reads claims from the validated JWT; it does not update LastLoginAt or any other field (that is a future concern).</li><li><b>API:</b> RFC 7807 on every error path; DTO only at the boundary.</li><li><b>Clean Architecture:</b> GetCurrentUserQuery in Application (reads claims from ICurrentUserService); thin endpoint in Api; no EF query needed.</li><li><b>Client route guard:</b> all board/list/card routes are protected; unauthenticated navigation redirects to /login with the original path preserved as a redirect query param.</li><li><b>Accessibility:</b> WCAG 2.2 AA on sign-out control and user identity display in header.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Server-side token revocation / blacklist (stateless JWT trade-off — acceptable for v1, noted as future concern).</li><li>'Sign out all devices' / session list (future).</li><li>Profile editing (display name, email, password change) — future.</li><li>Social/OAuth login — deferred (EPIC-0 notes).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I call GET /me <b>Then</b> I receive 200 OK with a user DTO containing my id, display name, and email — derived from the JWT claims without a database write.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am unauthenticated (missing, expired, or invalid token) <b>When</b> I call GET /me <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated and the app header is rendered <b>When</b> the page loads <b>Then</b> my display name (and/or avatar initials) is shown in the header, populated from the GET /me response, before any board-level data loads.</p><p><b>Given</b> I click 'Sign out' in the app <b>When</b> I confirm (or the action has no confirm prompt — sign-out is not destructive) <b>Then</b> my JWT is removed from client storage (localStorage / sessionStorage / cookie), the Pinia auth store is cleared, I am navigated to the login page, and no subsequent API request carries the old token.</p><p><b>Given</b> I sign out <b>When</b> I press the browser back button <b>Then</b> protected routes redirect me to the login page (client-side route guard) and no board data is displayed.</p><p><b>Given</b> the sign-out control is rendered <b>When</b> used by keyboard or assistive technology <b>Then</b> it is reachable by Tab, activatable by Enter/Space, and the resulting navigation to the login page is announced appropriately. WCAG 2.2 AA.</p><p><b>Given</b> GET /me fails (network error or 5xx) <b>When</b> the app header renders <b>Then</b> an error state is shown (e.g. 'Could not load user') and sign-out is still accessible (does not depend on a successful /me response).</p>"
```

**Link to parent**
```
az boards work-item relation add --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --id <this-story-id> --relation-type parent --target-id <EPIC-1-id>
```
### User Story — STORY-2.1: Create a list on a board
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-2 → <EPIC-2-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-2; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As an Editor or Owner of a board, I want to add a named list to the board, so that I can create new columns to organize cards.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Security / authorization: creation is permitted for Owner and Editor only. Status-code convention: 401 unauthenticated; 404 non-member; 403 Viewer; 400 validation.</li><li>Position model: lists carry a double-precision Position column (fractional index). New lists are always appended: rank = max(existing) + 1.0 (or 1.0 for the first list). No 'insert at position' in v1. When gap &lt; 1e-9, background re-normalisation writes integer ranks in one transaction.</li><li>Data: list name is 1–100 characters. A board may have up to 500 lists; returns 400 'list limit reached' if exceeded.</li><li>API: DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li>Clean Architecture (§2.2): List entity in Domain; create-list use-case in Application; EF Core persistence in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li>Real-time: propagation constraint noted; EPIC-6 owns the SignalR story.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Moving cards into the new list (EPIC-3).</li><li>Setting list colour/icon; archiving.</li><li>Real-time delivery story (EPIC-6).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am an Owner or Editor of a board <b>When</b> I POST a list with a valid name (1–100 characters) <b>Then</b> the list is created, appended after the last existing list on the board, assigned a stable fractional-index rank, persisted, and I receive 201 Created with a list DTO (id, boardId, name, rank/position, createdAt). The POST body accepts name only; no position parameter is accepted.</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a blank name or one longer than 100 characters <b>When</b> I create a list <b>Then</b> I receive an RFC 7807 400 validation problem and no list is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an unauthenticated caller <b>When</b> I POST a list <b>Then</b> I receive 401 and no list is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated but not a member of the board <b>When</b> I POST a list <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (existence not disclosed to non-members) and no list is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer of the board <b>When</b> I POST a list <b>Then</b> I receive 403 (member whose role forbids the mutation) and no list is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I create a list <b>When</b> another board member views the board <b>Then</b> real-time propagation &lt; 1 s (via EPIC-6) delivers the new list to connected clients.</p><p><b>Given</b> a board already has 500 lists <b>When</b> I POST a new list <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 ('list limit reached') and no list is created.</p>
```

**Create**
```

Status-code convention: 401 unauthenticated; 404 non-member; 403 Viewer; 400 validation.</li><li>Position model: lists carry a double-precision Position column (fractional index). New lists are always appended: rank = max(existing) + 1.0 (or 1.0 for the first list). No 'insert at position' in v1. When gap &lt; 1e-9, background re-normalisation writes integer ranks in one transaction.</li><li>Data: list name is 1–100 characters. A board may have up to 500 lists; returns 400 'list limit reached' if exceeded.</li><li>API: DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li>Clean Architecture (§2.2): List entity in Domain; create-list use-case in Application; EF Core persistence in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li>Real-time: propagation constraint noted; EPIC-6 owns the SignalR story.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Moving cards into the new list (EPIC-3).</li><li>Setting list colour/icon; archiving.</li><li>Real-time delivery story (EPIC-6).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am an Owner or Editor of a board <b>When</b> I POST a list with a valid name (1–100 characters) <b>Then</b> the list is created, appended after the last existing list on the board, assigned a stable fractional-index rank, persisted, and I receive 201 Created with a list DTO (id, boardId, name, rank/position, createdAt). The POST body accepts name only; no position parameter is accepted.</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a blank name or one longer than 100 characters <b>When</b> I create a list <b>Then</b> I receive an RFC 7807 400 validation problem and no list is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an unauthenticated caller <b>When</b> I POST a list <b>Then</b> I receive 401 and no list is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated but not a member of the board <b>When</b> I POST a list <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (existence not disclosed to non-members) and no list is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer of the board <b>When</b> I POST a list <b>Then</b> I receive 403 (member whose role forbids the mutation) and no list is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I create a list <b>When</b> another board member views the board <b>Then</b> real-time propagation &lt; 1 s (via EPIC-6) delivers the new list to connected clients.</p><p><b>Given</b> a board already has 500 lists <b>When</b> I POST a new list <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 ('list limit reached') and no list is created.</p>"

### User Story — STORY-2.2: Rename a list
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-2 → <EPIC-2-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-2; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As an Editor or Owner of a board, I want to rename an existing list, so that I can keep column labels accurate as the project evolves.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Security / authorization: rename is permitted for Owner and Editor only. Status-code convention: 401 unauthenticated; 404 non-member or list not found; 403 Viewer; 400 validation.</li><li>Idempotency: renaming to the current name is allowed and returns 200 without writing to the DB (the Application layer should short-circuit on no-op).</li><li>Data: list name 1–100 characters, same constraint as creation.</li><li>API: DTOs only; RFC 7807 on every error; updatedAt returned to allow clients to reconcile concurrent edits.</li><li>Clean Architecture (§2.2): rename use-case in Application; no Domain logic beyond the invariant; EF Core update in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li>Real-time: propagation constraint noted; EPIC-6 owns the SignalR story.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Bulk rename; list colour/icon changes.</li><li>Conflict resolution for simultaneous renames (last-write-wins via updatedAt is sufficient in v1).</li><li>Real-time delivery story (EPIC-6).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am an Owner or Editor of a board <b>When</b> I PATCH/PUT a list's name with a valid value (1–100 characters) <b>Then</b> the list is updated and persisted, and I receive 200 OK with the updated list DTO (id, boardId, name, position, updatedAt).</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a blank name or one longer than 100 characters <b>When</b> I rename a list <b>Then</b> I receive an RFC 7807 400 validation problem and the list name is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an unauthenticated caller <b>When</b> I attempt to rename a list <b>Then</b> I receive 401 and the list is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated but not a member of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to rename a list on that board <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (existence not disclosed to non-members) and the list is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to rename a list <b>Then</b> I receive 403 (member whose role forbids the mutation) and the list is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> the list id in the URL does not exist (or belongs to a different board) <b>When</b> I attempt to rename it <b>Then</b> I receive 404 and no change occurs.</p><p><b>Given</b> a list is successfully renamed <b>When</b> another board member views the board <b>Then</b> real-time propagation &lt; 1 s (via EPIC-6) delivers the updated name to connected clients.</p>
```

```

Status-code convention: 401 unauthenticated; 404 non-member or list not found; 403 Viewer; 400 validation.</li><li>Idempotency: renaming to the current name is allowed and returns 200 without writing to the DB (the Application layer should short-circuit on no-op).</li><li>Data: list name 1–100 characters, same constraint as creation.</li><li>API: DTOs only; RFC 7807 on every error; updatedAt returned to allow clients to reconcile concurrent edits.</li><li>Clean Architecture (§2.2): rename use-case in Application; no Domain logic beyond the invariant; EF Core update in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li>Real-time: propagation constraint noted; EPIC-6 owns the SignalR story.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Bulk rename; list colour/icon changes.</li><li>Conflict resolution for simultaneous renames (last-write-wins via updatedAt is sufficient in v1).</li><li>Real-time delivery story (EPIC-6).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am an Owner or Editor of a board <b>When</b> I PATCH/PUT a list's name with a valid value (1–100 characters) <b>Then</b> the list is updated and persisted, and I receive 200 OK with the updated list DTO (id, boardId, name, position, updatedAt).</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a blank name or one longer than 100 characters <b>When</b> I rename a list <b>Then</b> I receive an RFC 7807 400 validation problem and the list name is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an unauthenticated caller <b>When</b> I attempt to rename a list <b>Then</b> I receive 401 and the list is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated but not a member of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to rename a list on that board <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (existence not disclosed to non-members) and the list is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to rename a list <b>Then</b> I receive 403 (member whose role forbids the mutation) and the list is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> the list id in the URL does not exist (or belongs to a different board) <b>When</b> I attempt to rename it <b>Then</b> I receive 404 and no change occurs.</p><p><b>Given</b> a list is successfully renamed <b>When</b> another board member views the board <b>Then</b> real-time propagation &lt; ### User Story — STORY-2.3: Delete a list (and its cards)
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-2 → <EPIC-2-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-2; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As an Editor or Owner of a board, I want to delete a list after confirming the action, so that I can remove columns that are no longer needed, understanding that all cards inside them will also be permanently deleted.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Security / authorization: deletion is permitted for Owner and Editor only. Status-code convention: 401 unauthenticated; 404 non-member or list not found; 403 Viewer; 400 validation.</li><li>Cascade integrity: list + all child cards deleted in one database transaction; if the transaction fails, neither the list nor any cards are deleted. EF Core cascade delete (or explicit bulk delete in Application) — no orphaned rows.</li><li>Default list: the list seeded by STORY-0.3 carries no special flag — it is deletable like any other list.</li><li>Destructive action UX: confirmed before execution; the confirmation message explicitly names card deletion. No 'undo' in v1.</li><li>API: DELETE /boards/{boardId}/lists/{listId}; no request body; 204 on success; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li>Card count source: the board-view list DTO carries a cardCount: int field per list. The confirmation dialog uses this client-side value — no separate count endpoint is called.</li><li>Clean Architecture (§2.2): delete-list use-case in Application (deletes list + cards in one transaction); EF Core in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li>Real-time: propagation constraint noted; EPIC-6 owns the SignalR story.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Archiving lists (hide without deleting cards).</li><li>Soft-delete / undo / recycle bin.</li><li>Bulk deletion of multiple lists.</li><li>Real-time delivery story (EPIC-6).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am an Owner or Editor of a board <b>When</b> I confirm and DELETE a list <b>Then</b> the list and all of its cards are permanently deleted in a single transaction, and I receive 204 No Content.</p><p><b>Given</b> I delete a list that contains one or more cards <b>When</b> the deletion succeeds <b>Then</b> no orphaned cards remain in the database — the cascade is verified by a subsequent GET returning empty for that list's former listId.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an unauthenticated caller <b>When</b> I attempt to delete a list <b>Then</b> I receive 401 and the list is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated but not a member of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to delete a list <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (existence not disclosed to non-members) and the list is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to delete a list <b>Then</b> I receive 403 (member whose role forbids the mutation) and the list is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> the list id does not exist or belongs to a different board <b>When</b> I attempt to delete it <b>Then</b> I receive 404 and no change occurs.</p><p><b>Given</b> the UI <b>When</b> I initiate deletion of a list <b>Then</b> a confirmation dialog warns me that all cards in the list will also be permanently deleted, displaying the card count N from the list DTO's cardCount field, and deletion only proceeds on explicit confirmation.</p><p><b>Given</b> a list is successfully deleted <b>When</b> another board member views the board <b>Then</b> real-time propagation &lt; 1 s (via EPIC-6) removes the list and its cards from connected clients' views.</p><p><b>Given</b> the board has only the default seeded list from EPIC-0 <b>When</b> I delete it <b>Then</b> the deletion succeeds (there is no minimum-list invariant in v1) and the board becomes empty.</p>
```

**Create**
```

Status-code convention: 401 unauthenticated; 404 non-member or list not found; 403 Viewer; 400 validation.</li><li>Cascade integrity: list + all child cards deleted in one database transaction; if the transaction fails, neither the list nor any cards are deleted. EF Core cascade delete (or explicit bulk delete in Application) — no orphaned rows.</li><li>Default list: the list seeded by STORY-0.3 carries no special flag — it is deletable like any other list.</li><li>Destructive action UX: confirmed before execution; the confirmation message explicitly names card deletion. No 'undo' in v1.</li><li>API: DELETE /boards/{boardId}/lists/{listId}; no request body; 204 on success; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li>Card count source: the board-view list DTO carries a cardCount: int field per list. The confirmation dialog uses this client-side value — no separate count endpoint is called.</li><li>Clean Architecture (§2.2): delete-list use-case in Application (deletes list + cards in one transaction); EF Core in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li>Real-time: propagation constraint noted; EPIC-6 owns the SignalR story.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Archiving lists (hide without deleting cards).</li><li>Soft-delete / undo / recycle bin.</li><li>Bulk deletion of multiple lists.</li><li>Real-time delivery story (EPIC-6).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am an Owner or Editor of a board <b>When</b> I confirm and DELETE a list <b>Then</b> the list and all of its cards are cards remain in the database — the cascade is verified by a subsequent GET returning empty for that list's former listId.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an unauthenticated caller <b>When</b> I attempt to (existence not disclosed to non-members) and the list is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to delete a list <b>Then</b> I receive 403 (member whose role change occurs.</p><p><b>Given</b> the UI <b>When</b> I initiate deletion of a list <b>Then</b> a confirmation dialog warns me that all cards in the list will also be permanently deleted, displaying the card count N from the list DTO's cardCount field, and deletion only proceeds on explicit confirmation.</p><p><b>Given</b> a list is successfully deleted <b>When</b> another board member views the board <b>Then</b> real-time propagation &lt; 1 s (via EPIC-6) removes the list and its cards from connected clients' views.</p><p><b>Given</b> the board has only the default seeded list from EPIC-0 <b>When</b> I delete it <b>Then</b> the deletion succeeds (there is no minimum-list invariant in v1) and the board becomes empty.</p>"

### User Story — STORY-2.4: Reorder lists on a board
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-2 → <EPIC-2-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-2; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As an Editor or Owner of a board, I want to drag and drop lists into a new order, so that I can arrange columns to reflect my workflow without losing any other data.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Position model (canonical): each list carries a double-precision Position column. Insertion between predecessor p and successor s writes (p + s) / 2. Appending writes max + 1.0. Prepending writes min - 1.0. When insertion gap &lt; 1e-9, the Application layer re-normalises all positions for the board to integers in the same transaction. This model ensures at most one row written per reorder under normal conditions.</li><li>Concurrency: PATCH /boards/{boardId}/lists/{listId}/position is a single-row update. Concurrent reorders of different lists are serialisable without conflict. Concurrent reorders of the same list: last-write-wins (acceptable for v1).</li><li>API shape: PATCH /boards/{boardId}/lists/{listId}/position with body { 'afterListId': '&lt;guid | null&gt;' } — null means move to first position. Returns 200 OK with the updated list DTO.</li><li>Security / authorization: reorder is permitted for Owner and Editor only. Status-code convention: 401 unauthenticated; 404 non-member, list not found, or afterListId not found/belongs to different board; 403 Viewer; 400 validation.</li><li>Keyboard / accessibility: a keyboard-accessible reorder mechanism is required for WCAG 2.2 AA (e.g. 'Move left' / 'Move right' menu items, or arrow-key handling).</li><li>Clean Architecture (§2.2): reorder use-case in Application; Domain entity validates position bounds; EF Core single-row update in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li>Real-time: propagation constraint noted; EPIC-6 owns the SignalR story.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Card reorder / DnD (EPIC-3).</li><li>Multi-list selection and batch reorder.</li><li>Animated transitions beyond the drag placeholder.</li><li>Real-time delivery story (EPIC-6).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am an Owner or Editor of a board <b>When</b> I drag a list to a new position and drop it <b>Then</b> the list's rank is updated server-side, the board's visible column order reflects the new position immediately, and I receive 200 OK with the moved list's updated DTO (id, boardId, name, position).</p><p><b>Given</b> I drag a list to between two adjacent lists <b>When</b> the reorder is persisted <b>Then</b> only the moved list's position column changes — no other rows are rewritten — satisfying the concurrency-safe, minimal-write requirement.</p><p><b>Given</b> I drag a list to the first position <b>When</b> the reorder is persisted <b>Then</b> the moved list's rank is lower than all others on the board.</p><p><b>Given</b> I drag a list to the last position <b>When</b> the reorder is persisted <b>Then</b> the moved list's rank is higher than all others on the board.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an unauthenticated caller <b>When</b> I attempt to reorder a list <b>Then</b> I receive 401 and no list is moved.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated but not a member of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to reorder a list <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (existence not disclosed to non-members) and no list is moved.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to reorder a list <b>Then</b> I receive 403 (member whose role forbids the mutation) and no list is moved.</p><p><b>Given</b> two users reorder different lists concurrently <b>When</b> both writes land <b>Then</b> both are accepted (no error) and the resulting order is consistent — each list's final rank reflects both moves without a lost-update anomaly.</p><p><b>Given</b> the gap between two neighbouring ranks falls below 1e-9 <b>When</b> a reorder would need to insert between them <b>Then</b> the Application layer re-normalises all list ranks for the board (integer 1, 2, 3 …) in the same transaction before writing the target rank, so no error surfaces to the caller.</p><p><b>Given</b> a reorder succeeds <b>When</b> another board member views the board <b>Then</b> real-time propagation &lt; 1 s (via EPIC-6) updates the column order for connected clients.</p><p><b>Given</b> the drag begins <b>When</b> the user releases outside a valid drop target (or presses Esc) <b>Then</b> the list snaps back to its original position and no server call is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> an afterListId that belongs to a different board or does not exist <b>When</b> I PATCH the position <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (existence not disclosed) and the position is unchanged.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-2.4: Reorder lists on a board" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-2; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As an Editor or Owner of a board, I want to drag and drop lists into a new order, so that I can arrange columns to reflect my workflow without losing any other data.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Position model (canonical): each list carries a double-precision Position column. Insertion between predecessor p and successor s writes (p + s) / 2. Appending writes max + 1.0. Prepending writes min - 1.0. When insertion gap &lt; 1e-9, the Application layer re-normalises all positions for the board to integers in the same transaction. This model ensures at most one row written per reorder under normal conditions.</li><li>Concurrency: PATCH /boards/{boardId}/lists/{listId}/position is a single-row update. Concurrent reorders of different lists are serialisable without conflict. Concurrent reorders of the same list: last-write-wins (acceptable for v1).</li><li>API shape: PATCH /boards/{boardId}/lists/{listId}/position with body { 'afterListId': '&lt;guid | null&gt;' } — null means move to first position. Returns 200 OK with the updated list DTO.</li><li>Security / authorization: reorder is permitted for Owner and Editor only. Status-code convention: 401 unauthenticated; 404 non-member, list not found, or afterListId not found/belongs to different board; 403 Viewer; 400 validation.</li><li>Keyboard / accessibility: a keyboard-accessible reorder mechanism is required for WCAG 2.2 AA (e.g. 'Move left' / 'Move right' menu items, or arrow-key handling).</li><li>Clean Architecture (§2.2): reorder use-case in Application; Domain entity validates position bounds; EF Core single-row update in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li>Real-time: propagation constraint noted; EPIC-6 owns the SignalR story.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Card reorder / DnD (EPIC-3).</li><li>Multi-list selection and batch reorder.</li><li>Animated transitions beyond the drag placeholder.</li><li>Real-time delivery story (EPIC-6).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am an Owner or Editor of a board <b>When</b> I drag a list to a new position and drop it <b>Then</b> the list's rank is updated server-side, the board's visible column order reflects the new position immediately, and I receive 200 OK with the moved list's updated DTO (id, boardId, name, position).</p><p><b>Given</b> I drag a list to between two adjacent lists <b>When</b> the reorder is persisted <b>Then</b> only the moved list's position column changes — no other rows are rewritten — satisfying the concurrency-safe, minimal-write requirement.</p><p><b>Given</b> I drag a list to the first position <b>When</b> the reorder is persisted <b>Then</b> the moved list's rank is lower than all others on the board.</p><p><b>Given</b> I drag a list to the last position <b>When</b> the reorder is persisted <b>Then</b> the moved list's rank is higher than all others on the board.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an unauthenticated caller <b>When</b> I attempt to reorder a list <b>Then</b> I receive 401 and no list is moved.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated but not a member of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to reorder a list <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (existence not disclosed to non-members) and no list is moved.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to reorder a list <b>Then</b> I receive 403 (member whose role forbids the mutation) and no list is moved.</p><p><b>Given</b> two users reorder different lists concurrently <b>When</b> both writes land <b>Then</b> both are accepted (no error) and the resulting order is consistent — each list's final rank reflects both moves without a lost-update anomaly.</p><p><b>Given</b> the gap between two neighbouring ranks falls below 1e-9 <b>When</b> a reorder would need to insert between them <b>Then</b> the Application layer re-normalises all list ranks for the board (integer 1, 2, 3 …) in the same transaction before writing the target rank, so no error surfaces to the caller.</p><p><b>Given</b> a reorder succeeds <b>When</b> another board member views the board <b>Then</b> real-time propagation &lt; 1 s (via EPIC-6) updates the column order for connected clients.</p><p><b>Given</b> the drag begins <b>When</b> the user releases outside a valid drop target (or presses Esc) <b>Then</b> the list snaps back to its original position and no server call is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> an afterListId that belongs to a different board or does not exist <b>When</b> I PATCH the position <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (existence not disclosed) and the position is unchanged.</p>"
```

**Link to parent**
```
az boards work-item relation add --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --id <this-story-id> --relation-type parent --target-id <EPIC-2-id>
```

### User Story — STORY-2.5: View a board's lists in order
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-2 → <EPIC-2-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-2; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As any board member (Owner, Editor, or Viewer), I want to see the board's lists rendered in their correct order when I open the board, so that I can navigate the board's column layout and find the right place to work.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Pagination: the endpoint uses the shared offset-based envelope — page (1-indexed, default 1), pageSize (default 20, max 100), response { items, page, pageSize, total }. The client SHOULD request page 1 with a generous pageSize (e.g. 50) on initial load. No server-side streaming.</li><li>Ordering: SQL ORDER BY Position ASC in the query; ties broken by CreatedAt ASC (deterministic).</li><li>Security / authorization: any authenticated member (Owner, Editor, Viewer) may read; non-member → 404; unauthenticated → 401. No 403 is reachable on a GET.</li><li>Performance (§1.6): the board (~200 cards spread across lists) must load in &lt; 1.5 s. This endpoint returns lists only (no nested cards). The lists query should be fast: indexed on (BoardId, Position).</li><li>API: GET /boards/{boardId}/lists?page=1&amp;pageSize=50; DTOs only; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li>Clean Architecture (§2.2): list-query use-case in Application (returns paginated DTO); EF Core read in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Fetching cards nested inside the list response (separate card endpoint, EPIC-3).</li><li>Infinite scroll / virtual scrolling of lists (500-list cap means pagination is a safety valve, not a UX flow).</li><li>Filtering or sorting lists by attributes other than position.</li><li>Real-time delivery of list additions/reorders to connected clients (EPIC-6).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am a member of a board (any role) <b>When</b> I GET the board's lists <b>Then</b> I receive the lists sorted ascending by position (rank), with each list DTO containing at minimum: id, boardId, name, position, createdAt.</p><p><b>Given</b> the board has no lists <b>When</b> I GET the board's lists <b>Then</b> I receive an empty items array with total: 0 and the paginated envelope is still present.</p><p><b>Given</b> the board has lists that have been reordered (STORY-2.4) <b>When</b> I GET the board's lists <b>Then</b> the order matches the persisted rank order — reorder correctness is verified here end-to-end.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an unauthenticated caller <b>When</b> I GET a board's lists <b>Then</b> I receive 401.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated but not a member of the board <b>When</b> I GET its lists <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (existence not disclosed to non-members).</p><p><b>Given</b> the board view is loading <b>When</b> the API call is in flight <b>Then</b> placeholder skeleton columns are shown (not a blank screen).</p><p><b>Given</b> the board has no lists yet <b>When</b> the empty state is displayed <b>Then</b> an empty-state message ('No lists yet — add your first') is shown and an 'Add list' affordance (Owner/Editor) or a read-only notice (Viewer) is visible.</p><p><b>Given</b> the API call fails <b>When</b> the board view renders <b>Then</b> an error state with a retry option is shown and the error is announced via role='alert'.</p><p><b>Given</b> the board view meets WCAG 2.2 AA <b>Then</b> list columns are navigable by keyboard, column names are labelled, loading states are announced via aria-live, and colour is not the sole differentiator for any state.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-2.5: View a board's lists in order" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-2; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As any board member (Owner, Editor, or Viewer), I want to see the board's lists rendered in their correct order when I open the board, so that I can navigate the board's column layout and find the right place to work.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Pagination: the endpoint uses the shared offset-based envelope — page (1-indexed, default 1), pageSize (default 20, max 100), response { items, page, pageSize, total }. The client SHOULD request page 1 with a generous pageSize (e.g. 50) on initial load. No server-side streaming.</li><li>Ordering: SQL ORDER BY Position ASC in the query; ties broken by CreatedAt ASC (deterministic).</li><li>Security / authorization: any authenticated member (Owner, Editor, Viewer) may read; non-member → 404; unauthenticated → 401. No 403 is reachable on a GET.</li><li>Performance (§1.6): the board (~200 cards spread across lists) must load in &lt; 1.5 s. This endpoint returns lists only (no nested cards). list response (separate card endpoint, EPIC-3).</li><li>Infinite scroll / virtual scrolling of lists (500-list cap means pagination is a safety valve, not a UX flow).</li><li>Filtering or sorting lists by attributes other than position.</li><li>Real-time delivery of list additions/reorders to connected clients (EPIC-6).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am a member of a board (any role) <b>When</b> I GET the board's lists <b>Then</b> I receive the lists sorted ascending by position (rank), view is loading <b>When</b> the API call is in flight <b>Then</b> placeholder skeleton columns are shown (not a blank screen).</p><p><b>Given</b> the board has no lists yet <b>When</b> the empty state is displayed <b>Then</b> an empty-state message ('No lists yet — add your first') is shown and an 'Add list' affordance (Owner/Editor) or a read-only notice (Viewer) is visible.</p><p><b>Given</b> the AA <b>Then</b> list columns are navigable by keyboard, column names are labelled, loading states are announced via aria-live, and colour is not the sole differentiator for any state.</p>"

### User Story — STORY-3.1: View card details
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-3 → <EPIC-3-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-3; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a board member (any role), I want to open a card and see its title, description, and the list and board it belongs to, so that I can understand the full context of the task.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>API response is a DTO only at the boundary (no domain or EF types leak).</li><li>Server-side authorization: membership is checked before any card data is returned.</li><li>No separate list-of-cards endpoint is added here — that is already covered by EPIC-2 (list cards) and EPIC-0 (board card feed, paginated). This story adds only the single-card detail endpoint.</li><li>Real-time propagation of card edits made by others is a constraint: changes made by a concurrent user will not appear until the user reopens the card or a SignalR push arrives (EPIC-6 concern — not authored here).</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Editing or deleting the card (STORY-3.2, STORY-3.3).</li><li>Card metadata: labels, assignees, due dates, priorities (EPIC-4).</li><li>Comments section (EPIC-5).</li><li>Activity log within the card (EPIC-7).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am an authenticated member of the board (Owner, Editor, or Viewer) <b>When</b> I GET /cards/{cardId} <b>Then</b> I receive 200 OK with a card DTO containing: id, title, description (nullable), listId, listName, boardId, boardName, rank, createdAt, updatedAt.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board that owns the card, or I present no or an invalid JWT <b>When</b> I GET /cards/{cardId} <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (non-member — existence not disclosed) or 401 (unauthenticated), respectively.</p><p><b>Given</b> cardId does not exist <b>When</b> I request it <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 — indistinguishable from the non-member 404 (no information disclosure).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board member <b>When</b> I open the card detail view in the UI <b>Then</b> the panel/modal displays: card title, description (or placeholder if empty), the containing list name, and the board name. Loading, empty-description, and error states are all shown correctly. The view is read-only for Viewers.</p><p><b>Given</b> the card detail view loads <b>When</b> it renders <b>Then</b> it meets WCAG 2.2 AA: heading hierarchy correct, focus moves into the panel on open, Esc closes it, all interactive controls are keyboard-accessible with visible focus indicators.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-3.1: View card details" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-3; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As a board member (any role), I want to open a card and see its title, description, and the list and board it belongs to, so that I can understand the full context of the task.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>API response is a DTO only at the boundary (no domain or EF types leak).</li><li>Server-side authorization: membership is checked before any card data is returned.</li><li>No separate list-of-cards endpoint is added here — that is already covered by EPIC-2 (list cards) and EPIC-0 (board card feed, paginated). This story adds only the single-card detail endpoint.</li><li>Real-time propagation of card edits made by others is a constraint: changes made by a concurrent user will not appear until the user reopens the card or a SignalR push arrives (EPIC-6 concern — not authored here).</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Editing or deleting the card (STORY-3.2, STORY-3.3).</li><li>Card metadata: labels, assignees, due dates, priorities (EPIC-4).</li><li>Comments section (EPIC-5).</li><li>Activity log within the card (EPIC-7).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am an authenticated member of the board (Owner, Editor, or Viewer) <b>When</b> I GET /cards/{cardId} <b>Then</b> I receive 200 OK with a card DTO containing: id, title, description (nullable), listId, listName, boardId, boardName, rank, createdAt, updatedAt.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board that owns the card, or I present no or an invalid JWT <b>When</b> I GET /cards/{cardId} <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (non-member — existence not disclosed) or 401 (unauthenticated), respectively.</p><p><b>Given</b> cardId does not exist <b>When</b> I request it <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 — indistinguishable from the non-member 404 (no information disclosure).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a board member <b>When</b> I open the card detail view in the UI <b>Then</b> the panel/modal displays: card title, description (or placeholder if empty), the containing list name, and the board name. Loading, empty-description, and error states are all shown correctly. The view is read-only for Viewers.</p><p><b>Given</b> the card detail view loads <b>When</b> it renders <b>Then</b> it meets WCAG 2.2 AA: heading hierarchy correct, focus moves into the panel on open, Esc closes it, all interactive controls are keyboard-accessible with visible focus indicators.</p>"

### User Story — STORY-3.2: Edit a card (title and description)
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-3 → <EPIC-3-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-3; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As an Editor or Owner of a board, I want to edit a card's title and description, so that I can keep the task information accurate as work evolves.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Authorization: Editor and Owner may edit; Viewer receives 403. Checked server-side on every request.</li><li>Data bounds: title 1–255 chars (consistent with EPIC-0 domain entity and EF column constraint); description 0–4000 chars (nullable; null in the PATCH payload explicitly clears the field). Both enforced in Domain, EF column, and client validation.</li><li>Partial update: PATCH semantics — only fields present in the payload are updated; omitting title retains the existing title; omitting description retains the existing description; sending 'description': null clears it.</li><li>Concurrency: updatedAt is updated on every successful write. No optimistic-concurrency ETag required in this story; last-write-wins is acceptable.</li><li>Real-time: other board members' UIs will not reflect this edit in real time until EPIC-6 is in place — noted as a constraint.</li><li>DTOs only at the API boundary; RFC 7807 on all error paths; structured logging of edit events.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Moving or reordering the card (STORY-3.4, STORY-3.5).</li><li>Card metadata fields: labels, assignees, due dates, priorities (EPIC-4).</li><li>Optimistic-concurrency conflict detection (deferred).</li><li>Rich-text / markdown rendering in the description (deferred — plain text only in v1).</li><li>Auto-save on blur (deferred — v1 uses explicit Save only).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am an authenticated Editor or Owner of the board <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId} with a valid title (1–255 chars) and/or an optional description (0–4000 chars, or explicit null to clear it) <b>Then</b> the card is updated in the database, I receive 200 OK with the full updated card DTO (id, title, description, listId, boardId, updatedAt), and updatedAt is refreshed.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner with unsaved edits in the card edit form <b>When</b> I click the explicit Save button <b>Then</b> client-side validation fires, and on passing, the PATCH is submitted; on Cancel the form closes and unsaved edits are discarded.</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a blank title, a title longer than 255 characters, or a description longer than 4000 characters <b>When</b> I PATCH the card <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with field-level validation errors and the card is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer on the board <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId} <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 and the card is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board, or present no/invalid JWT <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId} <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member — existence not disclosed) or 401 (unauthenticated) and the card is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner editing a card <b>When</b> I submit the edit form in the UI <b>Then</b> the card detail shows the updated title and description immediately after save, with a loading/submitting state during the request and an inline error banner if the request fails.</p><p><b>Given</b> the edit form renders <b>When</b> viewed by a Viewer <b>Then</b> all inputs are disabled or the edit controls are hidden — Viewer cannot initiate an edit in the UI.</p><p><b>Given</b> the edit form is displayed <b>When</b> rendered <b>Then</b> it meets WCAG 2.2 AA: labels associated with inputs, inline validation errors announced via aria-live, visible focus indicators.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-3.2: Edit a card (title and description)" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-3; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As an Editor or Owner of a board, I want to edit a card's title and description, so that I can keep the task information accurate as work evolves.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Authorization: Editor and Owner may edit; Viewer receives 403. Checked server-side on every request.</li><li>Data bounds: title 1–255 chars (consistent with EPIC-0 domain entity and EF column constraint); description 0–4000 chars (nullable; null in the PATCH payload explicitly clears the field). Both enforced in Domain, EF column, and client validation.</li><li>Partial update: PATCH semantics — only fields present in the payload are updated; omitting title retains the existing title; omitting description retains the existing description; sending 'description': null clears it.</li><li>Concurrency: updatedAt is updated on every successful write. No optimistic-concurrency ETag required in this story; last-write-wins is acceptable.</li><li>Real-time: other board members' UIs will not reflect this edit in real time until EPIC-6 is in place — noted as a constraint.</li><li>DTOs only at the API boundary; RFC 7807 on all error paths; structured logging of edit events.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Moving or reordering the card (STORY-3.4, STORY-3.5).</li><li>Card metadata fields: labels, assignees, due dates, priorities (EPIC-4).</li><li>Optimistic-concurrency conflict detection (deferred).</li><li>Rich-text / markdown rendering in the description (deferred — plain text only in v1).</li><li>Auto-save on blur (deferred — v1 uses explicit Save only).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am an authenticated Editor or Owner of the board <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId} with a valid title (1–255 chars) and/or an optional description (0–4000 chars, or explicit null to clear it) <b>Then</b> the card is updated in the database, I receive 200 OK with the full updated card DTO (id, title, description, listId, boardId, updatedAt), and updatedAt is refreshed.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner with unsaved edits in the card edit form <b>When</b> I click the explicit Save button <b>Then</b> client-side validation fires, and on passing, the PATCH is submitted; on Cancel the form closes and unsaved edits are discarded.</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a blank title, a title longer than 255 characters, or a description longer than 4000 characters <b>When</b> I PATCH the card <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with field-level validation errors and the card is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer on the board <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId} <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 and the card is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board, or present no/invalid JWT <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId} <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member — existence not disclosed) or 401 (unauthenticated) and the card is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner editing a card <b>When</b> I submit the edit form in the UI <b>Then</b> the card detail shows the updated title and description immediately after save, with a loading/submitting state during the request and an inline error banner if the request fails.</p><p><b>Given</b> the edit form renders <b>When</b> viewed by a Viewer <b>Then</b> all inputs are disabled or the edit controls are hidden — Viewer cannot initiate an edit in the UI.</p><p><b>Given</b> the edit form is displayed <b>When</b> rendered <b>Then</b> it meets WCAG 2.2 AA: labels associated with inputs, inline validation errors announced via aria-live, visible focus indicators.</p>"
```
