### User Story — STORY-3.3: Delete a card
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-3 → <EPIC-3-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-3; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As an Editor or Owner of a board, I want to delete a card after confirming the action, so that I can remove tasks that are no longer relevant without accidentally losing work.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Authorization: Editor and Owner may delete; Viewer receives 403. Enforced server-side on every request.</li><li>Destructive action: confirmed in the UI before the DELETE is issued. The confirmation prompt states the card title so the user has enough context to decide.</li><li>Cascade: deleting a card removes it and any future child entities (comments — EPIC-5; activity entries — EPIC-7) via EF cascade delete. This story defines the cascade contract; child tables do not yet exist in EPIC-3 but the delete endpoint must be forward-compatible (cascade configured on the migration, not ad-hoc).</li><li>Real-time: other board members' UIs will not reflect the deletion in real time until EPIC-6 broadcasts the event — noted as a constraint.</li><li>204 No Content on success (no body); RFC 7807 on all error paths.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Soft-delete / archive / restore (deferred — v1 is hard delete only).</li><li>Bulk delete (deferred).</li><li>Deleting a list or board (separate features in EPIC-2 / Boards epic).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am an authenticated Editor or Owner of the board <b>When</b> I DELETE /cards/{cardId} <b>Then</b> the card is permanently removed from the database, I receive 204 No Content, and the card no longer appears in any list-cards response.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer on the board <b>When</b> I DELETE /cards/{cardId} <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 and the card remains in the database.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board, or present no/invalid JWT <b>When</b> I DELETE /cards/{cardId} <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member — existence not disclosed) or 401 (unauthenticated) and the card is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> cardId does not exist <b>When</b> DELETE is requested <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 — indistinguishable from the non-member 404.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner viewing a card <b>When</b> I trigger delete in the UI <b>Then</b> a confirmation dialog appears describing what will be deleted (card title) with explicit Cancel and Delete actions. Dismissing or pressing Esc cancels without any change.</p><p><b>Given</b> I confirm deletion in the UI <b>When</b> the DELETE request succeeds <b>Then</b> the card is removed from the board/list view immediately (optimistic or server-confirmed removal — design TBD), and focus returns to the list column it belonged to.</p><p><b>Given</b> the confirmation dialog or delete button renders <b>When</b> viewed by a Viewer <b>Then</b> the delete control is not shown or is disabled — Viewers cannot reach the confirmation step.</p><p><b>Given</b> the confirmation dialog is displayed <b>When</b> rendered <b>Then</b> it meets WCAG 2.2 AA: role='alertdialog', aria-modal='true', aria-labelledby, focus moves into the dialog on open, focus is trapped within it, Esc cancels.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-3.3: Delete a card" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-3; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As an Editor or Owner of a board, I want to delete a card after confirming the action, so that I can remove tasks that are no longer relevant without accidentally losing work.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Authorization: Editor and Owner may delete; Viewer receives 403. Enforced server-side on every request.</li><li>Destructive action: confirmed in the UI before the DELETE is issued. The confirmation prompt states the card title so the user has enough context to decide.</li><li>Cascade: deleting a card removes it and any future child entities (comments — EPIC-5; activity entries — EPIC-7) via EF cascade delete. This story defines the cascade contract; child tables do not yet exist in EPIC-3 but the delete endpoint must be forward-compatible (cascade configured on the migration, not ad-hoc).</li><li>Real-time: other board members' UIs will not reflect the deletion in real time until EPIC-6 broadcasts the event — noted as a constraint.</li><li>204 No Content on success (no body); RFC 7807 on all error paths.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Soft-delete / archive / restore (deferred — v1 is hard delete only).</li><li>Bulk delete (deferred).</li><li>Deleting a list or board (separate features in EPIC-2 / Boards epic).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am an authenticated Editor or Owner of the board <b>When</b> I DELETE /cards/{cardId} <b>Then</b> the card is permanently removed from the database, I receive 204 No Content, and the card no longer appears in any list-cards response.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer on the board <b>When</b> I DELETE /cards/{cardId} <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 and the card remains in the database.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board, or present no/invalid JWT <b>When</b> I DELETE /cards/{cardId} <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member — existence not disclosed) or 401 (unauthenticated) and the card is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> cardId does not exist <b>When</b> DELETE is requested <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 — indistinguishable from the non-member 404.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner viewing a card <b>When</b> I trigger delete in the UI <b>Then</b> a confirmation dialog appears describing what will be deleted (card title) with explicit Cancel and Delete actions. Dismissing or pressing Esc cancels without any change.</p><p><b>Given</b> I confirm deletion in the UI <b>When</b> the DELETE request succeeds <b>Then</b> the card is removed from the board/list view immediately (optimistic or server-confirmed removal — design TBD), and focus returns to the list column it belonged to.</p><p><b>Given</b> the confirmation dialog or delete button renders <b>When</b> viewed by a Viewer <b>Then</b> the delete control is not shown or is disabled — Viewers cannot reach the confirmation step.</p><p><b>Given</b> the confirmation dialog is displayed <b>When</b> rendered <b>Then</b> it meets WCAG 2.2 AA: role='alertdialog', aria-modal='true', aria-labelledby, focus moves into the dialog on open, focus is trapped within it, Esc cancels.</p>"
```

### User Story — STORY-3.4: Move a card to another list on the same board
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-3 → <EPIC-3-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-3; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As an Editor or Owner of a board, I want to move a card from one list to another list on the same board, so that I can reflect a change in the task's status or workflow stage.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Authorization: Editor and Owner may move; Viewer receives 403. Enforced server-side.</li><li>IDOR / cross-board guard: targetListId is validated to belong to the same board as the card before any write. Any targetListId that does not exist within this card's board — whether the list does not exist at all or belongs to another board — returns a single generic 404 RFC 7807 response. The two cases are merged so that list existence on other boards is never disclosed. 400 is NOT used for this guard; 404 is the correct status per the shared convention.</li><li>Ordering model: on move, the card's rank is computed as the midpoint between afterCardId.rank and the next card's rank (or afterCardId.rank + 1.0 if no next card, or 1.0 if the target list is empty). If the midpoint gap falls below epsilon, the list's ranks are renumbered in the same transaction.</li><li>Atomicity: the listId update and rank update occur in a single database transaction.</li><li>Real-time: other board members will not see the move until EPIC-6 broadcasts a card.moved event — noted as a constraint.</li><li>Response: 200 OK with updated card DTO on success; RFC 7807 on all error paths; structured logging of the move event (fromListId, toListId, cardId).</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Moving a card to a list on a different board (server returns 404 per non-disclosure convention — not a UX flow).</li><li>Moving multiple cards at once (deferred).</li><li>Reordering within the same list using this endpoint (use STORY-3.5 for within-list reorder).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am an authenticated Editor or Owner of the board <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/move with a valid targetListId and an optional afterCardId (position hint) <b>Then</b> the card's listId is updated to targetListId, its rank is set to place it immediately after afterCardId (or appended at the end if afterCardId is omitted or null), I receive 200 OK with the updated card DTO (id, title, listId, rank, updatedAt).</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a targetListId that belongs to a different board than the card, or a targetListId that does not exist <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/move <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 with a generic message (existence of the list is not disclosed — cross-board and not-found cases return the same response) and the card is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply an afterCardId that does not belong to targetListId <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/move <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a descriptive error and the card is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a targetListId that is the same as the card's current list with no afterCardId <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/move <b>Then</b> the card is appended to the end of the list (treated as a no-op reorder, not rejected); I receive 200 OK.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer on the board <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/move <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 and the card is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board, or present no/invalid JWT <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/move <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member — existence not disclosed) or 401 (unauthenticated) and the card is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I move a card in the board UI (drag from one list column to another, or use an explicit 'Move to list' control) <b>When</b> the move is confirmed <b>Then</b> the card disappears from the source column and appears in the target column at the chosen position. Loading/error states are shown; on error the card snaps back to its original position.</p><p><b>Given</b> the move UI renders <b>When</b> viewed by a Viewer <b>Then</b> the move affordance is not present or is disabled.</p><p><b>Given</b> the move UI is displayed <b>When</b> rendered <b>Then</b> it meets WCAG 2.2 AA: all interactive controls are keyboard-accessible, selection of target list is announced to assistive technology, visible focus indicators present.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-3.4: Move a card to another list on the same board" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-3; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As an Editor or Owner of a board, I want to move a card from one list to another list on the same board, so that I can reflect a change in the task's status or workflow stage.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Authorization: Editor and Owner may move; Viewer receives 403. Enforced server-side.</li><li>IDOR / cross-board guard: targetListId is validated to belong to the same board as the card before any write. Any targetListId that does not exist within this card's board — whether the list does not exist at all or belongs to another board — returns a single generic 404 RFC 7807 response. The two cases are merged so that list existence on other boards is never disclosed. 400 is NOT used for this guard; 404 is the correct status per the shared convention.</li><li>Ordering model: on move, the card's rank is computed as the midpoint between afterCardId.rank and the next card's rank (or afterCardId.rank + 1.0 if no next card, or 1.0 if the target list is empty). If the midpoint gap falls below epsilon, the list's ranks are renumbered in the same transaction.</li><li>Atomicity: the listId update and rank update occur in a single database transaction.</li><li>Real-time: other board members will not see the move until EPIC-6 broadcasts a card.moved event — noted as a constraint.</li><li>Response: 200 OK with updated card DTO on success; RFC 7807 on all error paths; structured logging of the move event (fromListId, toListId, cardId).</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Moving a card to a list on a different board (server returns 404 per non-disclosure convention — not a UX flow).</li><li>Moving multiple cards at once (deferred).</li><li>Reordering within the same list using this endpoint (use STORY-3.5 for within-list reorder).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am an authenticated Editor or Owner of the board <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/move with a valid targetListId and an optional afterCardId (position hint) <b>Then</b> the card's listId is updated to targetListId, its rank is set to place it immediately after afterCardId (or appended at the end if afterCardId is omitted or null), I receive 200 OK with the updated card DTO (id, title, listId, rank, updatedAt).</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a targetListId that belongs to a different board than the card, or a targetListId that does not exist <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/move <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 with a generic message (existence of the list is not disclosed — cross-board and not-found cases return the same response) and the card is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply an afterCardId that does not belong to targetListId <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/move <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a descriptive error and the card is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a targetListId that is the same as the card's current list with no afterCardId <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/move <b>Then</b> the card is appended to the end of the list (treated as a no-op reorder, not rejected); I receive 200 OK.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer on the board <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/move <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 and the card is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board, or present no/invalid JWT <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/move <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member — existence not disclosed) or 401 (unauthenticated) and the card is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I move a card in the board UI (drag from one list column to another, or use an explicit 'Move to list' control) <b>When</b> the move is confirmed <b>Then</b> the card disappears from the source column and appears in the target column at the chosen position. Loading/error states are shown; on error the card snaps back to its original position.</p><p><b>Given</b> the move UI renders <b>When</b> viewed by a Viewer <b>Then</b> the move affordance is not present or is disabled.</p><p><b>Given</b> the move UI is displayed <b>When</b> rendered <b>Then</b> it meets WCAG 2.2 AA: all interactive controls are keyboard-accessible, selection of target list is announced to assistive technology, visible focus indicators present.</p>"
```

### User Story — STORY-3.5: Reorder a card within a list (drag-and-drop)
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-3 → <EPIC-3-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-3; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As an Editor or Owner of a board, I want to drag a card to a new position within the same list, so that I can control the priority order of tasks without moving them to a different workflow stage.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Ordering model — fractional rank with gap strategy: each card has a rank column (FLOAT / double precision, non-null, default 0.0). On create: rank = max(existing ranks in list) + 1.0; first card in empty list gets rank = 1.0. On reorder (insert after card A, before card B): new_rank = (A.rank + B.rank) / 2. Edge cases: insert at top → new_rank = first_card.rank / 2; insert at bottom → new_rank = last_card.rank + 1.0. Gap renumber trigger: if gap &lt; epsilon (default 1e-9), server renumbers all cards in that list in a single transaction (1.0, 2.0, 3.0, …), then places the moved card at its correct position.</li><li>Concurrency: the reorder command reads the list's card ranks inside a serializable-isolation transaction (or SELECT … WITH (UPDLOCK) hint on SQL Server) to prevent two concurrent midpoints from landing on the same value. No ETag / optimistic-concurrency header required in v1.</li><li>Query order: all list-of-cards endpoints ORDER BY rank ASC, id ASC (id as tiebreaker).</li><li>Performance: a single reorder must not rewrite all card rows except during the gap-renumber pass. Normal moves are a single-row UPDATE. The rank column is indexed on (listId, rank).</li><li>Pagination: the paginated GET of a list's cards returns cards ordered by rank. Reordering does not break pagination.</li><li>Real-time: other board members will not see the reorder until EPIC-6 broadcasts a card.reordered event — noted as a constraint.</li><li>Authorization: Editor and Owner may reorder; Viewer receives 403. Checked server-side.</li><li>DTOs only at the API boundary; RFC 7807 on all error paths; structured logging of reorder events (cardId, fromRank, toRank, renumberTriggered).</li><li>Clean Architecture: rank computation logic lives in the Application layer (command handler). The IRankingService interface (Application layer) is the seam; its SQL implementation is in Infrastructure.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Cross-list moves via drag-and-drop (STORY-3.4).</li><li>Bulk reorder (reordering multiple selected cards at once — deferred).</li><li>Custom sort modes (e.g. sort by due date — deferred to EPIC-4/EPIC-8).</li><li>Persisting a user's personal view order separately from the shared board order (deferred).</li><li>Undo / redo of reorder (deferred).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.3, §1.4, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am an authenticated Editor or Owner of the board <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/reorder with a valid afterCardId (the card after which to insert; null or omitted means place at the top) <b>Then</b> the card's rank is updated to place it immediately after afterCardId within the same list, I receive 200 OK with the updated card DTO (id, title, listId, rank, updatedAt), and a subsequent paginated GET of the list's cards returns cards ordered by the new rank.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply an afterCardId that belongs to a different list than the card being reordered <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/reorder <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 ('Position anchor does not belong to the same list') and the card's rank is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply an afterCardId equal to the card being reordered <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/reorder <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 ('A card cannot be positioned after itself') and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> afterCardId is null or omitted <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/reorder <b>Then</b> the card is moved to rank position 0 (or midpoint between 0 and the current first card's rank), placing it at the top of the list.</p><p><b>Given</b> two concurrent reorder operations attempt to place cards at the same midpoint position <b>When</b> both are processed <b>Then</b> the server resolves the tie deterministically; the resulting order is stable and consistent — no duplicate rank values exist in a list after either transaction commits.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer on the board <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/reorder <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 and the card's rank is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board, or present no/invalid JWT <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/reorder <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member — existence not disclosed) or 401 (unauthenticated) and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I drag a card within a list column in the board UI <b>When</b> I drop it between two other cards <b>Then</b> the card appears at the new position immediately (optimistic reorder), the PATCH is issued in the background, and if the request fails the card snaps back to its original position with an error toast.</p><p><b>Given</b> the board list has ~200 cards <b>When</b> a single reorder is performed <b>Then</b> the PATCH request completes in &lt; ~500ms (well within the board's 1.5s load budget) and at most one additional renumber transaction is triggered (not N writes proportional to card count).</p><p><b>Given</b> the board UI renders cards in a list column <b>When</b> any reorder completes <b>Then</b> the visual order of cards matches the rank-ordered server response — no local order drift.</p><p><b>Given</b> a list column renders draggable cards <b>When</b> viewed by a Viewer <b>Then</b> cards are not draggable — no drag handle or drag affordance is shown.</p><p><b>Given</b> the drag-and-drop UI is displayed <b>When</b> rendered <b>Then</b> it meets WCAG 2.2 AA: each card's drag handle is keyboard-accessible (arrow keys to move up/down, Space/Enter to pick up and drop), drag state is announced via aria-grabbed, valid drop targets indicated via aria-dropeffect, visible focus on the drag handle.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-3.5: Reorder a card within a list (drag-and-drop)" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-3; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As an Editor or Owner of a board, I want to drag a card to a new position within the same list, so that I can control the priority order of tasks without moving them to a different workflow stage.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Ordering model — fractional rank with gap strategy: each card has a rank column (FLOAT / double precision, non-null, default 0.0). On create: rank = max(existing ranks in list) + 1.0; first card in empty list gets rank = 1.0. On reorder (insert after card A, before card B): new_rank = (A.rank + B.rank) / 2. Edge cases: insert at top → new_rank = first_card.rank / 2; insert at bottom → new_rank = last_card.rank + 1.0. Gap renumber trigger: if gap &lt; epsilon (default 1e-9), server renumbers all cards in that list in a single transaction (1.0, 2.0, 3.0, …), then places the moved card at its correct position.</li><li>Concurrency: the reorder command reads the list's card ranks inside a serializable-isolation transaction (or SELECT … WITH (UPDLOCK) hint on SQL Server) to prevent two concurrent midpoints from landing on the same value. No ETag / optimistic-concurrency header required in v1.</li><li>Query order: all list-of-cards endpoints ORDER BY rank ASC, id ASC (id as tiebreaker).</li><li>Performance: a single reorder must not rewrite all card rows except during the gap-renumber pass. Reordering does not break pagination.</li><li>Real-time: other board members will not see the reorder until EPIC-6 broadcasts a card.reordered event — noted as a constraint.</li><li>Authorization: Editor and Owner may reorder; Viewer receives 403. Checked server-side.</li><li>DTOs only at the API boundary; RFC 7807 on all error paths; structured logging of reorder events (cardId, fromRank, toRank, renumberTriggered).</li><li>Clean Architecture: rank computation logic lives in the Application layer (command handler). The IRankingService interface (Application layer) is the seam; its SQL implementation is in Infrastructure.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Cross-list moves via drag-and-drop (STORY-3.4).</li><li>Bulk reorder (reordering multiple selected cards at once — deferred).</li><li>Custom sort modes (e.g. sort by due date — deferred to EPIC-4/EPIC-8).</li><li>Persisting a user's personal view order separately from the shared board order (deferred).</li><li>Undo / redo of reorder (deferred).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.1, §1.3, §1.4, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am an authenticated Editor or Owner of the board <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/reorder with a valid afterCardId (the card after which to insert; null or omitted means place at the top) <b>Then</b> the card's rank is updated to place it immediately after afterCardId within the same list, I receive 200 OK with the updated card DTO (id, title, listId, rank, updatedAt), and a subsequent paginated GET of the list's cards returns cards ordered by the new rank.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply an afterCardId that belongs to a different list than the card being reordered <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/reorder <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 ('Position anchor does not belong to the same list') and the card's rank is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply an afterCardId equal to the card being reordered <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/reorder <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 ('A card cannot be positioned after itself') and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> afterCardId is null or omitted <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/reorder <b>Then</b> the card is moved to rank position 0 (or midpoint between 0 and the current first card's rank), placing it at the top of the list.</p><p><b>Given</b> two concurrent reorder operations attempt to place cards at the same midpoint position <b>When</b> both are processed <b>Then</b> the server resolves the tie deterministically; the resulting order is stable and consistent — no duplicate rank values exist in a list after either transaction commits.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer on the board <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/reorder <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 and the card's rank is unchanged.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board, or present no/invalid JWT <b>When</b> I PATCH /cards/{cardId}/reorder <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member — existence not disclosed) or 401 (unauthenticated) and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I drag a card within a list column in the board UI <b>When</b> I drop it between two other cards <b>Then</b> the card appears at the new position immediately (optimistic reorder), the PATCH is issued in the background, and if the request fails the card snaps back to its original position with an error toast.</p><p><b>Given</b> the board list has ~200 cards <b>When</b> a single reorder is performed <b>Then</b> the PATCH request completes in &lt; ~500ms (well within the board's 1.5s load budget) and at most one additional renumber transaction is triggered (not N writes proportional to card count).</p><p><b>Given</b> the board UI renders cards in a list column <b>When</b> any reorder completes <b>Then</b> the visual order of cards matches the rank-ordered server response — no local order drift.</p><p><b>Given</b> a list column renders draggable cards <b>When</b> viewed by a Viewer <b>Then</b> cards are not draggable — no drag handle or drag affordance is shown.</p><p><b>Given</b> the drag-and-drop UI is displayed <b>When</b> rendered <b>Then</b> it meets WCAG 2.2 AA: each card's drag handle is keyboard-accessible (arrow keys to move up/down, Space/Enter to pick up and drop), drag state is announced via aria-grabbed, valid drop targets indicated via aria-dropeffect, visible focus on the drag handle.</p>"
```

**Link to parent**
```
az boards work-item relation add --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --id <this-story-id> --relation-type parent --target-id <EPIC-3-id>
```
### User Story — STORY-4.1: Manage a board's label set (create / edit / delete)
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-4 → <EPIC-4-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-4; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a board Editor or Owner, I want to create, rename, recolour, and delete labels scoped to my board, so that my team has a consistent, reusable set of categories to apply to cards.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Security / authorization: all mutations require Editor or Owner role, enforced server-side. Viewer → 403. Non-member / unauthenticated → 404 / 401.</li><li>Data: name 1–50 characters (enforced in Domain entity, EF column, and client validation). color must be a valid 6-digit or 3-digit CSS hex string (e.g. #FF5733, #F53); non-hex strings such as red or rgb(...) are rejected with 400. name is unique per board (case-insensitive, at the database constraint and application layer).</li><li>Partial-update name uniqueness: the duplicate-name check is only triggered when a new name value is present in the PATCH body; a color-only PATCH does not re-evaluate the (unchanged) existing name.</li><li>labelId scope: a PATCH or DELETE referencing a labelId that does not exist or does not belong to boardId returns 404 (generic — existence not disclosed); no data is modified.</li><li>Cascade delete: deleting a label removes all CardLabel join-table rows for that label in the same DB transaction; no orphans.</li><li>Pagination: GET /boards/{boardId}/labels returns { items, page, pageSize, total } (offset-based, page default 1, pageSize default 20 max 100).</li><li>API: DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li>Clean Architecture: Label entity and CardLabel join in Domain; use-cases in Application; EF Core persistence in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api. No EF/Microsoft.* references in Domain.</li><li>a11y: label color is never the ONLY distinguisher — the name field is always required and displayed alongside (or instead of) the color swatch in all UI surfaces.</li><li>Real-time: update and delete events propagate to all board members &lt;1s (via EPIC-6); this story defines the data contract; SignalR wiring is EPIC-6's responsibility.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Applying labels to cards (STORY-4.2).</li><li>Filtering cards by label (EPIC-8).</li><li>Label ordering / drag-and-drop.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner of a board <b>When</b> I POST /boards/{boardId}/labels with a valid name (1–50 characters) and a valid color (CSS hex, e.g. #FF5733) <b>Then</b> the label is created, persisted, and I receive 201 Created with a label DTO (id, boardId, name, color).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner <b>When</b> I PATCH /boards/{boardId}/labels/{labelId} with an updated name and/or color <b>Then</b> the label is updated and I receive 200 OK with the updated DTO; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner <b>When</b> I DELETE /boards/{boardId}/labels/{labelId} <b>Then</b> the label is removed from the board AND all card–label associations for that label are cascade-removed atomically; I receive 204 No Content; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> a board has existing labels <b>When</b> I GET /boards/{boardId}/labels <b>Then</b> I receive a paginated list ({ items, page, pageSize, total }) of all labels for that board.</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a name that already exists on the same board (case-insensitive) <b>When</b> I create or rename a label <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 400 and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I PATCH a label with a new name value that already exists on the same board (case-insensitive) <b>When</b> the update is processed <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 400 and no change is made; a color-only PATCH (no name supplied) does NOT re-validate the existing name and succeeds if the color is valid.</p><p><b>Given</b> the labelId in a PATCH or DELETE request does not exist, or exists but does not belong to boardId <b>When</b> I attempt the operation <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (generic — existence not disclosed) and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a name that is blank or longer than 50 characters, or a color that is not a valid CSS hex string <b>When</b> I create or rename/recolour a label <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 400 and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to create, update, or delete a label <b>Then</b> I receive 403 Forbidden and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board or present no/invalid token <b>When</b> I attempt any label mutation or read <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member — existence not disclosed) or 401 (unauthenticated); no data is returned.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner viewing the label management panel <b>When</b> it is loading, empty, or encounters an error <b>Then</b> appropriate loading, empty ('No labels yet — create one to get started'), and error states are shown; all controls meet WCAG 2.2 AA.</p><p><b>Given</b> I initiate a label delete <b>When</b> the confirmation dialog appears <b>Then</b> I must confirm explicitly before the label is deleted; cancelling leaves the label intact.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-4.1: Manage a board's label set (create / edit / delete)" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-4; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As a board Editor or Owner, I want to create, rename, recolour, and delete labels scoped to my board, so that my team has a consistent, reusable set of categories to apply to cards.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Security / authorization: all mutations require Editor or Owner role, enforced server-side. Viewer → 403. Non-member / unauthenticated → 404 / 401.</li><li>Data: name 1–50 characters (enforced in Domain entity, EF column, and client validation). color must be a valid 6-digit or 3-digit CSS hex string (e.g. #FF5733, #F53); non-hex strings such as red or rgb(...) are rejected with 400. name is unique per board (case-insensitive, at the database constraint and application layer).</li><li>Partial-update name uniqueness: the duplicate-name check is only triggered when a new name value is present in the PATCH body; a color-only PATCH does not re-evaluate the (unchanged) existing name.</li><li>labelId scope: a PATCH or DELETE referencing a labelId that does not exist or does not belong to boardId returns 404 (generic — existence not disclosed); no data is modified.</li><li>Cascade delete: deleting a label removes all CardLabel join-table rows for that label in the same DB transaction; no orphans.</li><li>Pagination: GET /boards/{boardId}/labels returns { items, page, pageSize, total } (offset-based, page default 1, pageSize default 20 max 100).</li><li>API: DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li>Clean Architecture: Label entity and CardLabel join in Domain; use-cases in Application; EF Core persistence in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api. this story defines the data contract; SignalR wiring is EPIC-6's responsibility.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Applying labels to cards (STORY-4.2).</li><li>Filtering cards by label (EPIC-8).</li><li>Label ordering / drag-and-drop.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner of a board <b>When</b> I POST /boards/{boardId}/labels with a valid name (1–50 characters) and a valid color (CSS hex, e.g. #FF5733) <b>Then</b> the label is created, persisted, and I receive 201 Created with a label DTO (id, boardId, name, color).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner <b>When</b> I PATCH /boards/{boardId}/labels/{labelId} with an updated name and/or color <b>Then</b> the label is updated and I receive 200 OK with the updated DTO; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner <b>When</b> I DELETE /boards/{boardId}/labels/{labelId} <b>Then</b> the label is removed from the board AND all card–label associations for that label are cascade-removed atomically; a color-only PATCH (no name supplied) does NOT re-validate the existing name and succeeds if the color is valid.</p><p><b>Given</b> the labelId in a PATCH or DELETE request does not exist, or exists but does not belong to boardId <b>When</b> I attempt the operation <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (generic — existence not disclosed) and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a name that is blank or longer than 50 characters, or a color that is not a valid CSS hex string <b>When</b> I create or rename/recolour a label <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 400 and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to create, update, or delete a label <b>Then</b> I receive 403 Forbidden and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board or present no/invalid token <b>When</b> I attempt any label mutation or read <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member — existence not disclosed) or 401 (unauthenticated); no data is returned.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner viewing the label management panel <b>When</b> it is loading, empty, or encounters an error <b>Then</b> appropriate loading, empty ('No labels yet — create one to get started'), and error states are shown; all controls meet WCAG 2.2 AA.</p><p><b>Given</b> I initiate a label delete <b>When</b> the confirmation dialog appears <b>Then</b> I must confirm explicitly before the label is deleted; cancelling leaves the label intact.</p>"

### User Story — STORY-4.2: Add / remove a label on a card
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-4 → <EPIC-4-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-4; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a board Editor or Owner, I want to add or remove a board label from a card, so that cards can be categorised using the board's shared label set.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Security / authorization: add and remove label require Editor or Owner role, enforced server-side. Viewer → 403. Non-member / unauthenticated → 404 / 401.</li><li>Cross-board guard: the labelId must belong to the same board as the card; validated server-side (prevents IDOR).</li><li>Idempotency: adding an already-applied label is 400, not silent success (unambiguous client state).</li><li>API: DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path. No label data is modified — labels are managed in STORY-4.1.</li><li>Clean Architecture: CardLabel association managed in Application use-cases; no EF/Microsoft.* in Domain.</li><li>Read: GET /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/labels returns the list of labels currently applied to the card (non-paginated — a card's applied labels are bounded in practice).</li><li>Real-time: add and remove events propagate to all board members &lt;1s (via EPIC-6); this story defines the data contract only.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Creating or editing labels (STORY-4.1).</li><li>Filtering cards by label (EPIC-8).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner and a label exists on the board <b>When</b> I POST /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/labels with { 'labelId': '&lt;id&gt;' } <b>Then</b> the label is associated with the card, I receive 201 Created with { cardId, labelId }, and the updated card label list is visible; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> a label is already applied to a card <b>When</b> I POST the same labelId again <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 400 ('Label already applied to this card') and no duplicate association is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner and a label is applied to a card <b>When</b> I DELETE /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/labels/{labelId} <b>Then</b> the association is removed, I receive 204 No Content, and the label no longer appears on the card; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> the labelId is valid and belongs to the board but is <b>not currently applied</b> to the card <b>When</b> I DELETE /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/labels/{labelId} <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 404 ('Label is not applied to this card') and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a labelId that does not belong to the same board as the card <b>When</b> I attempt to add the label <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 400 ('Label does not belong to this board') and no association is created (prevents cross-board label injection).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to add or remove a label from a card <b>Then</b> I receive 403 Forbidden and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board or present no/invalid token <b>When</b> I attempt any card-label mutation <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member) or 401 (unauthenticated); no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> the card detail panel is open <b>When</b> it is loading, has no labels, or encounters an error <b>Then</b> appropriate loading, empty ('No labels'), and error states are shown; all controls meet WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>
```

**Create**
```

Viewer → 403. Non-member / unauthenticated → 404 / 401.</li><li>Cross-board guard: the labelId must belong to the same board as the card; validated server-side (prevents IDOR).</li><li>Idempotency: adding an already-applied label is 400, not silent success (unambiguous client state).</li><li>API: DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path. No label data is modified — labels are managed in STORY-4.1.</li><li>Clean Architecture: CardLabel association managed in Application use-cases; no EF/Microsoft.* in Domain.</li><li>Read: GET /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/labels returns the list of labels currently applied to the card (non-paginated — a card's applied labels are bounded in practice).</li><li>Real-time: add and remove events propagate to all board members &lt;1s (via EPIC-6); this story defines the data contract only.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Creating or editing labels (STORY-4.1).</li><li>Filtering cards by label (EPIC-8).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner and a label exists on the board <b>When</b> I POST /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/labels with { 'labelId': '&lt;id&gt;' } <b>Then</b> the label is associated with the card, I receive 201 Created with { cardId, labelId }, and the updated card label list is visible; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> a label is already applied to a card <b>When</b> I POST the same labelId again <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 400 ('Label already applied to this card') and no duplicate association is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner and a label is applied to a card <b>When</b> I DELETE /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/labels/{labelId} <b>Then</b> the association is removed, I receive 204 No Content, and the label no longer appears on the card; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> the labelId is valid and belongs to the board but is <b>not currently applied</b> to the card <b>When</b> I DELETE /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/labels/{labelId} <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 404 ('Label is not applied to this card') and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a labelId that does not belong to the same board as the card <b>When</b> I attempt to add the label <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 400 ('Label does not belong to this board') and no association is created (prevents cross-board label injection).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to add or remove a label from a card <b>Then</b> I receive 403 Forbidden and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board or present no/invalid token <b>When</b> I attempt any card-label mutation <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member) or 401 (unauthenticated); no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> the card detail panel is open <b>When</b> it is loading, has no labels, or encounters an error <b>Then</b> appropriate loading, empty ('No labels'), and error states are shown; all controls meet WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>"
```

### User Story — STORY-4.3: Assign / unassign a board member to a card
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-4 → <EPIC-4-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-4; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a board Editor or Owner, I want to assign board members to a card and remove those assignments, so that ownership and responsibility are clear at a glance.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Security / authorization: assign and unassign require Editor or Owner role, enforced server-side. Viewer → 403. Non-member / unauthenticated → 404 / 401.</li><li>Assignee pool guard: only current board members may be assigned; validated server-side at assignment time (prevents IDOR and assignment of arbitrary users). Existing assignments for removed members are not auto-purged (historical record preserved; UI flags them).</li><li>API: DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path. GET /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/assignees returns the list of current assignees (non-paginated — card assignees are bounded by board membership size).</li><li>Clean Architecture: CardAssignee join entity in Domain; use-cases in Application; EF Core in Infrastructure. No EF/Microsoft.* in Domain.</li><li>Real-time: add and remove events propagate &lt;1s (via EPIC-6); this story defines the data contract only.</li><li>Accessibility: assignee avatars are decorative (aria-hidden); display name is the accessible text. Remove button has aria-label='Remove assignee &lt;displayName&gt;'.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Managing board membership / inviting members (EPIC-1).</li><li>'My Tasks' aggregated view across boards (EPIC-9).</li><li>Notifying assignees by email or push (future).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner and userId is a current member of the board <b>When</b> I POST /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/assignees with { 'userId': '&lt;id&gt;' } <b>Then</b> the user is assigned to the card, I receive 201 Created with { cardId, userId, displayName, avatarUrl }, and the assignment is visible on the card; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> a user is already assigned to a card <b>When</b> I POST the same userId again <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 400 ('User already assigned to this card') and no duplicate assignment is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I attempt to assign a userId who is NOT a current member of the board <b>When</b> I POST the assignment <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 400 ('User is not a member of this board') and no assignment is created (prevents assigning non-members).</p><p><b>Given</b> a user has been removed from the board after being assigned to a card <b>When</b> an Editor or Owner views the card <b>Then</b> existing assignments are preserved and displayed (with a visual warning, e.g. '(removed from board)'); <b>When</b> an Editor or Owner attempts to add a NEW assignment for a removed user <b>Then</b> they receive 400 as above.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner and a user is assigned to a card <b>When</b> I DELETE /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/assignees/{userId} <b>Then</b> the assignment is removed, I receive 204 No Content, and the user no longer appears as an assignee; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> the userId in the DELETE path is not currently assigned to the card <b>When</b> I attempt to remove them <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 404 ('Assignee not found on this card') and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to add or remove an assignee <b>Then</b> I receive 403 Forbidden and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board or present no/invalid token <b>When</b> I attempt any assignee mutation <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member) or 401 (unauthenticated); no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> the card detail panel is open <b>When</b> it is loading, has no assignees, or encounters an error <b>Then</b> appropriate loading, empty ('No assignees'), and error states are shown; all controls meet WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-4.3: Assign / unassign a board member to a card" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-4; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As a board Editor or Owner, I want to assign board members to a card and remove those assignments, so that ownership and responsibility are clear at a glance.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Security / authorization: assign and unassign require Editor or Owner role, enforced server-side. Viewer → 403. Non-member / unauthenticated → 404 / 401.</li><li>Assignee pool guard: only current board members may be assigned; validated server-side at assignment time (prevents IDOR and assignment of arbitrary users). Existing assignments for removed members are not auto-purged (historical record preserved; UI flags them).</li><li>API: DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path. GET /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/assignees returns the list of current assignees (non-paginated — card assignees are bounded by board membership size).</li><li>Clean Architecture: CardAssignee join entity in Domain; use-cases in Application; EF Core in Infrastructure. No EF/Microsoft.* in Domain.</li><li>Real-time: add and remove events propagate &lt;1s (via EPIC-6); this story defines the data contract only.</li><li>Accessibility: assignee avatars are decorative (aria-hidden); display name is the accessible text. Remove button has aria-label='Remove assignee &lt;displayName&gt;'.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Managing board membership / inviting members (EPIC-1).</li><li>'My Tasks' aggregated view across boards (EPIC-9).</li><li>Notifying assignees by email or push (future).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner and userId is a current member of the board <b>When</b> I POST /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/assignees with { 'userId': '&lt;id&gt;' } <b>Then</b> the user is assigned to the card, I receive 201 Created with { cardId, userId, displayName, avatarUrl }, and the assignment is visible on the card; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> a user is already assigned to a card <b>When</b> I POST the same userId again <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 400 ('User already assigned to this card') and no duplicate assignment is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I attempt to assign a userId who is NOT a current member of the board <b>When</b> I POST the assignment <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 400 ('User is not a member of this board') and no assignment is created (prevents assigning non-members).</p><p><b>Given</b> a user has been removed from the board after being assigned to a card <b>When</b> an Editor or Owner views the card <b>Then</b> existing assignments are preserved and displayed (with a visual warning, e.g. '(removed from board)'); <b>When</b> an Editor or Owner attempts to add a NEW assignment for a removed user <b>Then</b> they receive 400 as above.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner and a user is assigned to a card <b>When</b> I DELETE /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/assignees/{userId} <b>Then</b> the assignment is removed, I receive 204 No Content, and the user no longer appears as an assignee; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> the userId in the DELETE path is not currently assigned to the card <b>When</b> I attempt to remove them <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 404 ('Assignee not found on this card') and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to add or remove an assignee <b>Then</b> I receive 403 Forbidden and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board or present no/invalid token <b>When</b> I attempt any assignee mutation <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member) or 401 (unauthenticated); no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> the card detail panel is open <b>When</b> it is loading, has no assignees, or encounters an error <b>Then</b> appropriate loading, empty ('No assignees'), and error states are shown; all controls meet WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>"
```

**Link to parent**
```
az boards work-item relation add --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --id <this-story-id> --relation-type parent --target-id <EPIC-4-id>
```

### User Story — STORY-4.4: Set / clear a card due date
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-4 → <EPIC-4-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-4; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a board Editor or Owner, I want to set or clear a due date on a card, so that my team knows when work is expected to be complete.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Security / authorization: set and clear due date require Editor or Owner role, enforced server-side. Viewer → 403. Non-member / unauthenticated → 404 / 401.</li><li>cardId scope: a PATCH referencing a cardId that does not exist or does not belong to boardId returns 404 (generic — existence not disclosed); no data is modified.</li><li>Timezone: dueDate is stored as DateTimeOffset (UTC) in SQL Server; API always accepts and returns ISO 8601 UTC strings (e.g. '2026-08-01T17:00:00Z'). The server has no concept of 'overdue' — that is a client display concern.</li><li>Null is valid: dueDate may be null (not set). A PATCH with 'dueDate': null explicitly clears it.</li><li>Partial update: the PATCH endpoint for a card accepts any subset of patchable fields (dueDate, and those added by STORY-4.5); omitting a field leaves it unchanged.</li><li>API: DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li>Clean Architecture: dueDate field on Card entity in Domain; update use-case in Application; EF Core in Infrastructure. No EF/Microsoft.* in Domain.</li><li>Real-time: due-date changes propagate to all board members &lt;1s (via EPIC-6); this story defines the data contract only.</li><li>Accessibility: the date picker (or date input) must be keyboard-accessible and have a visible label. The overdue indicator must not rely on color alone — the text 'Overdue' (or equivalent) must accompany the color change.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Server-side overdue computation or notifications.</li><li>Recurring due dates.</li><li>Filtering cards by due date (EPIC-8).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner <b>When</b> I PATCH /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId} with { 'dueDate': '&lt;ISO 8601 UTC datetime&gt;' } <b>Then</b> the due date is stored as UTC, I receive 200 OK with the updated card DTO (including dueDate as ISO 8601 UTC string), and the due date is visible on the card; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> a card has a due date <b>When</b> I PATCH with { 'dueDate': null } <b>Then</b> the due date is cleared, I receive 200 OK with 'dueDate': null, and the due date indicator is removed from the card; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a dueDate value that is not a valid ISO 8601 datetime string <b>When</b> I PATCH the card <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 400 and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to set or clear a due date <b>Then</b> I receive 403 Forbidden and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board or present no/invalid token <b>When</b> I attempt to set or clear a due date <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member) or 401 (unauthenticated) and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> the cardId in the PATCH request does not exist or does not belong to boardId <b>When</b> I attempt to set or clear a due date <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (generic — existence not disclosed) and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> a card has a due date in the past <b>When</b> a member views the card <b>Then</b> the due date is displayed with an overdue indicator (e.g. red color + 'Overdue' label text); overdue calculation is done client-side using the viewer's local time; the server stores and returns UTC only.</p><p><b>Given</b> the card detail panel is open <b>When</b> it is loading or encounters an error <b>Then</b> appropriate loading and error states are shown; the date picker meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>
```

**Create**
```

Viewer → 403. Non-member / unauthenticated → 404 / 401.</li><li>cardId scope: a PATCH referencing a cardId that does not exist or does not belong to boardId returns 404 (generic — existence not disclosed); no data is modified.</li><li>Timezone: dueDate is stored as DateTimeOffset (UTC) in SQL Server; API always accepts and returns ISO 8601 UTC strings (e.g. '2026-08-01T17:00:00Z'). The server has no concept of 'overdue' — that is a client display concern.</li><li>Null is valid: dueDate may be null (not set). A PATCH with 'dueDate': null explicitly clears it.</li><li>Partial update: the PATCH endpoint for a card accepts any subset of patchable fields (dueDate, and those added by STORY-4.5); omitting a field leaves it unchanged.</li><li>API: DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li>Clean Architecture: dueDate field on Card entity in Domain; update use-case in Application; EF Core in Infrastructure. overdue calculation is done client-side using the viewer's local time; the server stores and returns UTC only.</p><p><b>Given</b> the card detail panel is open <b>When</b> it is loading or encounters an error <b>Then</b> appropriate loading and error states are shown; the date picker meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>"

### User Story — STORY-4.5: Set / clear a card priority
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-4 → <EPIC-4-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-4; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a board Editor or Owner, I want to set or clear a priority level on a card, so that my team can immediately see which work is most urgent.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Security / authorization: set priority requires Editor or Owner role, enforced server-side. Viewer → 403. Non-member / unauthenticated → 404 / 401.</li><li>cardId scope: a PATCH referencing a cardId that does not exist or does not belong to boardId returns 404 (generic — existence not disclosed); no data is modified.</li><li>None display: when priority is None, the priority badge is HIDDEN — no 'None' label or placeholder chip is rendered.</li><li>Priority enum (canonical): None (0) / Low (1) / Medium (2) / High (3) — defined as an enum in Domain; stored as int column in SQL Server; serialised as the string name in API DTOs (e.g. 'High'). Default is None.</li><li>None is explicit: None is a first-class value meaning 'no priority set'; it is the default for new cards and the value used to clear priority (not null).</li><li>Partial update: shares the same PATCH endpoint as STORY-4.4 (dueDate); fields are independent; omitting a field leaves it unchanged.</li><li>API: DTOs only at the boundary; enum serialised as string name; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li>Clean Architecture: Priority enum in Domain; Card.Priority property in Domain entity; update use-case in Application; EF Core stores as int; thin controller in Api. No EF/Microsoft.* in Domain.</li><li>Real-time: priority changes propagate to all board members &lt;1s (via EPIC-6); this story defines the data contract only.</li><li>Accessibility: priority indicator must not rely on color alone — the text label ('High', 'Medium', 'Low') must always be visible alongside any color/icon. The selector is a labelled control.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Custom priority levels or additional enum values.</li><li>Filtering / sorting cards by priority (EPIC-8).</li><li>Automated escalation based on priority.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner <b>When</b> I PATCH /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId} with { 'priority': 'High' } (or 'Medium', 'Low', 'None') <b>Then</b> the priority is stored, I receive 200 OK with the updated card DTO (including 'priority': 'High'), and the priority badge is visible on the card; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> a card has a priority set <b>When</b> I PATCH with { 'priority': 'None' } <b>Then</b> the priority is cleared to None, I receive 200 OK with 'priority': 'None', and the priority badge is HIDDEN; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a priority value outside the allowed enum (None, Low, Medium, High) <b>When</b> I PATCH the card <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 400 ('Invalid priority value. Allowed values: None, Low, Medium, High') and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> a card has not had its priority set (new cards), or priority is explicitly set to None <b>When</b> a member views the card <b>Then</b> the priority field reads None (the default); the priority badge is HIDDEN (consistent with 'No labels'/'No assignees' empty states — the badge is not shown as 'None').</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer of the board <b>When</b> I attempt to set or clear a priority <b>Then</b> I receive 403 Forbidden and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board or present no/invalid token <b>When</b> I attempt to set or clear a priority <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (non-member) or 401 (unauthenticated) and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> the cardId in the PATCH request does not exist or does not belong to boardId <b>When</b> I attempt to set or clear a priority <b>Then</b> I receive 404 (generic — existence not disclosed) and no change is made.</p><p><b>Given</b> the card detail panel is open <b>When</b> it is loading or encounters an error <b>Then</b> appropriate loading and error states are shown; the priority selector meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>
```

**Create**
```

Viewer → 403. Non-member / unauthenticated → 404 / 401.</li><li>cardId scope: a PATCH referencing a cardId that does not exist or does not belong to boardId returns 404 (generic — existence not disclosed); no data is modified.</li><li>None display: when priority is None, the priority badge is HIDDEN — no 'None' label or placeholder chip is rendered.</li><li>Priority enum (canonical): None (0) / Low (1) / Medium (2) / High (3) — defined as an enum in Domain; stored as int column in SQL Server; serialised as the string name in API DTOs (e.g. 'High'). Default is None.</li><li>None is explicit: None is a first-class value meaning 'no priority set'; it is the default for new cards and the value used to clear priority (not null).</li><li>Partial update: shares the same PATCH endpoint as STORY-4.4 (dueDate); fields are independent; omitting a field leaves it unchanged.</li><li>API: DTOs only at the boundary; enum serialised as string name; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li>Clean Architecture: Priority enum in Domain; Card.Priority property in Domain entity; update use-case in Application; EF Core stores as int; thin controller in Api. The selector is a labelled control.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Custom priority levels or additional enum values.</li><li>Filtering / sorting cards by priority (EPIC-8).</li><li>Automated escalation based on priority.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am an Editor or Owner <b>When</b> I PATCH /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId} with { 'priority': 'High' } (or 'Medium', 'Low', 'None') <b>Then</b> the priority is stored, I receive 200 OK with the updated card DTO (including 'priority': 'High'), and the priority badge is visible on the card; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> a card has a priority set <b>When</b> I PATCH with { 'priority': 'None' } <b>Then</b> the priority is cleared to None, I receive 200 OK with 'priority': 'None', and the priority badge is HIDDEN; real-time propagation &lt;1s (via EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a priority value outside the allowed enum (None, Low, Medium, High) <b>When</b> I PATCH the card <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 400 ('Invalid priority value. ### User Story — STORY-5.1: Add a comment to a card
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-5 → <EPIC-5-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-5; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As an Editor or Owner of a board, I want to post a comment on a card, so that I can leave context, questions, or decisions directly on the work item.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Security / authz: role check against board membership performed server-side before any persistence. Roles that may create comments: Owner, Editor. Viewer → 403. Non-member → 404. Unauthenticated → 401.</li><li>Validation: body length 1–5000 characters enforced in the Domain Comment entity, the EF column (nvarchar(5000) NOT NULL), and client-side (non-blocking, server is authoritative).</li><li>API contract: POST /api/boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/comments. Returns 201 with comment DTO. RFC 7807 on all error paths.</li><li>DTOs only at the API boundary; no EF entities exposed.</li><li>Clean Architecture: Comment entity in Domain; use-case in Application; EF Core persistence in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api (no EF/Microsoft.* in Domain or Application layers).</li><li>Performance: comment creation must complete in &lt;500 ms under normal load (DB write + SignalR publish).</li><li>Reliability: EF Core migration adds Comments table with FK to Cards and AspNetUsers; structured logging; global RFC 7807 error handler.</li><li>Accessibility: WCAG 2.2 AA on the add-comment form; errors use role='alert' and aria-describedby.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Editing or deleting comments (STORY-5.3, STORY-5.4).</li><li>@mention autocomplete.</li><li>Rich-text / markdown input.</li><li>File attachments on comments.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.5, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated as an Editor or Owner of the board that contains the card <b>When</b> I POST { body } (1–5000 characters) to /api/boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/comments <b>Then</b> the comment is persisted and I receive 201 Created with a comment DTO (id, cardId, authorId, authorDisplayName, body, createdAt, updatedAt, isEdited: false).</p><p><b>Given</b> the comment is successfully created <b>When</b> other members are connected <b>Then</b> they observe the new comment appear in real-time (propagation &lt;1 s via EPIC-6) without refreshing.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated as a <b>Viewer</b> of the board <b>When</b> I POST a comment <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 and no comment is created (server-side role check — Viewers are read-only per §1.4).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am <b>not a member</b> of the board <b>When</b> I POST a comment <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (board/card existence not disclosed to non-members) and no comment is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I present <b>no or invalid JWT</b> <b>When</b> I POST a comment <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807 and no comment is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a body that is <b>empty or exceeds 5000 characters</b> <b>When</b> I POST a comment <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a validation problem detail and no comment is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> the cardId does not belong to boardId (cross-board insertion attempt) <b>When</b> I POST a comment <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 and no comment is created (card–board membership verified server-side to prevent IDOR).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am on the card detail view <b>When</b> I open the comment panel <b>Then</b> I see an add-comment text area (1–5000 chars), a submit button, and inline character count; loading, validation-error, and server-error states are all present; the form meets <b>WCAG 2.2 AA</b> (label, aria-describedby for errors, keyboard-only operable).</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-5.1: Add a comment to a card" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-5; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As an Editor or Owner of a board, I want to post a comment on a card, so that I can leave context, questions, or decisions directly on the work item.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Security / authz: role check against board membership performed server-side before any persistence. Roles that may create comments: Owner, Editor. Viewer → 403. Non-member → 404. Unauthenticated → 401.</li><li>Validation: body length 1–5000 characters enforced in the Domain Comment entity, the EF column (nvarchar(5000) NOT NULL), and client-side (non-blocking, server is authoritative).</li><li>API contract: POST /api/boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/comments. Returns 201 with comment DTO. RFC 7807 on all error paths.</li><li>DTOs only at the API boundary; no EF entities exposed.</li><li>Clean Architecture: Comment entity in Domain; use-case in Application; EF Core persistence in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api (no EF/Microsoft.* in Domain or Application layers).</li><li>Performance: comment creation must complete in &lt;500 ms under normal load (DB write + SignalR publish).</li><li>Reliability: EF Core migration adds Comments table with FK to Cards and AspNetUsers; structured logging; global RFC 7807 error handler.</li><li>Accessibility: WCAG 2.2 AA on the add-comment form; errors use role='alert' and aria-describedby.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Editing or deleting comments (STORY-5.3, STORY-5.4).</li><li>@mention autocomplete.</li><li>Rich-text / markdown input.</li><li>File attachments on comments.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.5, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated as an Editor or Owner of the board that contains the card <b>When</b> I POST { body } (1–5000 characters) to /api/boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/comments <b>Then</b> the comment is persisted and I receive 201 Created with a comment DTO (id, cardId, authorId, authorDisplayName, body, createdAt, updatedAt, isEdited: false).</p><p><b>Given</b> the comment is successfully created <b>When</b> other members are connected <b>Then</b> they observe the new comment appear in real-time (propagation &lt;1 s via EPIC-6) without refreshing.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated as a <b>Viewer</b> of the board <b>When</b> I POST a comment <b>Then</b> I receive 403 RFC 7807 and no comment is created (server-side role check — Viewers are read-only per §1.4).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am <b>not a member</b> of the board <b>When</b> I POST a comment <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (board/card existence not disclosed to non-members) and no comment is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I present <b>no or invalid JWT</b> <b>When</b> I POST a comment <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807 and no comment is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> I submit a body that is <b>empty or exceeds 5000 characters</b> <b>When</b> I POST a comment <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a validation problem detail and no comment is created.</p><p><b>Given</b> the cardId does not belong to boardId (cross-board insertion attempt) <b>When</b> I POST a comment <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 and no comment is created (card–board membership verified server-side to prevent IDOR).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am on the card detail view <b>When</b> I open the comment panel <b>Then</b> I see an add-comment text area (1–5000 chars), a submit button, and inline character count; loading, validation-error, and server-error states are all present; the form meets <b>WCAG 2.2 AA</b> (label, aria-describedby for errors, keyboard-only operable).</p>"
```

**Link to parent**
```
az boards work-item relation add --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --id <this-story-id> --relation-type parent --target-id <EPIC-5-id>
```

### User Story — STORY-5.2: View a card's comments (paginated)
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-5 → <EPIC-5-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-5; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As any board member (Owner, Editor, or Viewer), I want to see all comments on a card in chronological order, so that I can follow the discussion without losing context.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Security / authz: GET is permitted for all board members including Viewers; non-member → 404; unauthenticated → 401. Server-side only.</li><li>Pagination: offset-based, identical envelope { items, page, pageSize, total } as established in EPIC-0 (STORY-0.4). pageSize max 100, default 20; page 1-indexed, default 1.</li><li>Ordering: results ordered by createdAt ASC (chronological). Stable sort required (tie-break on id ASC).</li><li>Performance: comment list for a card (up to 100 per page) returns in &lt;500 ms; indexed on CardId, CreatedAt.</li><li>API contract: GET /api/boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/comments?page=1&amp;pageSize=20. Returns 200 with pagination envelope. RFC 7807 on all error paths.</li><li>DTOs only at the boundary; isEdited is true when updatedAt &gt; createdAt.</li><li>Clean Architecture: query in Application; EF Core read in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li>Accessibility: WCAG 2.2 AA — loading/empty/error states; comment list is a semantic list (&lt;ul&gt;/&lt;li&gt;) with accessible author attribution.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Editing or deleting comments from this view (STORY-5.3, STORY-5.4 author the controls, but this story establishes the list rendering they appear within).</li><li>Sorting order controls (chronological ascending is fixed in v1).</li><li>Full-text search or filtering within a card's comments.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.5, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated as <b>any board member</b> (Owner, Editor, or Viewer) <b>When</b> I GET /api/boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/comments <b>Then</b> I receive 200 OK with a paginated envelope { items, page, pageSize, total } containing comment DTOs in ascending createdAt order; each DTO includes (id, cardId, authorId, authorDisplayName, body, createdAt, updatedAt, isEdited).</p><p><b>Given</b> the card has no comments <b>When</b> I GET the comments list <b>Then</b> I receive 200 OK with { items: [], page: 1, pageSize: 20, total: 0 } (not 404).</p><p><b>Given</b> I provide valid page and pageSize query parameters <b>When</b> I GET the comments list <b>Then</b> the response honors offset-based pagination: page is 1-indexed (default 1), pageSize default 20 max 100; total reflects the full unfiltered count; requesting a page beyond the last returns { items: [], page: N, pageSize, total }.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply an invalid pageSize (e.g. 0, negative, or &gt; 100) <b>When</b> I GET the comments list <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a validation problem detail.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am <b>not a member</b> of the board <b>When</b> I GET the comments list <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (existence not disclosed).</p><p><b>Given</b> I present <b>no or invalid JWT</b> <b>When</b> I GET the comments list <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> the cardId does not belong to boardId <b>When</b> I GET the comments list <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am on the card detail view <b>When</b> comments are loading <b>Then</b> a skeleton/loading state is shown; <b>When</b> there are no comments, an empty state ('No comments yet') is shown; <b>When</b> the fetch fails, a server-error banner with a retry action is shown; all states meet <b>WCAG 2.2 AA</b>.</p><p><b>Given</b> a new comment is posted by another user <b>When</b> I am viewing the card <b>Then</b> it appears in the list in real-time (propagation &lt;1 s via EPIC-6) without a manual refresh.</p>
```

**Create**
```

Server-side only.</li><li>Pagination: offset-based, identical envelope { items, page, pageSize, total } as established in EPIC-0 (STORY-0.4). pageSize max 100, default 20; page 1-indexed, default 1.</li><li>Ordering: results ordered by createdAt ASC (chronological). Stable sort required (tie-break on id ASC).</li><li>Performance: comment list for a card (up to 100 per page) returns in &lt;500 ms; indexed on CardId, CreatedAt.</li><li>API contract: GET /api/boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/comments?page=1&amp;pageSize=20. Returns 200 with pagination envelope. RFC 7807 on all error paths.</li><li>DTOs only at the boundary; isEdited is true when updatedAt &gt; createdAt.</li><li>Clean Architecture: query in Application; EF Core read in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li>Accessibility: WCAG 2.2 AA — loading/empty/error states; comment list is a semantic list (&lt;ul&gt;/&lt;li&gt;) with accessible author attribution.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Editing or deleting comments from this view (STORY-5.3, STORY-5.4 author the controls, but this story establishes the list rendering they appear within).</li><li>Sorting order controls (chronological ascending is fixed in v1).</li><li>Full-text search or filtering within a card's comments.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.5, §1.4, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated as <b>any board member</b> (Owner, Editor, or Viewer) <b>When</b> I GET /api/boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}/comments <b>Then</b> I receive 200 OK with a paginated envelope { items, page, pageSize, total } containing comment DTOs in ascending createdAt order; total reflects the full unfiltered count; requesting a page beyond the last returns { items: [], page: N, pageSize, total }.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply an invalid pageSize (e.g. 0, negative, or &gt; <b>When</b> there are no comments, an empty state ('No comments yet') is shown; <b>When</b> the fetch fails, a server-error banner with a retry action is shown; all states meet <b>WCAG 2.2 AA</b>.</p><p><b>Given</b> a new comment is posted by another user <b>When</b> I am viewing the card <b>Then</b> it appears in the list in real-time (propagation &lt;1 s via EPIC-6) without a manual refresh.</p>"
