### User Story — STORY-7.2: View a board's activity feed
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-7 → <EPIC-7-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-7; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a board member (Owner, Editor, or Viewer), I want to browse a reverse-chronological log of everything that has changed on the board, so that I can understand what happened and who did it without asking teammates.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Authorization: enforced server-side on every request. Role check: any board member (Owner, Editor, Viewer) may read. Non-member → 404; unauthenticated → 401. Status code convention matches §1.6 and STORY-0.3/0.4 shared convention.</li><li>Pagination: offset-based; same envelope as all other list endpoints: { items, page, pageSize, total }, page 1-indexed default 1, pageSize default 20 max 100. The endpoint MUST always paginate — no unbounded list responses.</li><li>Read-only: no mutation (POST/PUT/PATCH/DELETE) is exposed on /activity. This endpoint is GET only.</li><li>Performance: the (BoardId, OccurredAt DESC) index (created in STORY-7.1) makes page reads efficient. The endpoint must not load all entries into memory before paginating.</li><li>DTOs only at the boundary (§2.2): the API returns an ActivityEntryDto (id, eventType, description, actorId, actorDisplayName, occurredAt). The ActivityEntry domain entity is never serialised directly.</li><li>Clean Architecture (§2.2): query handler in Application; EF Core read in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api; no EF/Microsoft.* in Domain.</li><li>RFC 7807: all error paths (400, 401, 404) return a valid problem detail.</li><li>Accessibility (§1.6 WCAG 2.2 AA): feed list is a semantic &lt;ol&gt; or &lt;ul&gt;, timestamps use &lt;time datetime='...'&gt;, loading skeleton is aria-busy, empty/error states are announced via role='status' or role='alert'. Infinite scroll / Load-more is keyboard-accessible.</li><li>Timestamps: occurredAt is returned in ISO 8601 UTC from the API. The UI may render it as a relative time (e.g. '3 minutes ago') with the full absolute timestamp in a title attribute or tooltip.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Filtering or searching within the feed (EPIC-8).</li><li>Live-updating the feed when new entries arrive (STORY-7.3).</li><li>Editing or deleting entries from the UI (immutable by design).</li><li>Exporting the activity log.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.3, §1.4, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am a board member (any role) <b>When</b> I GET /boards/{boardId}/activity <b>Then</b> I receive 200 OK with a paginated envelope { items, page, pageSize, total } where items is the list of activity entries sorted newest-first, each entry containing id, eventType, description, actorId, actorDisplayName, occurredAt (ISO 8601 UTC). Default page=1, pageSize=20; max pageSize=100.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board, or present no/invalid JWT <b>When</b> I GET /boards/{boardId}/activity <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (non-member — existence not disclosed) or 401 (unauthenticated) respectively. No data is returned.</p><p><b>Given</b> the board has no activity entries yet <b>When</b> I GET /boards/{boardId}/activity <b>Then</b> I receive 200 OK with { items: [], page: 1, pageSize: 20, total: 0 }.</p><p><b>Given</b> pageSize exceeds 100 or page is less than 1 <b>When</b> I call the endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a descriptive problem detail.</p><p><b>Given</b> I open the board's Activity tab in the UI <b>When</b> the page loads <b>Then</b> the feed renders in reverse-chronological order: each entry shows the actor's display name (or 'System'), the human-readable description, and the relative or absolute occurredAt timestamp. A loading skeleton is shown during fetch. An empty state ('No activity yet') is shown if the board has no entries. An error state with a retry button is shown on fetch failure.</p><p><b>Given</b> there are more entries than fit on one page <b>When</b> I reach the bottom of the feed <b>Then</b> the UI loads the next page (infinite scroll or a 'Load more' button), appending older entries below.</p><p><b>Given</b> I open the Activity tab on a board I am a Viewer of <b>When</b> the page loads <b>Then</b> the feed renders exactly as for an Owner or Editor (read-only is the same view; Viewer has no additional restrictions on reading the feed).</p><p><b>Given</b> the UI renders an entry for a deleted target (e.g. a card that was later deleted) <b>When</b> I view that entry <b>Then</b> the description snapshot (captured at write time) is displayed intact; no broken reference or missing-data placeholder.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-7.2: View a board's activity feed" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-7; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As a board member (Owner, Editor, or Viewer), I want to browse a reverse-chronological log of everything that has changed on the board, so that I can understand what happened and who did it without asking teammates.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Authorization: enforced server-side on every request. Role check: any board member (Owner, Editor, Viewer) may read. Non-member → 404; unauthenticated → 401. Status code convention matches §1.6 and STORY-0.3/0.4 shared convention.</li><li>Pagination: offset-based; same envelope as all other list endpoints: { items, page, pageSize, total }, page 1-indexed default 1, pageSize default 20 max 100. The endpoint MUST always paginate — no unbounded list responses.</li><li>Read-only: no mutation (POST/PUT/PATCH/DELETE) is exposed on /activity. This endpoint is GET only.</li><li>Performance: the (BoardId, OccurredAt DESC) index (created in STORY-7.1) makes page reads efficient. Infinite scroll / Load-more is keyboard-accessible.</li><li>Timestamps: occurredAt is returned in ISO 8601 UTC from the API. Default page=1, pageSize=20; max pageSize=100.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board, or present no/invalid JWT <b>When</b> I GET /boards/{boardId}/activity <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807 (non-member — existence not disclosed) or 401 (unauthenticated) respectively. No data is returned.</p><p><b>Given</b> the board has no activity entries yet <b>When</b> I GET /boards/{boardId}/activity <b>Then</b> I receive 200 OK with { items: [], page: 1, pageSize: 20, total: 0 }.</p><p><b>Given</b> pageSize exceeds 100 or page is less than 1 <b>When</b> I call the endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a descriptive problem detail.</p><p><b>Given</b> I open the board's Activity tab in the UI <b>When</b> the page loads <b>Then</b> the feed renders in reverse-chronological order: each entry shows the actor's display name (or 'System'), the human-readable description, and the relative or absolute occurredAt timestamp. A loading skeleton is shown during fetch. An empty state ('No activity yet') is shown if the board has no entries. An error state with a retry button is shown on fetch failure.</p><p><b>Given</b> there are more entries than fit on one page <b>When</b> I reach the bottom of the feed <b>Then</b> the UI loads the next page (infinite scroll or a 'Load more' button), appending older entries below.</p><p><b>Given</b> I open the Activity tab on a board I am a Viewer of <b>When</b> the page loads <b>Then</b> the feed renders exactly as for an Owner or Editor (read-only is the same view; Viewer has no additional restrictions on reading the feed).</p><p><b>Given</b> the UI renders an entry for a deleted target (e.g. a card that was later deleted) <b>When</b> I view that entry <b>Then</b> the description snapshot (captured at write time) is displayed intact; no broken reference or missing-data placeholder.</p>"
```

### User Story — STORY-7.3: Live activity updates
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-7 → <EPIC-7-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-7; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a board member with the Activity feed open, I want new activity entries to appear automatically within about one second of them being recorded, so that I can see the board's live history without refreshing.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Transport: consumes the board-{boardId} SignalR group provided by EPIC-6. This story MUST NOT implement a new Hub, connection manager, or group subscription mechanism — those belong to EPIC-6. STORY-7.3 only adds: (a) the server-side Hub method invocation to push the new ActivityEntryDto on the existing group, and (b) the client-side handler that prepends the DTO to the Pinia feed store.</li><li>Latency target: new entry visible to all connected board members within ~1s of the originating mutation committing (§1.2, §1.6).</li><li>Deduplication: the client must guard against receiving the same ActivityEntryDto twice (e.g. on reconnect + re-fetch race). Deduplicate by id in the Pinia store before prepending.</li><li>No unbounded growth: the Pinia store for live-prepended entries MUST NOT grow without bound. Cap the in-memory list at a configurable maximum (e.g. 200 entries) consistent with the pagination page-size contract; older entries remain available via the paginated REST endpoint.</li><li>Reconnection recovery: on SignalR reconnect, the UI calls the REST endpoint (page 1) to recover missed entries, then resumes live updates. The REST and live paths must produce the same ActivityEntryDto shape.</li><li>Authorization: EPIC-6 enforces group membership at the Hub level; STORY-7.3 relies on that. No additional per-push authorization check is required here.</li><li>Orchestration (Application layer only): the Application command handler calls IActivityWriter WITHIN the unit-of-work (same SaveChanges as the mutation), then — AFTER commit — calls IActivityPublisher.Publish fire-and-forget. Both calls live in the Application layer; there is no extra orchestration layer between them. The Infrastructure IActivityPublisher implementation holds the Hub reference; the Application layer has no knowledge of SignalR types.</li><li>Clean Architecture (§2.2): the server push is triggered from the Application layer (after the mutation commits and the activity entry is written) via an IActivityPublisher interface; the SignalR Hub implementation lives in Infrastructure/Api. No SignalR types in Domain or Application.</li><li>Publisher failure isolation: if IActivityPublisher.Publish throws after commit, the exception MUST be caught and logged (structured log including boardId and activityEntryId) but MUST NOT propagate to the caller. The mutation response and the activity write are already durable; only the real-time push is lost.</li><li>Accessibility: new entries prepended live are announced to screen readers via an aria-live='polite' region on the feed list. The announcement must not be intrusive — polite (not assertive) so it does not interrupt ongoing interactions.</li><li>Performance: Hub invocations are fire-and-forget from the API's perspective; a SignalR delivery failure MUST NOT cause the mutation transaction to roll back or the API request to fail.</li><li>Testing: the real-time path is integration-tested against the actual Hub (using Microsoft.AspNetCore.SignalR.Client in test); unit tests mock IActivityPublisher.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Implementing the SignalR Hub, connection lifecycle, or group management (EPIC-6 owns this).</li><li>Push notifications or browser notifications for activity (future).</li><li>Live updates on parts of the UI other than the Activity feed (board column updates belong to EPIC-6's own consumers).</li><li>Offline support or full catch-up replay beyond page-1 re-fetch on reconnect.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.2, §1.3, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I have the board's Activity feed open in my browser <b>When</b> another member (or I myself in another tab) performs any mutation that produces an activity entry <b>Then</b> the new entry appears at the top of my visible feed within ~1s, without any manual page action, using the real-time channel provided by EPIC-6.</p><p><b>Given</b> multiple activity entries are produced in rapid succession (e.g. bulk card moves) <b>When</b> they arrive via the real-time channel <b>Then</b> each is prepended to the top of the feed in order of occurredAt descending; no duplicates appear; existing entries are not re-fetched from the server.</p><p><b>Given</b> IActivityPublisher.Publish throws (e.g. Hub invocation fails) AFTER the mutation has committed and the activity entry has been written <b>When</b> the request completes <b>Then</b> the API still returns the original success response (e.g. 200 OK or 201 Created); the exception is caught and logged as a structured error (including boardId and activityEntryId); no rollback of the mutation or the activity entry occurs.</p><p><b>Given</b> SignalR reconnects and a page-1 REST re-fetch is in-flight <b>When</b> a live ActivityEntryPushed event arrives for an entry that is also included in the re-fetch response <b>Then</b> the Pinia feed store shows that entry exactly once (deduplication by id before prepending/merging).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer with the Activity feed open <b>When</b> another member makes a change <b>Then</b> the new entry is pushed to my feed exactly as for Owner or Editor (role does not restrict live updates — authorization is already enforced at the Hub connection/group level by EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> my SignalR connection is temporarily dropped and then reconnects <b>When</b> the reconnection succeeds <b>Then</b> the UI re-fetches page 1 of the feed (a full refresh of the visible window) so any missed entries during the outage are recovered; new live updates then continue from the reconnected state.</p><p><b>Given</b> I navigate away from the Activity tab or close the board <b>When</b> my component unmounts <b>Then</b> the SignalR group subscription is released (no memory leak, no phantom updates to unmounted components).</p><p><b>Given</b> I have NOT opened the Activity feed <b>When</b> an activity entry is produced on the board <b>Then</b> the real-time push still delivers the entry to any peer who does have the feed open; there is no side effect on other parts of the UI that have not opted in.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-7.3: Live activity updates" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-7; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As a board member with the Activity feed open, I want new activity entries to appear automatically within about one second of them being recorded, so that I can see the board's live history without refreshing.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Transport: consumes the board-{boardId} SignalR group provided by EPIC-6. This story MUST NOT implement a new Hub, connection manager, or group subscription mechanism — those belong to EPIC-6. STORY-7.3 only adds: (a) the server-side Hub method invocation to push the new ActivityEntryDto on the existing group, and (b) the client-side handler that prepends the DTO to the Pinia feed store.</li><li>Latency target: new entry visible to all connected board members within ~1s of the originating mutation committing (§1.2, §1.6).</li><li>Deduplication: the client must guard against receiving the same ActivityEntryDto twice (e.g. on reconnect + re-fetch race). Deduplicate by id in the Pinia store before prepending.</li><li>No unbounded growth: the Pinia store for live-prepended entries MUST NOT grow without bound. Cap the in-memory list at a configurable maximum (e.g. 200 entries) consistent with the pagination page-size contract; older entries remain available via the paginated REST endpoint.</li><li>Reconnection recovery: on SignalR reconnect, the UI calls the REST endpoint (page 1) to recover missed entries, then resumes live updates. The REST and live paths must produce the same ActivityEntryDto shape.</li><li>Authorization: EPIC-6 enforces group membership at the Hub level; STORY-7.3 relies on that. No additional per-push authorization check is required here.</li><li>Orchestration (Application layer only): the Application command handler calls IActivityWriter WITHIN the unit-of-work (same SaveChanges as the mutation), then — AFTER commit — calls IActivityPublisher.Publish fire-and-forget. Both calls live in the Application layer; there is no extra orchestration layer between them. The Infrastructure IActivityPublisher implementation holds the Hub reference; the Application layer has no knowledge of SignalR types.</li><li>Clean Architecture (§2.2): the server push is triggered from the Application layer (after the mutation commits and the activity entry is written) via an IActivityPublisher interface; the SignalR Hub implementation lives in Infrastructure/Api. No SignalR types in Domain or Application.</li><li>Publisher failure isolation: if IActivityPublisher.Publish throws after commit, the exception MUST be caught and logged (structured log including boardId and activityEntryId) but MUST NOT propagate to the caller. The mutation response and the activity write are already durable; only the real-time push is lost.</li><li>Accessibility: new entries prepended live are announced to screen readers via an aria-live='polite' region on the feed list. The announcement must not be intrusive — polite (not assertive) so it does not interrupt ongoing interactions.</li><li>Performance: Hub invocations are fire-and-forget from the API's perspective; a SignalR delivery failure MUST NOT cause the mutation transaction to roll back or the API request to fail.</li><li>Testing: the real-time path is integration-tested against the actual Hub (using Microsoft.AspNetCore.SignalR.Client in test); unit tests mock IActivityPublisher.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Implementing the SignalR Hub, connection lifecycle, or group management (EPIC-6 owns this).</li><li>Push notifications or browser notifications for activity (future).</li><li>Live updates on parts of the UI other than the Activity feed (board column updates belong to EPIC-6's own consumers).</li><li>Offline support or full catch-up replay beyond page-1 re-fetch on reconnect.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> §1.2, §1.3, §1.5, §1.6, §2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I have the board's Activity feed open in my browser <b>When</b> another member (or I myself in another tab) performs any mutation that produces an activity entry <b>Then</b> the new entry appears at the top of my visible feed within ~1s, without any manual page action, using the real-time channel provided by EPIC-6.</p><p><b>Given</b> multiple activity entries are produced in rapid succession (e.g. bulk card moves) <b>When</b> they arrive via the real-time channel <b>Then</b> each is prepended to the top of the feed in order of occurredAt descending; no duplicates appear; existing entries are not re-fetched from the server.</p><p><b>Given</b> IActivityPublisher.Publish throws (e.g. Hub invocation fails) AFTER the mutation has committed and the activity entry has been written <b>When</b> the request completes <b>Then</b> the API still returns the original success response (e.g. 200 OK or 201 Created); the exception is caught and logged as a structured error (including boardId and activityEntryId); no rollback of the mutation or the activity entry occurs.</p><p><b>Given</b> SignalR reconnects and a page-1 REST re-fetch is in-flight <b>When</b> a live ActivityEntryPushed event arrives for an entry that is also included in the re-fetch response <b>Then</b> the Pinia feed store shows that entry exactly once (deduplication by id before prepending/merging).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a Viewer with the Activity feed open <b>When</b> another member makes a change <b>Then</b> the new entry is pushed to my feed exactly as for Owner or Editor (role does not restrict live updates — authorization is already enforced at the Hub connection/group level by EPIC-6).</p><p><b>Given</b> my SignalR connection is temporarily dropped and then reconnects <b>When</b> the reconnection succeeds <b>Then</b> the UI re-fetches page 1 of the feed (a full refresh of the visible window) so any missed entries during the outage are recovered; new live updates then continue from the reconnected state.</p><p><b>Given</b> I navigate away from the Activity tab or close the board <b>When</b> my component unmounts <b>Then</b> the SignalR group subscription is released (no memory leak, no phantom updates to unmounted components).</p><p><b>Given</b> I have NOT opened the Activity feed <b>When</b> an activity entry is produced on the board <b>Then</b> the real-time push still delivers the entry to any peer who does have the feed open; there is no side effect on other parts of the UI that have not opted in.</p>"
```

### User Story — STORY-8.1: Filter a board's cards by metadata
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-8 → <EPIC-8-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-8; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a board member, I want to filter a board&apos;s cards by one or more metadata attributes (label, assignee, priority, due-date range), so that I can focus on the work most relevant to me without scrolling through all cards.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Pagination: offset-based; page (1-indexed, default 1) + pageSize (default 20, max 100); response envelope { items, page, pageSize, total } &mdash; consistent with the shared convention.</li><li>Performance: response &lt; ~1.5s for a ~200-card board. Required SQL indexes: Composite index on Cards(BoardId, Priority); Composite index on Cards(BoardId, DueDate); Join table CardLabels(CardId, LabelId) &mdash; index on (LabelId, CardId); Join table CardAssignees(CardId, UserId) &mdash; index on (UserId, CardId). All indexes should be evaluated with INCLUDE columns for the projected DTO fields.</li><li>Authorization: board membership verified server-side for every request; boardId in the route is the only scope. Roles Owner/Editor/Viewer may all read.</li><li>Filter semantics: AND across filter types; OR within multi-value params (labelIds, assigneeIds). Semantics must appear in OpenAPI description fields.</li><li>Validation: unknown labelId/assigneeId returns 400, not silent omission. Invalid date format returns 400. Invalid priority enum value returns 400 with a field-level problem detail. page &lt;= 0, pageSize &lt;= 0 or &gt; 100, or non-integer pagination params return 400.</li><li>DTOs only at the API boundary; input validated via FluentValidation or data annotations; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li>Clean Architecture: query handler in Application layer; EF Core LINQ query in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li>No mutations: this endpoint is strictly read-only.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Text / keyword search (STORY-8.2).</li><li>Combining filters with text search in a single request (STORY-8.3).</li><li>Active filter chip display and clear-individual-filter UX (STORY-8.3).</li><li>Sorting the filtered result set (future).</li><li>Cross-board filtering (EPIC-9).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> &sect;1.3, &sect;1.4, &sect;1.6, &sect;2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am a member of a board <b>When</b> I call GET /boards/{boardId}/cards?labelIds=&hellip;&amp;assigneeIds=&hellip;&amp;priority=&hellip;&amp;dueBefore=&hellip;&amp;dueAfter=&hellip; with any combination of valid filter params <b>Then</b> I receive 200 with a paginated envelope { items, page, pageSize, total } containing only cards that match ALL supplied filters (implicit AND); unmatched cards are excluded; the response is scoped to that board only.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a member of a board <b>When</b> I supply multiple values for labelIds or assigneeIds (comma-separated or repeated params) <b>Then</b> cards matching ANY of the supplied values for that attribute are included (OR within attribute, AND across attributes); the semantics are documented in the API response headers or an OpenAPI description.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a priority value that is not one of the defined enum values (None, Low, Medium, High) <b>When</b> I call the filter endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a field-level problem detail identifying the priority parameter; no cards are returned.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a dueBefore or dueAfter date <b>When</b> either is not a valid ISO 8601 date string, or dueAfter is later than dueBefore <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a clear field-level problem detail and no cards are returned.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply an assigneeId or labelId that does not belong to this board <b>When</b> I call the filter endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 (unknown filter value &mdash; not silently ignored); the error identifies the offending parameter.</p><p><b>Given</b> all filter params are valid but no cards match <b>When</b> I call the filter endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 200 with { items: [], page: 1, pageSize: &lt;requested&gt;, total: 0 } &mdash; an empty result is not an error.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board (or the board does not exist) <b>When</b> I call the filter endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807; the board&apos;s existence is not disclosed.</p><p><b>Given</b> I present no token or an expired token <b>When</b> I call the filter endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a page or pageSize param <b>When</b> page &lt;= 0, pageSize &lt;= 0, pageSize &gt; 100, or either value is non-integer <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a field-level problem detail identifying the offending parameter; no cards are returned.</p><p><b>Given</b> a board has ~200 cards <b>When</b> I apply metadata filters <b>Then</b> the API responds in &lt; ~1.5s (p95 on SQL Server with the required indexes in place).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am viewing the board&apos;s filter panel <b>When</b> I apply or change metadata filters <b>Then</b> the card list updates without a full page reload; loading, empty-result, and error states are displayed; the UI meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-8.1: Filter a board's cards by metadata" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-8; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As a board member, I want to filter a board&apos;s cards by one or more metadata attributes (label, assignee, priority, due-date range), so that I can focus on the work most relevant to me without scrolling through all cards.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Pagination: offset-based; page (1-indexed, default 1) + pageSize (default 20, max 100); response envelope { items, page, pageSize, total } &mdash; consistent with the shared convention.</li><li>Performance: response &lt; ~1.5s for a ~200-card board. no cards are returned.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a dueBefore or dueAfter date <b>When</b> either is not a valid ISO 8601 date string, or dueAfter is later than dueBefore <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a clear field-level problem detail and no cards are returned.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply an assigneeId or labelId that does not belong to this board <b>When</b> I call the filter endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 (unknown filter value &mdash; not silently ignored); the error identifies the offending parameter.</p><p><b>Given</b> all filter params are valid but no cards match <b>When</b> I call the filter endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 200 with { items: [], page: 1, pageSize: &lt;requested&gt;, total: 0 } &mdash; an empty result is not an error.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board (or the board does not exist) <b>When</b> I call the filter endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807; the board&apos;s existence is not disclosed.</p><p><b>Given</b> I present no token or an expired token <b>When</b> I call the filter endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a page or pageSize param <b>When</b> page &lt;= 0, pageSize &lt;= 0, pageSize &gt; ### User Story — STORY-8.2: Text-search a board's cards by title and description
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-8 → <EPIC-8-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-8; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a board member, I want to type a keyword and have the board surface cards whose title or description contains that text, so that I can locate a specific card instantly without knowing which list it is in.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Matching strategy: case-insensitive LIKE &apos;%term%&apos; (substring) against Cards.Title and Cards.Description. v1 choice &mdash; simple, zero-migration, sufficient for a ~200-card board. Migration to SQL Server Full-Text Search (FTS) is the documented upgrade path when corpus size or relevance ranking demands it.</li><li>Performance: response &lt; ~1.5s for a ~200-card board. Required index: Index on Cards(BoardId) covering Title and Description columns (or an existing BoardId index with INCLUDE (Title, Description)) &mdash; limits the LIKE scan to only the target board&apos;s rows.</li><li>Pagination: offset-based; page (1-indexed, default 1) + pageSize (default 20, max 100); envelope { items, page, pageSize, total }.</li><li>Validation: q &gt; 200 characters &rarr; 400 RFC 7807. Blank/whitespace q &rarr; treated as absent (not 400). page &lt;= 0, pageSize &lt;= 0 or &gt; 100, or non-integer pagination params &rarr; 400 RFC 7807 field-level problem detail.</li><li>LIKE metacharacter escaping: %, _, and [ in q must be escaped before being passed to the LIKE predicate (EF Core .Contains() handles this automatically). A q containing these characters must never expand to an unintended wildcard match.</li><li>Authorization: board membership verified server-side; result set never leaks cards from other boards. Roles Owner/Editor/Viewer may all search; endpoint is read-only.</li><li>DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li>Clean Architecture: search query handler in Application; EF Core LINQ (.Contains()) in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li>No mutations: strictly read-only.</li><li>Debounce: frontend fires the request no more than once per 300 ms of typing inactivity to avoid excess API calls; in-flight requests for a superseded term are cancelled (AbortController).</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Combining text search with metadata filters in a single request (STORY-8.3).</li><li>Relevance ranking or fuzzy matching (future / FTS upgrade path).</li><li>Searching in comments, activity log, or card attachments.</li><li>Cross-board search (EPIC-9).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> &sect;1.3, &sect;1.4, &sect;1.6, &sect;2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am a member of a board <b>When</b> I call GET /boards/{boardId}/cards?q=&lt;term&gt; with a non-empty query string <b>Then</b> I receive 200 with a paginated envelope { items, page, pageSize, total } containing only cards whose title or description contains the term (case-insensitive, substring/LIKE match); cards are scoped to this board only.</p><p><b>Given</b> the query matches multiple fields on the same card <b>When</b> the card is returned <b>Then</b> it appears exactly once in the result set (no duplicates from multi-field matching).</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply q with leading or trailing whitespace <b>When</b> the query is evaluated <b>Then</b> the whitespace is trimmed server-side and the trimmed term is used; an all-whitespace q is treated as absent (see the blank q criterion below).</p><p><b>Given</b> I omit q or supply a blank/whitespace-only q <b>When</b> I call the search endpoint <b>Then</b> the text-search predicate is not applied and all cards on the board are returned (or the intersection with any other supplied filters if STORY-8.3 is combined); this is not an error.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a q term longer than 200 characters <b>When</b> I call the endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a clear problem detail; no query is executed.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a page or pageSize param <b>When</b> page &lt;= 0, pageSize &lt;= 0, pageSize &gt; 100, or either value is non-integer <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a field-level problem detail identifying the offending parameter; no cards are returned.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a q containing SQL LIKE metacharacters (%, _, [) <b>When</b> the query is evaluated <b>Then</b> those characters are treated as literal text &mdash; they do not function as wildcards; a q of 100% must match only cards whose title or description contains the literal string 100%, not all cards.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board (or the board does not exist) <b>When</b> I call the search endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807; the board&apos;s existence is not disclosed.</p><p><b>Given</b> I present no token or an expired token <b>When</b> I call the search endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> the search term matches no cards <b>When</b> I call the search endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 200 with { items: [], page: 1, pageSize: &lt;requested&gt;, total: 0 }.</p><p><b>Given</b> a board has ~200 cards <b>When</b> I search with a term that hits a significant portion of cards <b>Then</b> the API responds in &lt; ~1.5s (p95 with the required index in place).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am viewing the board <b>When</b> I type into the search input <b>Then</b> the card list filters live (debounced, &gt;= 300 ms) without a full page reload; loading, empty-result, and error states are shown; the UI meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-8.2: Text-search a board's cards by title and description" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-8; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As a board member, I want to type a keyword and have the board surface cards whose title or description contains that text, so that I can locate a specific card instantly without knowing which list it is in.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Matching strategy: case-insensitive LIKE &apos;%term%&apos; (substring) against Cards.Title and Cards.Description. v1 choice &mdash; simple, zero-migration, sufficient for a ~200-card board. Migration to SQL Server Full-Text Search (FTS) is the documented upgrade path when corpus size or relevance ranking demands it.</li><li>Performance: response &lt; ~1.5s for a ~200-card board. Required index: Index on Cards(BoardId) covering Title and Description columns (or an existing BoardId index with INCLUDE (Title, Description)) &mdash; limits the LIKE scan to only the target board&apos;s rows.</li><li>Pagination: offset-based; page (1-indexed, default 1) + pageSize (default 20, max 100); envelope { items, page, pageSize, total }.</li><li>Validation: q &gt; 200 characters &rarr; 400 RFC 7807. Blank/whitespace q &rarr; treated as absent (not 400). page &lt;= 0, pageSize &lt;= 0 or &gt; 100, or non-integer pagination params &rarr; 400 RFC 7807 field-level problem detail.</li><li>LIKE metacharacter escaping: %, _, and [ in q must be escaped before being passed to the LIKE predicate (EF Core .Contains() handles this automatically). A q containing these characters must never expand to an unintended wildcard match.</li><li>Authorization: board membership verified server-side; result set never leaks cards from other boards. Roles Owner/Editor/Viewer may all search; endpoint is read-only.</li><li>DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li>Clean Architecture: search query handler in Application; EF Core LINQ (.Contains()) in Infrastructure; thin controller in Api.</li><li>No mutations: strictly read-only.</li><li>Debounce: frontend fires the request no more than once per 300 ms of typing inactivity to avoid excess API calls; in-flight requests for a superseded term are cancelled (AbortController).</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Combining text search with metadata filters in a single request (STORY-8.3).</li><li>Relevance ranking or fuzzy matching (future / FTS upgrade path).</li><li>Searching in comments, activity log, or card attachments.</li><li>Cross-board search (EPIC-9).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> &sect;1.3, &sect;1.4, &sect;1.6, &sect;2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am a member of a board <b>When</b> I call GET /boards/{boardId}/cards?q=&lt;term&gt; with a non-empty query string <b>Then</b> I receive 200 with a paginated envelope { items, page, pageSize, total } containing only cards whose title or description contains the term (case-insensitive, substring/LIKE match); cards are scoped to this board only.</p><p><b>Given</b> the query matches multiple fields on the same card <b>When</b> the card is returned <b>Then</b> it appears exactly once in the result set (no duplicates from multi-field matching).</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply q with leading or trailing whitespace <b>When</b> the query is evaluated <b>Then</b> the whitespace is trimmed server-side and the trimmed term is used; an all-whitespace q is treated as absent (see the blank q criterion below).</p><p><b>Given</b> I omit q or supply a blank/whitespace-only q <b>When</b> I call the search endpoint <b>Then</b> the text-search predicate is not applied and all cards on the board are returned (or the intersection with any other supplied filters if STORY-8.3 is combined); this is not an error.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a q term longer than 200 characters <b>When</b> I call the endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a clear problem detail; no query is executed.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a page or pageSize param <b>When</b> page &lt;= 0, pageSize &lt;= 0, pageSize &gt; 100, or either value is non-integer <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a field-level problem detail identifying the offending parameter; no cards are returned.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a q containing SQL LIKE metacharacters (%, _, [) <b>When</b> the query is evaluated <b>Then</b> those characters are treated as literal text &mdash; they do not function as wildcards; a q of 100% must match only cards whose title or description contains the literal string 100%, not all cards.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board (or the board does not exist) <b>When</b> I call the search endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807; the board&apos;s existence is not disclosed.</p><p><b>Given</b> I present no token or an expired token <b>When</b> I call the search endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> the search term matches no cards <b>When</b> I call the search endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 200 with { items: [], page: 1, pageSize: &lt;requested&gt;, total: 0 }.</p><p><b>Given</b> a board has ~200 cards <b>When</b> I search with a term that hits a significant portion of cards <b>Then</b> the API responds in &lt; ~1.5s (p95 with the required index in place).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am viewing the board <b>When</b> I type into the search input <b>Then</b> the card list filters live (debounced, &gt;= 300 ms) without a full page reload; loading, empty-result, and error states are shown; the UI meets WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>"
```

**Link to parent**
```
az boards work-item relation add --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --id <this-story-id> --relation-type parent --target-id <EPIC-8-id>
```

### User Story — STORY-8.3: Combine filters and text search, display active filter chips, and clear them
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-8 → <EPIC-8-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-8; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As a board member, I want to apply both text search and metadata filters simultaneously, see which filters are active as dismissible chips, and clear any or all of them with one action, so that I can iteratively narrow my results and always understand what is shaping the card list.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Single endpoint: GET /boards/{boardId}/cards accepts all params from STORY-8.1 and STORY-8.2 in one call; the Application-layer query handler composes predicates dynamically &mdash; each absent param is a no-op. No separate &apos;combined&apos; endpoint.</li><li>Validation: collect all field-level validation errors before returning 400; do not halt on the first failure. Use FluentValidation RuleFor chaining or equivalent to surface all problems in one RFC 7807 errors map. Invalid pagination params (page &lt;= 0, pageSize &lt;= 0 or &gt; 100, non-integer) are included in this collected validation.</li><li>Pagination: offset-based; page (1-indexed, default 1) + pageSize (default 20, max 100); envelope { items, page, pageSize, total }. Pagination resets to page 1 on every filter change (frontend responsibility).</li><li>Performance: &lt; ~1.5s p95 for ~200-card boards. The indexes from STORY-8.1 and STORY-8.2 together cover all predicate combinations. EF Core LINQ composes predicates as a single SQL query; no N+1.</li><li>Authorization: board membership verified server-side; all predicates evaluated within the board&apos;s row set. Read-only; no role distinction among Owner/Editor/Viewer for reading.</li><li>Client state: active filters and search term are held in a Pinia store slice (or a composable) so chip state and filter-panel state remain in sync without prop-drilling. URL query-string sync is optional (future nice-to-have; not an AC here).</li><li>Focus management: after removing a chip via keyboard, focus moves to the next chip if one exists, otherwise to the &apos;Clear all filters&apos; button, otherwise to the search input. Announced via aria-live=&apos;assertive&apos; for chip removal.</li><li>DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path.</li><li>Clean Architecture: the combined query handler in Application composes EF Core predicates; Infrastructure layer executes one SQL query; thin controller in Api.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Cross-board search (EPIC-9).</li><li>Saving, naming, or sharing filter presets (future).</li><li>URL query-string sync / deep-linking to a filtered view (future).</li><li>Sorting or reordering the filtered result set (future).</li><li>Searching comments, activity, or attachments.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> &sect;1.3, &sect;1.4, &sect;1.6, &sect;2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am a member of a board <b>When</b> I call GET /boards/{boardId}/cards with any combination of q, labelIds, assigneeIds, priority, dueBefore, and dueAfter supplied together <b>Then</b> I receive 200 with a paginated envelope { items, page, pageSize, total } containing only cards that satisfy ALL supplied predicates simultaneously (text match AND all metadata filters); omitted params are not applied.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a combination that individually produces results but their intersection is empty <b>When</b> I call the endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 200 with { items: [], page: 1, pageSize: &lt;requested&gt;, total: 0 } &mdash; an empty intersection is not an error.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply any invalid parameter value (bad date, q &gt; 200 chars, unknown labelId/assigneeId) <b>When</b> I call the endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with field-level problem details covering all validation failures in a single response (do not short-circuit on the first error).</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a page or pageSize param <b>When</b> page &lt;= 0, pageSize &lt;= 0, pageSize &gt; 100, or either value is non-integer <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a field-level problem detail identifying the offending parameter; no cards are returned.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am not a member of the board (or the board does not exist) <b>When</b> I call the combined endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 404 RFC 7807; the board&apos;s existence is not disclosed.</p><p><b>Given</b> I present no token or an expired token <b>When</b> I call the endpoint <b>Then</b> I receive 401 RFC 7807.</p><p><b>Given</b> a board has ~200 cards <b>When</b> I apply a combined query (text + two metadata filters) <b>Then</b> the API responds in &lt; ~1.5s (p95), reusing the indexes established in STORY-8.1 and STORY-8.2.</p><p><b>Given</b> I have applied one or more filters or a search term <b>When</b> I view the board <b>Then</b> each active predicate is shown as a labelled chip (e.g. &apos;Label: Bug&apos;, &apos;Assignee: Alice&apos;, &apos;Priority: High&apos;, &apos;Due before: 2026-07-31&apos;, q: &apos;payment&apos;); chips are keyboard-focusable and dismissible individually without navigating away. The priority filter is single-select (at most one priority chip is ever shown); dismissing the priority chip clears the single selected value and the priority query param is omitted from the next request.</p><p><b>Given</b> I click or keyboard-activate the &times; on an individual chip <b>When</b> the chip closes <b>Then</b> that single predicate is removed, the remaining active filters are preserved, and the card list refreshes with the updated (narrower) filter set.</p><p><b>Given</b> one or more filters are active <b>When</b> I click or keyboard-activate &apos;Clear all filters&apos; <b>Then</b> all predicates (text + metadata) are reset to their defaults (absent), the chip row disappears, the card list returns to the full unfiltered board view, and the search input and all filter controls are reset to their empty/default states.</p><p><b>Given</b> I clear all filters <b>When</b> no filters remain active <b>Then</b> the chip row and &apos;Clear all filters&apos; control are hidden (not rendered as an empty row).</p><p><b>Given</b> the board has no cards at all <b>When</b> I open it (no filters active) <b>Then</b> the standard board-level empty state is shown, not the &apos;no filter results&apos; empty state.</p><p><b>Given</b> all filters are valid but produce no cards <b>When</b> the empty-result state is rendered <b>Then</b> it includes a &apos;Clear all filters&apos; affordance so the user can recover without manually undoing each chip.</p><p><b>Given</b> the combined search/filter UI <b>When</b> I interact with it <b>Then</b> all controls and chip interactions meet WCAG 2.2 AA (keyboard nav, focus management after chip removal, screen-reader announcements).</p>
```

**Create**
```

### User Story — STORY-9.1: View my assigned cards across all my boards (paginated, with isolation guarantee)
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-9 → <EPIC-9-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-9; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As an authenticated user, I want to see every card assigned to me across all boards I am a member of, so that I have a single place to review my outstanding work regardless of which board it lives on.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Security / isolation: the query MUST join through the user&apos;s active board membership &mdash; not merely the assignee table alone. Any card on a board the user cannot access must be excluded. This is the primary security invariant of this feature.</li><li>Performance: the assignee &rarr; card &rarr; list &rarr; board join is backed by a database index on (UserId, CardId) in the assignee join table (or equivalent composite) and a covering index on board membership (UserId, BoardId) to meet the &lt;1.5 s response-time NFR (&sect;1.6).</li><li>Pagination: offset-based; page (1-indexed, default 1), pageSize (default 20, max 100); { items, page, pageSize, total } &mdash; consistent with every other list endpoint.</li><li>API: DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path; 401 unauthenticated; 400 invalid query params.</li><li>Clean Architecture (&sect;2.2): GetMyTasksQuery use-case in Application; repository/query in Infrastructure; thin controller action in Api. No EF/Microsoft.* references in Domain.</li><li>Due dates: stored as UTC DateTimeOffset; surfaced as-is in the DTO; overdue rendering is a client concern.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Sorting or filtering the list (STORY-9.2).</li><li>Navigating to the card&apos;s board view (STORY-9.3).</li><li>Mutating the card from this view (EPIC-4).</li><li>Real-time push of new assignments into this view (EPIC-6).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> &sect;1.4, &sect;1.5, &sect;1.6, &sect;2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated and assigned to one or more cards across one or more boards <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks <b>Then</b> I receive a paginated response { items, page, pageSize, total } where each item contains: cardId, cardTitle, cardDueDate (nullable), cardPriority, boardId, boardName, listId, listName; and the result includes exactly the cards assigned to me on boards where I am an active member.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated and have no cards assigned to me <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks <b>Then</b> I receive 200 OK with { items: [], page: 1, pageSize: 20, total: 0 } &mdash; not a 404.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks?page=2&amp;pageSize=10 <b>Then</b> I receive the correct page of results following the shared offset-based pagination envelope; page defaults to 1, pageSize defaults to 20 (max 100); out-of-range page or non-integer/negative pageSize returns RFC 7807 400.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am a member of Board A and am assigned to a card there, AND I am NOT a member of Board B but am assigned to a card there (e.g. a test fixture with a direct DB row) <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks <b>Then</b> the response NEVER contains the card from Board B &mdash; the isolation guarantee holds regardless of the assignment row&apos;s existence.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am removed from a board (EPIC-1 STORY-1.4) that had cards assigned to me <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks after removal <b>Then</b> none of the cards from that board appear in the response &mdash; the membership boundary is enforced at query time, not cached.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am unassigned from a card (EPIC-4 STORY-4.3) <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks after the unassignment <b>Then</b> that card no longer appears in the response.</p><p><b>Given</b> I present no token or an invalid/expired token <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks <b>Then</b> I receive 401 Unauthorized.</p><p><b>Given</b> I open the My Tasks view <b>When</b> results are loading, there are no assignments, or an error occurs <b>Then</b> a loading state, a friendly empty state (&apos;Nothing assigned to you yet&apos;), and an error state are each shown appropriately; all states meet WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>
```

**Create**
```
az boards work-item create --organization https://dev.azure.com/bitbodhi --project taskflow --type "User Story" --title "STORY-9.1: View my assigned cards across all my boards (paginated, with isolation guarantee)" --area "taskflow" --iteration "taskflow" --fields "System.State=New" "System.Tags=EPIC-9; spec-traced" "System.Description=<p>As an authenticated user, I want to see every card assigned to me across all boards I am a member of, so that I have a single place to review my outstanding work regardless of which board it lives on.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Security / isolation: the query MUST join through the user&apos;s active board membership &mdash; not merely the assignee table alone. Any card on a board the user cannot access must be excluded. This is the primary security invariant of this feature.</li><li>Performance: the assignee &rarr; card &rarr; list &rarr; board join is backed by a database index on (UserId, CardId) in the assignee join table (or equivalent composite) and a covering index on board membership (UserId, BoardId) to meet the &lt;1.5 s response-time NFR (&sect;1.6).</li><li>Pagination: offset-based; page (1-indexed, default 1), pageSize (default 20, max 100); { items, page, pageSize, total } &mdash; consistent with every other list endpoint.</li><li>API: DTOs only at the boundary; RFC 7807 on every error path; 401 unauthenticated; 400 invalid query params.</li><li>Clean Architecture (&sect;2.2): GetMyTasksQuery use-case in Application; repository/query in Infrastructure; thin controller action in Api. No EF/Microsoft.* references in Domain.</li><li>Due dates: stored as UTC DateTimeOffset; surfaced as-is in the DTO; overdue rendering is a client concern.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Sorting or filtering the list (STORY-9.2).</li><li>Navigating to the card&apos;s board view (STORY-9.3).</li><li>Mutating the card from this view (EPIC-4).</li><li>Real-time push of new assignments into this view (EPIC-6).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> &sect;1.4, &sect;1.5, &sect;1.6, &sect;2.2</p>" "Microsoft.VSTS.Common.AcceptanceCriteria=<p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated and assigned to one or more cards across one or more boards <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks <b>Then</b> I receive a paginated response { items, page, pageSize, total } where each item contains: cardId, cardTitle, cardDueDate (nullable), cardPriority, boardId, boardName, listId, listName; not a 404.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks?page=2&amp;pageSize=10 <b>Then</b> I receive the correct page of results following the shared offset-based pagination envelope; the isolation guarantee holds regardless of the assignment row&apos;s existence.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am removed from a board (EPIC-1 STORY-1.4) that had cards assigned to me <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks after removal <b>Then</b> none of the cards from that board appear in the response &mdash; the membership boundary is enforced at query time, not cached.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am unassigned from a card (EPIC-4 STORY-4.3) <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks after the unassignment <b>Then</b> that card no longer appears in the response.</p><p><b>Given</b> I present no token or an invalid/expired token <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks <b>Then</b> I receive 401 Unauthorized.</p><p><b>Given</b> I open the My Tasks view <b>When</b> results are loading, there are no assignments, or an error occurs <b>Then</b> a loading state, a friendly empty state (&apos;Nothing assigned to you yet&apos;), and an error state are each shown appropriately; all states meet WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>"
```

### User Story — STORY-9.2: Sort and filter My Tasks for triage
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-9 → <EPIC-9-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-9; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As an authenticated user, I want to sort my assigned cards by due date or priority and filter them by board or priority, so that I can triage my workload and focus on what matters most.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Isolation inherited: sort and filter are applied on top of the membership-gated query from STORY-9.1. Filtering by boardId never bypasses the membership check &mdash; even if the caller supplies a boardId they are not a member of, the result is an empty list (the board&apos;s existence is not disclosed).</li><li>Supported sort keys: dueDate, priority. Default: dueDate asc, nulls last. sortDir: asc | desc.</li><li>Supported filter params: boardId (must be a syntactically valid GUID &mdash; invalid GUID format returns 400 RFC 7807; a valid GUID that is not a board the caller is a member of returns an empty list, not 404); priority (None | Low | Medium | High).</li><li>Combining: sort and filter params are combined additively. Pagination applies after filtering and sorting.</li><li>Performance: the same assignee/membership indexes from STORY-9.1 are sufficient; filter params map to WHERE clause predicates rather than application-side filtering.</li><li>API: query-string params only (no request body on GET); RFC 7807 400 for unrecognised/invalid param values; DTOs unchanged from STORY-9.1.</li><li>Clean Architecture: GetMyTasksQuery extended with optional sort/filter fields; the Application use-case assembles the predicate; Infrastructure translates to EF Core query; no raw SQL unless a query-plan analysis requires it.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Filtering by label within My Tasks (future cross-epic concern).</li><li>Persisting filter/sort preferences across sessions (future).</li><li>Full-text search of card titles from this view (EPIC-8 covers within-board search; cross-board text search is future).</li><li>Saved filter presets.</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> &sect;1.4, &sect;1.5, &sect;1.6, &sect;2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks?sortBy=dueDate&amp;sortDir=asc <b>Then</b> the paginated response is ordered by cardDueDate ascending; cards with no due date appear last.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks?sortBy=dueDate&amp;sortDir=desc <b>Then</b> the response is ordered by cardDueDate descending; cards with no due date appear last.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks?sortBy=priority&amp;sortDir=desc <b>Then</b> the response is ordered by priority descending (High &rarr; Medium &rarr; Low &rarr; None).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks?sortBy=priority&amp;sortDir=asc <b>Then</b> the response is ordered by priority ascending (None &rarr; Low &rarr; Medium &rarr; High).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I supply an unrecognised sortBy value or an invalid sortDir value <b>Then</b> I receive RFC 7807 400 and no results.</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks?boardId={boardId} <b>Then</b> the response contains only cards from that specific board (still within my membership &mdash; a boardId I am not a member of returns an empty list, not a 404 or a leak).</p><p><b>Given</b> I am authenticated <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks?priority=High <b>Then</b> the response contains only cards with cardPriority = High; invalid priority values return RFC 7807 400.</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply a boardId value that is not a valid GUID (e.g. abc, 123, an empty string) <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks?boardId={value} <b>Then</b> I receive 400 RFC 7807 with a field-level problem detail identifying the boardId parameter; no results are returned. (A syntactically valid GUID that is not a board I am a member of still returns 200 with an empty list &mdash; the board&apos;s existence is not disclosed.)</p><p><b>Given</b> I supply both boardId and priority filter params <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks <b>Then</b> both filters are applied together (AND logic); sorting is also applied if provided.</p><p><b>Given</b> I omit sortBy <b>When</b> I GET /me/tasks <b>Then</b> the default ordering is by cardDueDate ascending with nulls last (consistent with STORY-9.1&apos;s default presentation).</p><p><b>Given</b> I open the My Tasks view <b>When</b> I interact with the sort/filter controls <b>Then</b> the view updates to reflect the selected options; loading, empty, and error states each render correctly for the filtered/sorted result; all controls meet WCAG 2.2 AA.</p>
```

**Create**
```

Filtering by boardId never bypasses the membership check &mdash; even if the caller supplies a boardId they are not a member of, the result is an empty list (the board&apos;s existence is not disclosed).</li><li>Supported sort keys: dueDate, priority. ### User Story — STORY-9.3: Navigate from a My Tasks item to the card in its board (deep link)
- **Type:** User Story · **Parent:** EPIC-9 → <EPIC-9-id>
- **Area:** taskflow · **Iteration:** taskflow · **State:** New · **Tags:** EPIC-9; spec-traced

**Description (HTML)**
```html
<p>As an authenticated user, I want to click on a My Tasks item and be taken directly to that card within its board view, so that I can read the card&apos;s full detail and take action without manually finding the right board.</p><p><b>NFR / constraints:</b></p><ul><li>Authorization on arrival: the deep link DOES NOT bypass board authorization. The board view&apos;s existing authorization guard (EPIC-1, EPIC-3) applies on arrival; no new auth surface is introduced.</li><li>URL stability: the route /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId} is a client-side route (Vue Router); the backend API serves the SPA on any sub-path. The cardId is resolved by an existing card-detail endpoint that already enforces board membership.</li><li>No new API endpoint: this story is primarily a frontend routing and UX concern. It reuses existing endpoints: the board-load endpoint (EPIC-3) and the card-detail endpoint (established by earlier epics). The only new code is the Vue Router route definition and the deep-link open-on-mount behavior in the card detail panel component.</li><li>Accessibility (WCAG 2.2 AA): each task row in the My Tasks list is a navigable element (&lt;a&gt; or role=&apos;link&apos;) with an accessible name that includes the card title and board name (e.g. &apos;Review onboarding copy &mdash; Board: Marketing&apos;); screen-reader users can distinguish rows. The card detail panel: keyboard-navigable; focus moves to panel heading on open, returns to triggering row on close; accessible names on all controls (panel close, retry button, etc.); color is not the sole differentiator for any interactive or status state.</li><li>Clean Architecture: no new Application or Infrastructure layer work; this story is constrained to the Api routing layer and the Vue frontend.</li></ul><p><b>Out of scope:</b></p><ul><li>Editing or updating the card from the deep-link panel (EPIC-4 owns card mutation).</li><li>Sharing links with users outside the board &mdash; no public/guest link feature in v1 (&sect;1.3 Out).</li><li>Notification-driven deep links (email/push notifications are out of scope, &sect;1.3 Out).</li><li>Breadcrumb or &apos;back to My Tasks&apos; navigation affordance &mdash; useful but deferred (routing history handles it via the browser back button).</li></ul><p><b>Traces:</b> &sect;1.4, &sect;1.5, &sect;1.6, &sect;2.2</p>
```

**Acceptance Criteria (HTML)**
```html
<p><b>Given</b> I am viewing My Tasks and click on a task row <b>When</b> the navigation begins <b>Then</b> the browser navigates to the board view for that card&apos;s board, with the card detail panel open (URL form: /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId}).</p><p><b>Given</b> I navigate to /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId} directly (e.g. from a copied link) and I am a member of that board <b>When</b> the page loads <b>Then</b> the board view renders and the card detail panel opens automatically; the URL remains stable and is shareable.</p><p><b>Given</b> I navigate to /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId} and I am NOT a member of that board <b>When</b> the page loads <b>Then</b> I am shown an access-denied page (&apos;You don&apos;t have access to this board&apos;) &mdash; the card&apos;s content is never revealed; the board&apos;s existence is not disclosed (same 404-equivalent treatment as all board endpoints for non-members).</p><p><b>Given</b> I navigate to /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId} where cardId does not belong to boardId <b>When</b> the page loads <b>Then</b> the board view renders normally, the card detail panel is not opened, and a dismissible &apos;Card not found&apos; toast/notification is shown to inform the user that the linked card could not be located on this board; the toast does not block board interaction and disappears on dismissal.</p><p><b>Given</b> I navigate to /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId} where boardId does not exist <b>When</b> the page loads <b>Then</b> I see a not-found page (consistent with the board-not-found treatment elsewhere in the app).</p><p><b>Given</b> I share the deep-link URL with another user who IS a member of the board <b>When</b> they navigate to it <b>Then</b> they see the board and card detail panel (their own authorization applies; the link itself carries no elevated privilege).</p><p><b>Given</b> the deep link is followed and the card detail panel is loading <b>When</b> a loading state is in progress <b>Then</b> a loading indicator is shown within the panel; if the card load fails an error state is shown with a retry option.</p><p><b>Given</b> I use keyboard navigation in My Tasks <b>When</b> I focus a task row and press Enter <b>Then</b> navigation to the deep link occurs (equivalent to clicking the row); the task row is keyboard-focusable and has an accessible name.</p><p><b>Given</b> I interact with the deep-link task row, the board view, and the card detail panel <b>When</b> I use a keyboard or assistive technology <b>Then</b> all elements meet WCAG 2.2 AA: the task row and card detail panel are fully keyboard-navigable; all interactive elements have accessible names; focus moves to the panel heading when the panel opens and returns to the triggering element when it closes; color is not the sole visual differentiator for any state (open panel, active row, error state); aria-label or equivalent is present on the panel close button and all icon-only controls.</p>
```

**Create**
```

the URL remains stable and is shareable.</p><p><b>Given</b> I navigate to /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId} and I am NOT a member of that board <b>When</b> the page loads <b>Then</b> I am shown an access-denied page (&apos;You don&apos;t have access to this board&apos;) &mdash; the card&apos;s content is never revealed; the board&apos;s existence is not disclosed (same 404-equivalent treatment as all board endpoints for non-members).</p><p><b>Given</b> I navigate to /boards/{boardId}/cards/{cardId} where cardId does not belong to boardId <b>When</b> the page loads <b>Then</b> the board view renders normally, the card detail panel is not opened, and a dismissible &apos;Card not found&apos;
